------------------------------------------------------------------------

### Xhosa Bible: Jeremiah

<span id="an_1:1">1:1</span> Amazwi kaYeremiya unyana kaHilekiya,
wakubabingeleli baseAnatoti ezweni lakwaBhenjamin:

<span id="an_1:2">1:2</span> ekwafika kuye ilizwi likaYehova ngemihla
kaYosiya unyana ka-Amon, ukumkani wakwaYuda, ngomnyaka weshumi
elinesithathu wobukumkani bakhe;

<span id="an_1:3">1:3</span> nangemihla kaYoyakim unyana kaYosiya,
ukumkani wakwaYuda, kwada kwaba sekupheleni komnyaka weshumi elinamnye
kaZedekiya unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, kwada kwaba
sekufudusweni kweYerusalem ngenyanga yesihlanu.

<span id="an_1:4">1:4</span> Kwafika ke ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_1:5">1:5</span> Ndingekakubumbi esizalweni, bendikwazi;
ungekaphumi embilinini, ndakungcwalisa, ndakumisa waba ngumprofeti
weentlanga.

<span id="an_1:6">1:6</span> Ndathi mna, Kwowu, Nkosi Yehova, yabona,
andikwazi ukuthetha, ngokuba ndingumntwana.

<span id="an_1:7">1:7</span> Wathi uYehova kum, Musa ukuthi,
Ndingumntwana: ke uya kuya kubo bonke endikuthuma kubo; konke
endikuwisela umthetho ngako, uze ukuthethe.

<span id="an_1:8">1:8</span> Uze ungaboyiki, ngokuba ndinawe ukuba
ndikuhlangule; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_1:9">1:9</span> Wasolula uYehova isandla sakhe, wachukumisa
umlomo wam; wathi ke uYehova kum, Yabona, ndibeke amazwi am emlonyeni
wakho.

<span id="an_1:10">1:10</span> Khangela, ndikwenza namhla umveleli
weentlanga nezikumkani, ukuba unyothule, udilize, utshabalalise,
ugungxule; ukuba wakhe, utyale.

<span id="an_1:11">1:11</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum lisithi,
Yintoni na le uyibonayo, Yeremiya? Ndathi, Ndibona intonga yomthi
womamangile.

<span id="an_1:12">1:12</span> Wathi uYehova kum, Ubone walungisa;
ngokuba ndiya kuliphaphela ilizwi lam ukuba ndilenze.

<span id="an_1:13">1:13</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum
ngokwesibini, lisithi, Yintoni na le uyibonayo? Ndathi, Ndibona imbiza
ebaselweyo, ubuso bayo bubheke neno, isentla.

<span id="an_1:14">1:14</span> Wathi ke uYehova kum, Entla kuya kuphuma
ububi, bube phezu kwabemi bonke belizwe.

<span id="an_1:15">1:15</span> Ngokuba, yabona, ndiya kubiza yonke
imizalwane yezikumkani zasentla, utsho uYehova; ziya kuza ke, zimise
iseso itrone yaso ekungeneni kwamasango eYerusalem, nasezindongeni zayo
zonke ngeenxa zonke, nasemizini yonke yakwaYuda.

<span id="an_1:16">1:16</span> Ndiya kuthetha elokubagweba kwam ngenxa
yobubi babo bonke, kuba bendishiyile, baqhumisela thixweni bambi,
baqubuda emisebenzini yezandla zabo.

<span id="an_1:17">1:17</span> Ke wena, bhinqa amanqe akho, usuk’ ume,
uthethe kubo konke endikuwisela umthetho ngako. Musa ukuqhiphuka
umbilini ngabo, hleze mna ndikuqhiphule umbilini ngabo.

<span id="an_1:18">1:18</span> Uyabona ke, mna ndikwenza namhla umzi
onqatyisiweyo, intsika yesinyithi, udonga lobhedu kulo lonke ilizwe,
lokumkani bakwaYuda, nakubathetheli balo, kubabingeleli balo, nakubantu
belizwe.

<span id="an_1:19">1:19</span> Baya kulwa nawe, bangabi nakukweyisa,
ngokuba ndinawe ukuba ndikuhlangule; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_2:1">2:1</span> Kwafika ke ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_2:2">2:2</span> Yiya, umemeze ezindlebeni zeYerusalem,
uthi, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ndikukhumbulele inceba yobutsha bakho,
uthando lobutshakazi bakho, ukundilandela kwakho entlango, ezweni
elingahlwayelwayo.

<span id="an_2:3">2:3</span> Ubengcwele uSirayeli kuYehova, intlahlela
yakhe yongeniselo; bonke abamdlayo bozeka ityala, bofikelwa bububi;
utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_2:4">2:4</span> Liveni ilizwi likaYehova, ndlu kaYakobi,
nonke mizalwane yendlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_2:5">2:5</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Bafumana bubi buni na
kum ooyihlo, le nto bakhwelela kude kum, balandela izinto ezingento,
baba yinto engeyakonto?

<span id="an_2:6">2:6</span> Abatsho ukuthi, Uphi na uYehova
owasinyusayo, wasikhupha ezweni laseYiputa, owasihambisa entlango,
ezweni eliyinkqantosi, lezihogo, ezweni elingumqwebedu, elethunzi
lokufa, ezweni elingacandi mntu, elingahlali mntu?

<span id="an_2:7">2:7</span> Ndaningenisa ezweni elimasimi achumayo,
ukuba nidle iziqhamo zalo, nezinto ezilungileyo zalo; ukanti nakungena
nalenza inqambi ilizwe lam, ilifa lam nalenza langamasikizi.

<span id="an_2:8">2:8</span> Ababingeleli abatshongo ukuthi, Uphi na
uYehova? Abaphathi bomyalelo abandazanga, nabalusi bakreqa kum;
nabaprofeti baprofeta ngoBhahali, balandela abangancedi nto.

<span id="an_2:9">2:9</span> Ngako oko ndisaya kubambana nani, utsho
uYehova, ndibambane noonyana boonyana benu.

<span id="an_2:10">2:10</span> Kuba welani, niye eziqithini zamaKiti,
nibone; nithume nakwaKedare, nigqale kunene, nikhangele ukuba zikhe
zakho na izinto ezinjalo;

<span id="an_2:11">2:11</span> ukuba uhlanga lwakhe lwananisa na
ngoothixo balo, bengethixo ke bona? Ke bona abantu bam banane ngozuko
lwabo into engancediyo.

<span id="an_2:12">2:12</span> Mangaliswani, mazulu, yile nto, nibe
namanwele, niqothole kunene; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_2:13">2:13</span> Ngokuba benze ububi obubini abantu bam:
bandishiyile mna, thende lamanzi aphilileyo; bazimbele amaqula, amaqula
aqhekekileyo, angagcini manzi.

<span id="an_2:14">2:14</span> USirayeli ulikhoboka na? Ulelizalelwe
ekhaya na? Kungathubani na, ukuba abe yinto ephangiweyo?

<span id="an_2:15">2:15</span> Zimbharhulele iingonyama ezintsha,
zalikhupha izwi lazo, zalenza laba senkangala ilizwe lakhe, imizi yakhe
yafakwa isikhuni, ayaba nabemi.

<span id="an_2:16">2:16</span> Kananjalo oonyana baseNofu nabaseTapanesi
badlela elukakayini lwakho.

<span id="an_2:17">2:17</span> Oko asikukwenza kwakho na, ngokushiya
kwakho uYehova uThixo wakho, ngexesha abekuhambisa ngendlela?

<span id="an_2:18">2:18</span> Okanye yintoni na enawe nendlela
yaseYiputa, ukuba usele amanzi oMnayile? Yintoni na enawe nendlela
yaseAsiriya, ukuba usele amanzi oMlambo lowo?

<span id="an_2:19">2:19</span> Buya kukuthethisa ububi bakho, nokuphamba
kwakho kuya kukohlwaya; yazi ke ubone, ukuba kubi, kukrakra, ukumshiya
uYehova uThixo wakho, nokuthi ungankwantyi phambi kwam; itsho iNkosi,
uYehova wemikhosi.

<span id="an_2:20">2:20</span> Ngokuba kususela kwakude, uyaphule
idyokhwe yakho, waziqhawula izitropu zakho; wathi, Andiyi kukukhonza;
kuba ezindulini zonke ezinde, naphantsi kwemithi yonke eluhlaza,
wazolula ngokwehenyukazi.

<span id="an_2:21">2:21</span> Mna ke ndakutyala ungumdiliya wohlobo,
wonke uphela uyimbewu yenyaniso; utheni na ke ukujika, ube ngamasebe
angcakacileyo omdiliya ongeguwo kum?

<span id="an_2:22">2:22</span> Ungafanelana uzihlikihla ngesoda,
wathabatha isepha eninzi: ubugwenxa bakho buhleli budyobhekile phambi
kwam; itsho iNkosi uYehova.

<span id="an_2:23">2:23</span> Ungathini na ukuthi, Andizenzanga
inqambi, andibalandelanga ooBhahali? Yibone indlela yakho emfuleni lowo,
ukwazi okwenzileyo, wena mazi yenkamela enamendu, etshobela ngapha
nangapha;

<span id="an_2:24">2:24</span> mazi ye-esile lasendle, eqhele intlango,
ethi ngokunqwena kwayo isezele umoya; ukungxamela kwayo inkunzi, ngubani
na ongakubuyisayo? Bonke abayifunayo abazidinisi; boyifumana ngenyanga
yayo.

<span id="an_2:25">2:25</span> Luthintele unyawo lwakho lungabi ze,
nomqala wakho unganxanwa. Uthi ke wena, Kuncamekile; hayi, kuba
ndibathandile abasemzini, ndiya kubalandela ke.

<span id="an_2:26">2:26</span> Njengokudana kwesela lakufunyanwa,
kunjalo ukudana kwendlu kaSirayeli: bona ngokwabo, nookumkani babo,
nabathetheli babo, nababingeleli babo, nabaprofeti babo;

<span id="an_2:27">2:27</span> besithi emthini, Ungubawo; nasetyeni,
Undizele; ngokuba bandinikela ikhosi, abandinikela buso ngexesha ke
lobubi babo baya kuthi, Suk’ ume usisindise.

<span id="an_2:28">2:28</span> Baphi na kaloku oothixo bakho ozenzeleyo?
Mabasuke beme, ukuba boba nokukusindisa na ngexesha lobubi bakho; kuba
oothixo bakho babengangenani lemizi yakho, Yuda.

<span id="an_2:29">2:29</span> Yini na ukuba nibambane nam? Nonke
niphela nikreqile kum; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_2:30">2:30</span> Ndifumane ndababetha oonyana benu;
intethiso abayamkelanga; ikrele lenu lidle abaprofeti benu
njengengonyama edlavulayo.

<span id="an_2:31">2:31</span> Sizukulwanandini, likhangeleni ilizwi
likaYehova. Bendiyintlango na kuSirayeli? Bendililizwe lesithokothoko
na? Kungathuba lini na ukuba bathi abantu bam, Siyaphaphatheka, asizi
kuwe?

<span id="an_2:32">2:32</span> Iyazilibala na intombi izivatho zayo,
umtshakazi uyazilibala na iinqwemesha zakhe? Ke bona abantu bam
bandilibele imihla engenakubalwa.

<span id="an_2:33">2:33</span> Uyakwazi ukuyilungisa indlela yakho
ngokufuna uthando; ngako oko iindlela zakho uziqhelisa izinto ezimbi.

<span id="an_2:34">2:34</span> Kwanasemasondweni akho kufumaneka igazi
lemiphefumlo yamahlwempu amsulwa; akuwafumananga egqobhoza zindlu:
bekungenxa yoku konke.

<span id="an_2:35">2:35</span> Ukanti uthi ke, Ndimsulwa, ewe, umsindo
wakhe ubuyile kum. Yabona, ndiya kumangalelana nawe ngenxa yokuba
usithi, Andonanga.

<span id="an_2:36">2:36</span> Yini na ukuba uzulazule kangaka, uyijike
indlela yakho? Uya kudana ngenxa yeYiputa, njengokuba udanile ngenxa
yeAsiriya.

<span id="an_2:37">2:37</span> Nakuyo leyo uya kuphuma, zisentloko
izandla zakho; ngokuba uYehova uya kubacekisa okholose ngabo, ungabi
nampumelelo ngabo.

<span id="an_3:1">3:1</span> Kuthiwa, Ukuba ithe indoda yamgxotha
umkayo, wemka kuyo, waba ngowandoda yimbi, inokumbuyela na? Alingebi
lihlanjelwe na elo lizwe? Wena ke uhenyuzile nezithandane ezininzi;
unokubuyela na ke kum? utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_3:2">3:2</span> Phosa amehlo akho eluqayini ubone; kuphi na
apho ungalalwanga khona? Wabahlalela ngasezindleleni, njengomArabhi
entlango; walihlambela ilizwe ngokuhenyuza kwakho, nangezinto zakho
ezimbi.

<span id="an_3:3">3:3</span> Yathintelwa ke imikhumezelo, ayeza nemvula
evuthisayo; usuke wanebunzi lehenyukazi, akwavuma ukuba neentloni.

<span id="an_3:4">3:4</span> Akuyi kuthi na ngoku undibize, uthi, Bawo,
ulikholwane lobutsha bam?

<span id="an_3:5">3:5</span> Uya kuba nenqala ngonaphakade na, ahlale
ewugcinile na umsindo? Yabona, uthetha njalonje, wenza ububi, ubufezile.

<span id="an_3:6">3:6</span> Wathi uYehova kum ngemihla yokumkani
uYosiya, Ukubonile na elikwenzileyo iphambakazi uSirayeli? Belihamba
phezu kweentaba zonke ezinde, naphantsi kwemithi yonke eluhlaza,
lihenyuza khona.

<span id="an_3:7">3:7</span> Ndathi, emveni kokuba likwenzile oko konke,
Liya kubuyela kum. Lasuka alabuya; lakubona oko ingininginikazi, udade
wabo uYuda.

<span id="an_3:8">3:8</span> Ndabona ukuba, noko iphambakazi uSirayeli
likrexezileyo, ndaligxotha, ndalinika incwadi yokwahlukana nalo, lisuke
noko ingininginikazi uYuda, udade walo aloyika; lasuka ke laya kuhenyuza
nalo.

<span id="an_3:9">3:9</span> Kwathi, ngenxa yesandi sokuhenyuza kwalo,
lahlanjelwa ilizwe, lakrexeza namatye nemithi.

<span id="an_3:10">3:10</span> Nakuko konke oko, alabuyela kum
ingininginikazi, udade walo uYuda, ngentliziyo yonke; kwaba ngokuxoka;
utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_3:11">3:11</span> Wathi uYehova kum, Iphambakazi uSirayeli
lizigwebele ngokwalo, ngaphezu kwengininginikazi uYuda.

<span id="an_3:12">3:12</span> Yiya umemeze la mazwi entla, uthi, Buya,
phambakazi Sirayeli, utsho uYehova; andiyi kubusanganisa ubuso bam kuni,
ngokuba ndinenceba, utsho uYehova; andiyi kuba nanqala ngonaphakade.

<span id="an_3:13">3:13</span> Buvume kodwa ubugwenxa bakho; ngokuba
ukreqile kuYehova uThixo wakho, waziphangalalisa iindlela zakho
kwabasemzini, ngaphantsi kwayo yonke imithi eluhlaza; ke ilizwi lam
analiphulaphula; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_3:14">3:14</span> Buyani, nyana bangamaphamba, utsho
uYehova; ngokuba ndinizekile mna. Ndiya kunithabatha abe mnye emzini,
babe babini kwimizalwane, ndinizise eZiyon;

<span id="an_3:15">3:15</span> ndininike abalusi abangantliziyo yam,
banaluse ngokwazi nangengqiqo.

<span id="an_3:16">3:16</span> Kothi, xa nithe nanda naqhama ezweni
ngaloo mihla, utsho uYehova, bangabi sathi, Ityeya yomnqophiso kaYehova;
ingathi qatha entliziyweni; ingakhunjulwa ngabo, ingafuneki, ingabuye
yenziwe.

<span id="an_3:17">3:17</span> Ngelo xesha iYerusalem kuya kuthiwa
yitrone kaYehova, zixhontelane khona zonke iintlanga ngenxa yegama
likaYehova eliseYerusalem; zingabi salandela ubungqola bentliziyo yazo
embi.

<span id="an_3:18">3:18</span> Ngaloo mihla iya kuhamba indlu yakwaYuda
kunye nendlu yakwaSirayeli, bavele kunye ezweni lasentla, beze ezweni
endabanikayo ooyise laba lilifa.

<span id="an_3:19">3:19</span> Ndathi mna, Azi ndingathini na ukukumisa
phakathi koonyana, ndikunike ilizwe elinqwenelekayo, ilifa eliligugu
lawo amagugu eentlanga? Ndathi, Niya kundibiza ngokuthi, Bawo; ningabuyi
ekundilandeleni.

<span id="an_3:20">3:20</span> Inyaniso, njengoko umfazi atshinizayo
kuwabo, nitshinizile ngokunjalo kum, nina ndlu kaSirayeli; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_3:21">3:21</span> Livakele izwi eluqayini, isililo
sokutarhuzisa soonyana bakaSirayeli; ngokuba bebezigwenxile iindlela
zabo, bamlibala uYehova uThixo wabo.

<span id="an_3:22">3:22</span> Buyani, nyana bangamaphamba; ndokuphilisa
ukuphamba kwenu. Uyabona, siza kuwe; ngokuba wena, Yehova, unguThixo
wethu.

<span id="an_3:23">3:23</span> Inyaniso, yaba bubuxoki ingxokozelo
yasezindulini, yasezintabeni; inyaniso, lukuYehova uThixo wethu usindiso
lukaSirayeli.

<span id="an_3:24">3:24</span> Isikizi liyidlile indyebo yoobawo
kwasebuncinaneni bethu: impahla yabo emfutshane neenkomo zabo, oonyana
babo neentombi zabo.

<span id="an_3:25">3:25</span> Masilale esikizini lethu, lisigubungele
ihlazo lethu; ngokuba kuYehova uThixo wethu sonile, thina noobawo,
kwasebuncinaneni bethu, unanamhla; asaliphulaphula ilizwi likaYehova
uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_4:1">4:1</span> Ukuba uthe wabuya, Sirayeli, utsho uYehova,
wabuyela kum; wawasusa amazothe akho phambi kwam, akwaphalaphala;

<span id="an_4:2">4:2</span> wafunga wathi, Ehleli nje uYehova,
ngokwenyaniso, ngokusesikweni, nangobulungisa; zozisikelela ngaye
iintlanga, ziqhayise ngaye.

<span id="an_4:3">4:3</span> Ngokuba uthi uYehova kumadoda akwaYuda
nakwiYerusalem, Zikhubeleleni intsinde, ningahlwayeli emithaneni
enameva.

<span id="an_4:4">4:4</span> Zaluseleni kuYehova, nisuse ukungaluki
kwentliziyo yenu, madoda akwaYuda, bemi baseYerusalem; hleze buphume
ubushushu bam njengomlilo, buvuthe kungabikho ucimayo, ngenxa yobubi
beentlondi zenu.

<span id="an_4:5">4:5</span> Xelani kwaYuda, nivakalise eYerusalem,
nithi, Vuthelani isigodlo elizweni; dandulukani, nithi, Hlanganisanani,
singene emizini enqatyisiweyo.

<span id="an_4:6">4:6</span> Phakamisani ibhanile ngaseZiyon, sabani,
ningemi; kuba entla ndizisa ububi, nembubhiso enkulu.

<span id="an_4:7">4:7</span> Kunyuka ingonyama iphuma entshinyeleni yayo
yehlathi, kunduluka umonakalisi weentlanga; uphuma endaweni yakhe, ukuze
aliphanzise ilizwe lakho, imizi yakho yenziwe imiwewe, ingabi nabemi.

<span id="an_4:8">4:8</span> Ngenxa yoko bhinqani ezirhwexayo,
nimbambazele, nibhomboloze; ngokuba ukuvutha komsindo kaYehova
akubuyanga kuthi.

<span id="an_4:9">4:9</span> Kothi ke ngaloo mini, utsho uYehova, iphele
intliziyo yokumkani nentliziyo yabathetheli; bamangaliswe ababingeleli,
bangakhulumi abaprofeti.

<span id="an_4:10">4:10</span> Ndathi ke, Kwowu, Nkosi Yehova, inyaniso,
ubalukuhlile kakhulu aba bantu neYerusalem, usithi, Niya kuba noxolo;
libe ikrele lide lafika emphefumlweni.

<span id="an_4:11">4:11</span> Ngelo xesha kuya kuthiwa kwaba bantu
nakwiYerusalem, Umoya olulophu lwaseluqayini entlango uza ngendlela
yentombi yabantu bam, ungazeli kwela, ungazeli kucoca;

<span id="an_4:12">4:12</span> umoya onamandla ngaphezu kwezo nto uzela
mna; ngoku nam ndiya kuthetha nabo imigwebo.

<span id="an_4:13">4:13</span> Yabona, unyuka njengamafu,
zinjengesaqhwithi iinqwelo zokulwa zawo; anamendu kunamaxhalanga
amahashe awo. Yeha ke thina, ngokuba sibhuqiwe!

<span id="an_4:14">4:14</span> Yihlambulule ububi intliziyo yakho,
Yerusalem, ukuze usindiswe. Kunini na zilalisile phakathi kwakho
iingcinga zakho zobutshinga?

<span id="an_4:15">4:15</span> Ngokuba ilizwi lixelile, liphuma kwaDan,
livakalisa ububi ezintabeni zakwaEfrayim:

<span id="an_4:16">4:16</span> khankanyani ezintlangeni; yabonani,
vakalisani eYerusalem, nithi, Abangqingi beza bevela ezweni elikude,
belikhuphela ilizwi labo phezu kwemizi yakwaYuda.

<span id="an_4:17">4:17</span> Njengabalindi bamasimi bayichasa ngeenxa
zonke; ngokuba ibineenkani kum, utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_4:18">4:18</span> Iindlela zakho neentlondi zakho
zakwenzela oko. Zizinto zakho ezimbi ezo, inene zikrakra, inene zifike
entliziyweni yakho.

<span id="an_4:19">4:19</span> Izibilini zam, izibilini zam!
Ndiyazibhijabhija iingontsi zentliziyo yam! Iyaxokozela intliziyo yam,
andinakuthi tu! Kuba usivile isandi sesigodlo, mphefumlo wam, ukuhlatywa
komkhosi wemfazwe.

<span id="an_4:20">4:20</span> Kumenyezwa intshabalalo kantshabalalo,
ngokuba libhuqiwe lonke ilizwe; zibhuqiwe ngesiquphe iintente zam;
ngephanyazo, amalengalenga am.

<span id="an_4:21">4:21</span> Kunini na ndibona ibhanile, ndisiva
isandi sesigodlo?

<span id="an_4:22">4:22</span> Kuba bamathile abantu bam, mna abandazi;
ngoonyana abazizidenge, abanangqondo bona; banobulumko bokwenza ububi,
ukulungisa abakwazi.

<span id="an_4:23">4:23</span> Ndakhangela emhlabeni, nanko
kusenyanyeni, lilubala; nasezulwini, akwabakho kukhanya kulo.

<span id="an_4:24">4:24</span> Ndakhangela ezintabeni, nanzo zinyikima,
neenduli zonke zididizela.

<span id="an_4:25">4:25</span> Ndakhangela, nanko ke kungekho mntu,
neentaka zonke zezulu zibalekile.

<span id="an_4:26">4:26</span> Ndakhangela, nantso iKarmele iyintlango,
yonke imizi yayo idilikile phambi koYehova, phambi kokuvutha komsindo
wakhe.

<span id="an_4:27">4:27</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Kuya kuba
senkangala kulo lonke ilizwe; kodwa ndingaligqibeli kuphele.

<span id="an_4:28">4:28</span> Ngenxa yoko ihlabathi liya kuba
nesijwili, libe nezimnyama zokuzila izulu ngaphezulu; ngenxa enokuba
ndithethile, ndinkqangiyele, andisayi kuzohlwaya, andiyi kubuya umva
kuloo nto.

<span id="an_4:29">4:29</span> Ngesandi sabamahashe nabezaphetha,
iyabaleka yonke imizi; bangena ezintshinyeleni zehlathi, benyuka
emixawukeni; yonke imizi ishiyiwe, akuhlali mntu kuyo.

<span id="an_4:30">4:30</span> Ke wena ubhuqiweyo, uyakuthini na? Nokuba
uthe wambatha ezibomvu, nokuba uthe wavatha izivatho zegolide, nokuba
uthe wawazoba amehlo akho ngestibhiya, ufumane wahomba: ziya kukucekisa
izithandane, zifuna umphefumlo wakho,

<span id="an_4:31">4:31</span> Ngokuba ndive ilizwi elinjengelomfazi
onenimba, imbandezelo enjengeyozibulayo, izwi lentombi enguZiyon;
inesingqala, izolula izandla zayo, isithi, Athi ke mna! ngokuba
umphefumlo wam utyhafile ngababulali.

<span id="an_5:1">5:1</span> Zityhutyheni izitrato zaseYerusalem;
khanikhangele, nazi, nifune ezindaweni zayo zembutho, ukuba nomfumana na
umntu, ukuba ukho na umntu owenza ngokusesikweni, ofuna ukunyanisa:
ndoyixolela.

<span id="an_5:2">5:2</span> Nokuba bathi, Ehleli nje uYehova, boba
bafunga bexoka.

<span id="an_5:3">5:3</span> Yehova, amehlo akho akajonge ekunyaniseni,
yini na? Uyababetha, abevi ntlungu; uyabagqibela kuphele, abavumi
ukuthethiswa; babenza ngwanyalala ubuso babo ngaphezu kwengxondorha,
abavumi ukubuya.

<span id="an_5:4">5:4</span> Ndathi mna, Zizisweli zodwa zona,
zimathile; ngokuba abayazi indlela kaYehova, nesiko loThixo wabo.

<span id="an_5:5">5:5</span> Ndokha ndiye kwabakhulu, ndithethe nabo;
ngokuba bayayazi bona indlela kaYehova, isiko loThixo wabo; ke bona
bayaphule kunye idyokhwe, baziqhawula izitropu.

<span id="an_5:6">5:6</span> Ngenxa yoko iyababulala ingonyama
yasehlathini, iyabadlavula ingcuka yasezinkqantosini, ingwe ilalela
imizi yabo; bonke abo baphuma kuyo bayaqwengwa; ngokuba luninzi ukreqo
lwabo, kuninzi ukuphamba kwabo.

<span id="an_5:7">5:7</span> Ndothini na ukukuxolela? Oonyana bakho
bandishiyile, bafunga abangethixo; ndabafungisa, ke bakrexeza, bathi
ngunga endlwini yamahenyukazi.

<span id="an_5:8">5:8</span> Bayazibela njengeenkunzi zamahashe
ezityetyisiweyo, elowo ukhonyela umfazi wommelwane wakhe.

<span id="an_5:9">5:9</span> Mandingaveleli na ke ngenxa yezo zinto?
utsho uYehova; ungaphindezeli na ke umphefumlo wam, kuhlanga olunje?

<span id="an_5:10">5:10</span> Nyukani ezindongeni zayo, nonakalise;
kodwa ningagqibeli kuphele; susani amasebe ayo, ngokuba engengakaYehova.

<span id="an_5:11">5:11</span> Ngokuba itshinizile kakhulu kum indlu
kaSirayeli nendlu kaYuda, utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_5:12">5:12</span> Bayamkhanyela uYehova; bathi, Asinguye,
abuyi kusifikela ububi, asiyi kubona krele nandlala;

<span id="an_5:13">5:13</span> abaprofeti baya kuba ngumoya; othethayo
akakho kubo; makwenjiwe njalo kubo.

<span id="an_5:14">5:14</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova, uThixo
wemikhosi, ukuthi, Ngenxa enokuba nilithetha elo lizwi, yabona, ndiwenza
umlilo amazwi am emlonyeni wakho, naba bantu babe ziinkuni, ubadle.

<span id="an_5:15">5:15</span> Yabona, ndifikisa phezu kwenu, ndlu
kaSirayeli, uhlanga lwakude, utsho uYehova; luhlanga oluqinileyo,
luhlanga oludala, luhlanga oluntetho ungayaziyo, ongayivayo into
oluyithethayo.

<span id="an_5:16">5:16</span> Umphongolo walo unjengengcwaba
elivulekileyo; bonke bephela bangamagorha.

<span id="an_5:17">5:17</span> Luya kukudla ukuvuna kwakho nesonka
sakho; luya kubadla oonyana bakho neentombi zakho; luya kuyidla impahla
yakho emfutshane neenkomo zakho; luya kuwudla umdiliya wakho nomkhiwane
wakho; luya kuyiviva ngekrele imizi yakho enqatyisiweyo, okholose ngayo.

<span id="an_5:18">5:18</span> Noko ke ngaloo mihla, utsho uYehova,
andiyi kunigqibela kuphele.

<span id="an_5:19">5:19</span> Kuthi, xa nithi, UYehova uThixo wethu
uzenzeleni na ezo zinto zonke kuthi? uze uthi kubo, Njengokuba
nindishiyile mna, nakhonza oothixo bolunye uhlanga ezweni lenu,
kwangokunjalo niya kukhonza abasemzini ezweni elingelenu.

<span id="an_5:20">5:20</span> Kuxeleni oku endlwini kaYakobi,
nikuvakalise kwaYuda, nithi,

<span id="an_5:21">5:21</span> Khanive oku, bantu bazizidenge,
bangenantliziyo; banamehlo, bengaboni; baneendlebe, bengeva.

<span id="an_5:22">5:22</span> Mna anindoyiki na? utsho uYehova;
anizibhijabhiji na ebusweni bam, mna ndiyibekileyo intlabathi yangumda
wolwandle, yangummiselo ongunaphakade olungawugqithiyo? Ayalatyuza amaza
alo, angabi nakwenza nto; agqume, angawugqithi.

<span id="an_5:23">5:23</span> Ke aba bantu banentliziyo eyinjubaqa,
eneenkani; bakreqile bemka.

<span id="an_5:24">5:24</span> Abatsho nokuthi ezintliziyweni zabo,
Makhe soyike uYehova uThixo wethu, osinika imvula ethambisayo
nevuthisayo ngexesha elililo; osigcinela iiveki ezimisiweyo zasekwindla.

<span id="an_5:25">5:25</span> Izenzo zenu ezigwenxa zizisunduzile ezo
zinto, izono zenu zikuthintele kuni okulungileyo.

<span id="an_5:26">5:26</span> Ngokuba kufunyanwa abangendawo phakathi
kwabantu bam; bayalalela ngokuncathama kwabathiyeli, benza isihogo,
babambisa abantu.

<span id="an_5:27">5:27</span> Njengendlwane izele ziintaka, zinjalo
izindlu zabo ukuzala yinkohliso; ngenxa yoko bakhulile baba zizityebi.

<span id="an_5:28">5:28</span> Batyebile, bagudile; kananjalo
bagqithisele ngezinto ezimbi; ityala abalilungisa, ityala leenkedama,
ukuze zibe nempumelelo; abaligwebi ityala lamahlwempu.

<span id="an_5:29">5:29</span> Ndingaveleli na ke ngenxa yezo nto? utsho
uYehova; ungaphindezeli na umphefumlo wam kuhlanga olunje?

<span id="an_5:30">5:30</span> Kwenziwa into emangalisayo, ebanga
amanwele ezweni:

<span id="an_5:31">5:31</span> abaprofeti baprofeta ngobuxoki,
nababingeleli banobukhosi ngezandla zabo; abantu bam ke bathanda ukuba
kube njalo. Niya kuthini na ke ekupheleni kwako oko?

<span id="an_6:1">6:1</span> Sabani, nyana bakaBhenjamin, niphume
phakathi kweYerusalem, naseTekowa, nivuthele isigodlo, niphakamise into
iphakame phezu kweBhete-hakerem; ngokuba ububi buyalunguza, buvela
entla, nembubhiso enkulu.

<span id="an_6:2">6:2</span> Umntwana omhle, umteketiswa, intombi
enguZiyon, ndiyayitshabalalisa.

<span id="an_6:3">6:3</span> Beza kuyo abalusi nemihlambi yabo,
bagxumeka kuyo iintente zabo ngeenxa zonke; badla elowo endaweni yakhe.

<span id="an_6:4">6:4</span> Yingcwaliseleni imfazwe; sukani nime,
sinyuke emini enkulu. Athi ke thina! Imini iza kusangana, ngokuba
amathunzi okuhlwa ayoluka.

<span id="an_6:5">6:5</span> Sukani nime, sinyuke ebusuku,
sizitshabalalise iingxande zayo ezinde.

<span id="an_6:6">6:6</span> Ngokuba utshilo uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi,
Yigawuleni imithi yayo, niyifumbele iYerusalem udonga lokungqinga; wona
mzi wokuvelelwa, wonke uphela, unocudiso phakathi kwawo.

<span id="an_6:7">6:7</span> Njengoko iqula liwampompozisayo amanzi alo,
yenjenjalo ukumpompozisa izinto zayo ezimbi. Ukugonyamela nokubhuqa
kuvakala kuyo; kuhleli kukho phambi kobuso bam isifo nesibetho.

<span id="an_6:8">6:8</span> Yaleka, Yerusalem, hleze umphefumlo wam
uziqhawule kuwe; hleze ndikwenze kube senkangala kuwe, ube lilizwe
elingamiweyo.

<span id="an_6:9">6:9</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi, Baya
kuwabhikica bawabhikice amasalela amaSirayeli, njengomdiliya; sibuyisele
isandla sakho emagatyeni, njengomvuni weediliya.

<span id="an_6:10">6:10</span> Ndiya kuthetha koobani na,
ndiqononondise, beve? Yabona, ayaluswanga indlebe yabo, abanako ke
ukubaza indlebe. Yabona, ilizwi likaYehova libe liyingcikivo kubo,
abalinanzile.

<span id="an_6:11">6:11</span> Ndizele bubushushu bukaYehova; ndidiniwe
kubububamba. Buphalazele phezu komntwana esitratweni, naphezu kwembutho
yamadodana kunye; ngokuba indoda kwanomfazi baya kubanjwa, amadoda
amakhulu kwanabazele yimihla.

<span id="an_6:12">6:12</span> Ziya kugqithela kubambi izindlu zabo,
amasimi nabafazi kunye; ngokuba isandla sam ndisolula phezu kwabemi
belizwe; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_6:13">6:13</span> Kuthabathela kwabancinane kwesa
kwabakhulu, bonke bephela babawa bebawile; kuthabathela kumprofeti kwesa
kumbingeleli, bonke bephela benza ngobuxoki.

<span id="an_6:14">6:14</span> Bakuphilisa kalula ukwaphuka kwentombi
yabantu bam, besithi, Luxolo, luxolo; kungekho luxolo.

<span id="an_6:15">6:15</span> Baya kudaniswa, ngokuba benze amasikizi;
noko ke abadani nokudana, abakwazi ukuba neentloni; ngako oko baya kuwa
phakathi kwabawayo; ngexesha lokubavelela kwam baya kukhubeka; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_6:16">6:16</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yimani ezindleleni,
nikhangele, nibuze umendo ongunaphakade, ukuba yiyiphi na indlela
yokulungileyo, nihambe ngayo; noyifumanela ukuphumla imiphefumlo yenu;
bathi ke bona, Asiyi kuhamba ngayo.

<span id="an_6:17">6:17</span> Ndamisa phezu kwenu ababoniseli,
ndisithi, Libazeleni indlebe ilizwi lesigodlo; bathi ke bona, Asiyi
kulibazela ndlebe.

<span id="an_6:18">6:18</span> Ngako oko yivani, zintlanga; wazi, wena
bandla, okubahlelayo.

<span id="an_6:19">6:19</span> Yiva, hlabathi; yabona, aba bantu
ndibazisela ububi, isiqhamo seengcinga zabo; ngokuba amazwi am
abawabazelanga ndlebe, nomyalelo wam bawucekisile.

<span id="an_6:20">6:20</span> Yeyani na ke le ntlaka imhlophe
yakwaShebha iza kum, nekalamo evumba limnandi yasezweni elikude? Amadini
enu anyukayo akakholekile kum, nemibingelelo yenu ayimnandi kum.

<span id="an_6:21">6:21</span> Ngako oko utshilo uYehova ukuthi, Yabona,
ndibabekela izikhubekiso aba bantu, bakhubeke kuzo ooyise noonyana,
ummelwane kunye nowabo, batshabalale.

<span id="an_6:22">6:22</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabona, kuza abantu
bevela ezweni lasentla, uhlanga olukhulu, luxhoxhwa, luvele esinqeni
somhlaba.

<span id="an_6:23">6:23</span> Baqubule isaphetha nenkcula; bazizijorha,
abanamfesane; ilizwi labo ligquma njengolwandle; bakhwela emahasheni,
bexhobe njengendoda yokulwa, ukukufikela wena, ntombi enguZiyon.

<span id="an_6:24">6:24</span> Siluvile udaba lwaloo nto; ziwile izandla
zethu; imbandezelo isibambile, ukuzibhijabhija njengozalayo.

<span id="an_6:25">6:25</span> Musani ukuya emasimini, ningahambi
ngendlela: ngokuba utshaba lunekrele, kunxunguphala ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_6:26">6:26</span> Ntombi yabantu bam, bhinqa ezirhwexayo,
uzigalele ngothuthu; menzele isijwili ozelwe wamnye, ukumbambazela
okukrakra; ngokuba uya kusizela ngesiquphe umbhuqi.

<span id="an_6:27">6:27</span> Ndikwenze umcikidi phakathi kwabantu bam
njengenqaba, ukuze uyazi uyicikide indlela yabo.

<span id="an_6:28">6:28</span> Bonke bephela baziinjubaqa zazo
iinjubaqa, behamba behleba; balubhedu nesinyithi, bonke bephela
bayonakalisa.

<span id="an_6:29">6:29</span> Itshe ngumlilo imfutho, isekupheleni
ilothe; bafumana benyibilikisa banyibilikise; abenzi bobubi abahlengeki.

<span id="an_6:30">6:30</span> Bayisilivere ecekisiweyo, ukubizwa kwabo,
ngokuba uYehova ebacekisile.

<span id="an_7:1">7:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya lalisithi,

<span id="an_7:2">7:2</span> Yima esangweni lendlu kaYehova, umemeze
khona eli lizwi, uthi, Liveni ilizwi likaYehova, nonke maYuda angenayo
ngala masango, ukuba nimnqule uYehova.

<span id="an_7:3">7:3</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli,
ukuthi, Zilungiseni iindlela zenu nezenzo zenu, ukuze ndinibeke kule
ndawo.

<span id="an_7:4">7:4</span> Musani ukukholosa ngamazwi obuxoki, okuthi,
Yitempile kaYehova, yitempile kaYehova, yitempile kaYehova yona leyo.

<span id="an_7:5">7:5</span> Okanye ukuba nithe nazilungisa nizilungisa
iindlela zenu nezenzo zenu; ukuba nithe nakwenza nikwenza okusesikweni
phakathi komntu nommelwane wakhe;

<span id="an_7:6">7:6</span> anamcudisa owasemzini, nenkedama,
nomhlolokazi, analiphalaza igazi elimsulwa kule ndawo, analandela thixo
bambi, ukuba kube kubi kuni;

<span id="an_7:7">7:7</span> ndonibeka kule ndawo, ezweni endalinika
ooyihlo, kwasephakadeni kuse ephakadeni.

<span id="an_7:8">7:8</span> Yabonani, nikholosa ngamazwi obuxoki
angancediyo.

<span id="an_7:9">7:9</span> Yini? Niyeba, nincinithe, nikrexeze,
nifunge ngobuxoki, niqhumisele kuBhahali, nilandele thixo bambi
eningabaziyo;

<span id="an_7:10">7:10</span> nize ke nime phambi kwam kule ndlu,
ibizwa ngegama lam, nithi, Sihlangulwe; ukuze nenze la masikizi onke?

<span id="an_7:11">7:11</span> Yaba ngumqolomba wezihange na emehlweni
enu le ndlu ibizwa ngegama lam? Yabonani, mna lo ndibonile; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_7:12">7:12</span> Ngokuba khaniye endaweni yam ebiseShilo,
apho ndalibeka khona igama lam ekuqaleni, nibone endakwenzayo kuyo,
ngenxa yezinto ezimbi zabantu bam amaSirayeli.

<span id="an_7:13">7:13</span> Kaloku ke, ngokokuba nizenzile ezi zenzo
zonke, utsho uYehova, ndathetha kuni, ndithetha kwakusa ningeva,
ndinibiza ningasabeli:

<span id="an_7:14">7:14</span> ndokwenza kule ndlu, ibizwa ngegama lam,
nikholosa ngayo, nakule ndawo ndaninika yona nina nooyihlo, njengoko
ndakwenzayo kwiShilo.

<span id="an_7:15">7:15</span> Ndiya kunigxotha nisuke ebusweni bam,
njengoko ndabagxothayo abazalwana benu bonke, imbewu yonke yakwaEfrayim.

<span id="an_7:16">7:16</span> Wena ke, musa ukubathandazela aba bantu,
ungaphimiseli kuhlahlamba nakuthandaza ngenxa yabo, ungandizami, ngokuba
andiyi kukuphulaphula.

<span id="an_7:17">7:17</span> Akuboni na abakwenzayo emizini yakwaYuda,
nasezitratweni zaseYerusalem?

<span id="an_7:18">7:18</span> Oonyana batheza iinkuni, ooyise baphemba
umlilo, abafazi baxovula intlama, ukuba enzelwe izonkana ukumkanikazi
wezulu; bathululele thixo bambi umnikelo othululwayo, ukuze
bandiqumbise.

<span id="an_7:19">7:19</span> Baqumbisa mna na, utsho uYehova;
abaziqumbisi bona na, ukuze budane ubuso babo?

<span id="an_7:20">7:20</span> Ngako oko, itsho iNkosi uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, umsindo wam nobushushu bam buya kuphalazelwa phezu kwale ndawo,
phezu kwabantu, naphezu kweenkomo, naphezu kwemithi yasendle, naphezu
kweziqhamo zomhlaba, buvuthe bungacimi.

<span id="an_7:21">7:21</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yongezani amadini enu anyukayo emibingelelweni yenu,
nidle inyama.

<span id="an_7:22">7:22</span> Ngokuba andithethanga nooyihlo,
andibawiselanga methetho ngeendawo zamadini anyukayo nemibingelelo, mini
ndabakhuphayo ezweni lamaYiputa;

<span id="an_7:23">7:23</span> ke ndabamisela eli lizwi lokuthi,
Phulaphulani ilizwi lam: ndoba nguThixo wenu, nibe ngabantu bam, nihambe
ngendlela yonke endinimiselayo, ukuze kulunge kuni.

<span id="an_7:24">7:24</span> Ke abaphulaphulanga, abayithobanga
indlebe yabo; bahamba ngamaqhinga, ngobungqola bentliziyo yabo embi,
bandinikela umhlana, ayaba bubuso.

<span id="an_7:25">7:25</span> Kususela kwalaa mini baphuma ngayo
ooyihlo ezweni lamaYiputa unanamhla, ndabathumela kuni bonke abakhonzi
bam, abaprofeti, ndibathuma imihla ngemihla kwakusasa;

<span id="an_7:26">7:26</span> ke abaphulaphula kum, abayithoba indlebe
yabo; bayenza lukhuni intamo yabo, benza okubi kunooyise.

<span id="an_7:27">7:27</span> Ke uya kuwathetha kubo la mazwi onke,
abayi kukuphulaphula; umemeza kubo, abayi kusabela.

<span id="an_7:28">7:28</span> Ke yithi kubo, Lulo olu uhlanga
olungaliphulaphuliyo ilizwi likaYehova uThixo walo, olungayivumiyo
intethiso. Kuphelile ukuthembeka, kunqumkile emlonyeni wabo.

<span id="an_7:29">7:29</span> Nqumla isithsaba sakho, Yerusalem,
usilahle, umise isimbonono eluqayini; ngokuba uYehova usicekisile,
usincamile isizukulwana sokuphuphuma kwakhe umsindo.

<span id="an_7:30">7:30</span> Ngokuba oonyana bakaYuda benze into embi
emehlweni am, utsho uYehova; babeke izinto zabo ezinezothe endlwini
elibizelwa phezu kwayo igama lam, ukuze bayenze inqambi.

<span id="an_7:31">7:31</span> Bakhe iziganga zaseTofete, ezisemfuleni
wakwaBhen-hinom, ukuze batshise oonyana babo neentombi zabo ngomlilo;
into endingabawiselanga mthetho ngayo, engathanga qatha entliziyweni
yam.

<span id="an_7:32">7:32</span> Ngako oko, yabona, iyeza imihla, utsho
uYehova, abangasayi kuba sathi yiTofete, ngumfula wakwaBhen-hinom; baya
kuthi nguMfula wokuBulala, bangcwabele eTofete ngenxa enokuba kungekho
ndawo.

<span id="an_7:33">7:33</span> Izidumbu zaba bantu ziya kuba kukudla
kweentaka zasendle nokwezilo zelizwe, kungabikho bani uziphekuzayo.

<span id="an_7:34">7:34</span> Ndiya kuliphezisa emizini yakwaYuda
nasezitratweni zaseYerusalem izwi lemihlali nezwi lemivuyo, izwi lomyeni
nezwi lomtshakazi; ngokuba liya kubharha ilizwe.

<span id="an_8:1">8:1</span> Ngelo xesha, utsho uYehova, aya kukhutshwa
emangcwabeni abo amathambo ookumkani bakwaYuda, namathambo abathetheli
bakhe, namathambo ababingeleli, namathambo abaprofeti, namathambo abemi
baseYerusalem;

<span id="an_8:2">8:2</span> anekwe elangeni, nasenyangeni, nasemkhosini
wonke wezulu, izinto ezo ababezithanda, ababezikhonza, ababezilandela,
ababequqela kuzo, ababequbuda kuzo; akayi kuhlanganiswa, akayi
kungcwatywa, aya kuba ngumgquba phezu kobuso bomhlaba.

<span id="an_8:3">8:3</span> Konyulwa ukufa phezu kobomi ngamasalela
onke aseleyo kule mizalwane ineento ezimbi, ezindaweni zonke
endiwagxothele kuzo amasalela; utsho uYehova wemikhosi.

<span id="an_8:4">8:4</span> Yithi ke kubo, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Baya
kuwa, bangavuki na? Uya kuphamba, angabuyi na umntu?

<span id="an_8:5">8:5</span> Kungathuba lini na ukuba aba bantu
baseYerusalem baphambe ngokuphamba okungunaphakade? Babambelela
engohlisweni, bengavumi ukubuya.

<span id="an_8:6">8:6</span> Ndabaza indlebe, ndeva, bathetha into
engeyiyo; akukho bani uzohlwayayo ngeento zakhe ezimbi, athi, Yintoni na
le ndiyenzileyo? Bonke bephela babuyela ekugidimeni kwabo, njengehashe
lifunzela emfazweni.

<span id="an_8:7">8:7</span> Kanti nengwamza ezulwini iyawazi amaxesha
ayo amisiweyo; nehobe nehlankomo nendwe ziligcinile ixesha lokufika
kwazo; ke bona abantu bam abalazi isiko likaYehova.

<span id="an_8:8">8:8</span> Ningathini na ukuthi, Sizizilumko, umyalelo
kaYehova unathi? Yabonani, okwenene usiba lwababhali olubuxoki luwenze
wabubuxoki.

<span id="an_8:9">8:9</span> Zidanile izilumko, ziqhiphuke umbilini,
zibanjisiwe; yabona, ziyalicekisa ilizwi likaYehova; zinobulumko
bukabani na ke?

<span id="an_8:10">8:10</span> Ngako oko abafazi babo ndiya kubanikela
kubambi, namasimi abo ndiwanikele kwabawahluthayo; ngokuba, bethabathela
komncinane besa komkhulu, bonke bephela babawa bebawile; bethabathela
kumprofeti besa kumbingeleli, bonke bephela benza ngobuxoki.

<span id="an_8:11">8:11</span> Bakuphilisa kalula ukwaphuka kwentombi
yabantu bam, besithi, Luxolo, luxolo; kungekho luxolo.

<span id="an_8:12">8:12</span> Baya kudaniswa, ngokuba benze amasikizi;
noko ke abadani nokudana, abakwazi ukuba neentloni; ngako oko baya kuwa
phakathi kwabawayo, ngexesha lokubavelela kwam baya kukhubeka; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_8:13">8:13</span> Ndiya kubatshayela impela, utsho uYehova;
kungabikho zidiliya emdiliyeni, kungabikho makhiwane emkhiwaneni; igqabi
liya kubuna; ndisuke ndimise abo baya kugqitha phezu kwabo.

<span id="an_8:14">8:14</span> Sihlaleleni na? Zihlanganiseni, singene
emizini enqatyisiweyo, sitshabalale khona; ngokuba uYehova uThixo wethu
uza kusitshabalalisa, asiseze inyongo; ngokuba sonile kuYehova.

<span id="an_8:15">8:15</span> Besithembe uxolo, akwabakho nto
ilungileyo: besithembe ixesha lokuphiliswa, nanko ikukudandatheka.

<span id="an_8:16">8:16</span> Livakala livela kwaDan ithatha lamahashe
abo; ngezwi lokukhonya kweembalasane zamahashe abo liyanyikima ilizwe
lonke. Bayeza, bayalidla ilizwe nenzaliseko yalo, umzi nabemi bawo.

<span id="an_8:17">8:17</span> Ngokuba, yabonani, ndithumela phakathi
kwenu iinyoka, amarhamba angenakukhafulwa, anilume; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_8:18">8:18</span> Uye phi na umthuthuzeli wam esingqaleni?
Inobulwelwe kum intliziyo yam.

<span id="an_8:19">8:19</span> Nalo ilizwi lokuzibika kwentombi yabantu
bakowethu, livela ezweni elikude, lisithi, UYehova akakho na eZiyon?
akakho na kuyo ukumkani wayo? Kungathuba lini na ukuba bandiqumbise
ngemifanekiso yabo eqingqiweyo, ngeento ezingento zolunye uhlanga?

<span id="an_8:20">8:20</span> Ukuvuna kudlule, ihlobo liphelile, thina
ke asikasindiswa.

<span id="an_8:21">8:21</span> Ngenxa yokwaphuka kwentombi yabantu
bakowethu, ndaphukile; ndinezimnyama zokuzila, ndibanjwe kukumangaliswa.

<span id="an_8:22">8:22</span> Akukho mafutha aqholiweyo na eGiliyadi?
Akukho gqirha na khona? Kutheni na ke ukuba kungabotshwa ukwaphuka
kwentombi yabantu bakowethu?

<span id="an_9:1">9:1</span> Ayaba intloko yam ibingamanzi, amehlo am
aba lithende leenyembezi; bendiya kubalilela imini nobusuku ababuleweyo
bentombi yabantu bakowethu!

<span id="an_9:2">9:2</span> Akwaba bendinendawo yokulalisa kwabahambi
entlango; bendiya kubashiya abantu bakowethu, ndimke kubo! Ngokuba bonke
ngabakrexezi, yingqungquthela yamanginingini.

<span id="an_9:3">9:3</span> Bayalutyeda ulwimi lwabo ngobuxoki
njengesaphetha; abaphathi ngokuthembeka ezweni; baphuma entweni embi,
bangene entweni embi, babe mna ke bengandazi; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_9:4">9:4</span> Elowo makamlumkele ummelwane wakhe,
ningakholosi nangomzalwana; ngokuba wonke umzalwana wenza ubuqhinga,
wonke ummelwane uhamba ehleba.

<span id="an_9:5">9:5</span> Elowo uyamkhohlisa ummelwane wakhe,
abathethi nyaniso; bafundisa ulwimi lwabo ukuthetha ubuxoki, bazidinise
ngokwenza okugwenxa.

<span id="an_9:6">9:6</span> Ukuhlala kwakho kuphakathi kwenkohliso;
ngenkohliso abavumi ukundazi; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_9:7">9:7</span> Ngako oko, utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi,
Yabona, ndiya kubanyibilikisa, ndibacikide; ngokuba ndingathini na
ngenxa yentombi yabantu bam?

<span id="an_9:8">9:8</span> Lutolo olubulalayo ulwimi lwabo; bathetha
inkohliso; omnye uthetha uxolo ngomlomo wakhe kummelwane wakhe, ukanti
embilinini wakhe umlalele.

<span id="an_9:9">9:9</span> Mandingabaveleli na ke ngenxa yezo zinto?
utsho uYehova; ungaziphindezeli na umphefumlo wam kuhlanga olunje?

<span id="an_9:10">9:10</span> Ngenxa yeentaba ndibeka isililo nesimema,
nangenxa yamakriwa entlango ndibeka isimbonono; ngokuba afakwe isikhuni,
akwabakho bani ugqithayo kuwo, alavakala izwi lemfuyo; kuthabathela
ezintakeni zezulu lwesa ezilweni, kusatyiwe, kwemkiwa.

<span id="an_9:11">9:11</span> Ndiyenze iYerusalem yangumwewe,
yazizikhundla zeempungutye; ndiyenze imizi yakwaYuda yangamanxuwa, ayaba
nammi.

<span id="an_9:12">9:12</span> Ngubani na indoda elumkileyo, ikuqonde
oku? othethileyo kuyo umlomo kaYehova, ikuxele? Kungenxa yani na ukuba
ilizwe litshabalale, lifakwe isikhuni njengentlango, kungabikho bani
ugqitha kulo?

<span id="an_9:13">9:13</span> Wathi uYehova, Kungenxa enokuba
bewushiyile umyalelo wam, endawubeka phambi kwabo, abaliphulaphula
ilizwi lam, abahamba ngawo.

<span id="an_9:14">9:14</span> Balandela ubungqola bentliziyo yabo,
balandela ooBhahali, into abayifundiswa ngooyise.

<span id="an_9:15">9:15</span> Ngako oko, utsho uYehova wemikhosi,
uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabona, ndiya kubadlisa aba bantu umhlonyane,
ndibaseze inyongo;

<span id="an_9:16">9:16</span> ndibaphangalalise phakathi kweentlanga,
ababengazazi bona nooyise; ndilithumele ikrele emva kwabo, ndide
ndibaphelise.

<span id="an_9:17">9:17</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi, Gqalani,
nibize iintokazi ezenza isimbonono, zize, nithumele kwezilumkileyo,
zize;

<span id="an_9:18">9:18</span> zingxame, ziphimisele phezu kwethu
isimema; ehle iinyembezi amehlo ethu, zityityizele amanzi iinkophe
zethu.

<span id="an_9:19">9:19</span> Ngokuba ilizwi lesimema livakala liphuma
eZiyon, lisithi, Hayi, ukubhuqeka kwethu! Sidane kakhulu, kuba
silishiyile ilizwe, kuba bewakhahlele phantsi amakhaya ethu.

<span id="an_9:20">9:20</span> Noko ke liveni, zintokazi, ilizwi
likaYehova, indlebe yenu ilamkele ilizwi lomlomo wakhe, nizifundise
iintombi zenu isimema, omnye afundise ummelwane wakhe isimbonono.

<span id="an_9:21">9:21</span> Ngokuba kunyukile ukufa ngeefestile
zethu; kungene ezingxandeni zethu ezinde, ukuba kunqumle abantwana
ezitratweni, amadodana endaweni yembutho.

<span id="an_9:22">9:22</span> Thetha uthi, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ziya
kuwa ke izidumbu zabantu, njengomgquba phezu kwentsimi, nanjengesinde
emva komvuni, kungabikho ubahlanganisayo.

<span id="an_9:23">9:23</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Isilumko
masingaqhayisi ngobulumko baso, igorha malingaqhayisi ngobugorha balo,
isityebi masingaqhayisi ngobutyebi baso.

<span id="an_9:24">9:24</span> Oqhayisayo makaqhayise ngale nto yokuba
endiqiqa, endazi mna ukuba ndinguYehova, owenza inceba, nesiko,
nobulungisa, ehlabathini; ngokuba ndinanze ezo zinto; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_9:25">9:25</span> Yabona, iyeza imihla, utsho uYehova,
endiya kubohlwaya ngayo bonke abalukileyo, phofu bengalukile:

<span id="an_9:26">9:26</span> amaYiputa, namaYuda, namaEdom, noonyana
baka-Amon, namaMowabhi, noonquthula-iinwele, abemi entlango; ngokuba
zonke iintlanga zingabangalukileyo, nendlu yonke yakwaSirayeli
ingalukile ngentliziyo.

<span id="an_10:1">10:1</span> Liveni ilizwi alithethayo kuni uYehova,
ndlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_10:2">10:2</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Musani ukuziqhelisa
indlela yeentlanga, ningaqhiphuki umbilini yimiqondiso yezulu, ngakuba
iintlanga ziqhiphuke umbilini yiyo.

<span id="an_10:3">10:3</span> Ngokuba imimiselo yezizwe ayinto yanto.
Kuba izithixo zingumthi ogawulwe ehlathini, sisenzo sezandla zengcibi
ngezembe.

<span id="an_10:4">10:4</span> Izivathisa ngesilivere nangegolide;
baziqinisa ngezikhonkwane nangezando, ukuba zingagexagexi.

<span id="an_10:5">10:5</span> Zinjengentsika echweliweyo, azithethi;
zimele ukuthwalwa, ngokuba zingenakuhamba. Musani ukuzoyika; kuba
azinakwenza bubi; kwanokulungisa azinako.

<span id="an_10:6">10:6</span> Akukho namnye unjengawe, Yehova; umkhulu
wena, likhulu igama lakho, linobugorha.

<span id="an_10:7">10:7</span> Ngubani na ongeze akoyike, Kumkani
weentlanga? Ngokuba kukufanele; kuba phakathi kwezilumko zonke
zeentlanga, naphakathi kwezikumkani zonke, akukho namnye unjengawe.

<span id="an_10:8">10:8</span> Zizityhakala, ziinyabi zodwa; uqeqesho
lwento engento, ngumthi.

<span id="an_10:9">10:9</span> Yisilivere ekhandiweyo, iziswa ivela
eTarshishe, negolide yaseUfazi, isenzo sengcibi nesezandla
zomnyibilikisi wegolide; yimisonto emsi nemfusa izambatho zazo; zonke
ziphela zisisenzo sezilumko.

<span id="an_10:10">10:10</span> Ke yena uYehova nguThixo, inyaniso,
nguThixo ophilileyo, ngukumkani ongunaphakade; ihlabathi liyanyikima
buburhalarhume bakhe, neentlanga azinakuluthwala ubhavumo lwakhe.

<span id="an_10:11">10:11</span> Notsho kubo ukuthi, Bona oothixo
abangalenzanga izulu nehlabathi, baya kudaka ehlabathini, naphantsi
kwezulu.

<span id="an_10:12">10:12</span> Ke yena ngulowenza ihlabathi ngamandla
akhe; ulozinzisa elimiweyo ngobulumko bakhe; waneka izulu ngengqondo
yakhe;

<span id="an_10:13">10:13</span> kwakubon’ ukuba kukho isithonga
sokwenza kwakhe, ingxolo yamanzi ezulwini, unyusa amafu esiphelweni
sehlabathi; imvula uyenzela imibane, arhole umoya koovimba bakhe.

<span id="an_10:14">10:14</span> Uba sisityhakala wonke umntu,
engenakwazi; udaniswa wonke umnyibilikisi wegolide ngumfanekiso
oqingqiweyo, ngokuba umfanekiso wakhe otyhidiweyo bubuxoki, awunamoya.

<span id="an_10:15">10:15</span> Zingamampunge ezo zinto, zizenzo
zokugxekwa; ngexesha lokuvelelwa kwazo ziyadaka.

<span id="an_10:16">10:16</span> Akanjengazo yena uSahlulelo sikaYakobi,
ngokuba ngumbumbi weento zonke yena; uSirayeli sisizwe selifa lakhe;
nguYehova wemikhosi, igama lakhe.

<span id="an_10:17">10:17</span> Hlanganisa impahla yakho, umke nayo
kweli lizwe, wena uhleliyo ekungqingweni.

<span id="an_10:18">10:18</span> Ngokuba uYehova utshilo ukuthi, Yabona,
ngesi sihlandlo, ndisawula abemi belizwe, ndibabandezele, ukuze
bafunyanwe.

<span id="an_10:19">10:19</span> Athi ke mna, ngenxa yokwaphuka kwam!
Lelokubulala inxeba lam; ke mna ndithi, Inyaniso, sisifo sam esi, ndiya
kusinyamezela.

<span id="an_10:20">10:20</span> Intente yam ibhuqiwe, neentambo zam
zonke ziqhawukile; oonyana bam baphumile kum, ababa sabakho; akusekho
uyitwabululayo intente yam, amise amalengalenga am.

<span id="an_10:21">10:21</span> Ngokuba abalusi baba zizityhakala,
abamquqela uYehova; ngenxa yoko abenzanga ngangqiqo, wachithwachitwa
wonke umhlambi wabo.

<span id="an_10:22">10:22</span> Phulaphulani! Kuvakala into; nantso
isiza! Yingxolo enkulu, iphuma ezweni asentla, ukuze imizi yakwaYuda ibe
ngamanxuwa, ibe sisikhundla seempungutye.

<span id="an_10:23">10:23</span> Ndiyazi, Yehova, ukuba ayikhona
emntwini indlela yakhe; akukhona endodeni ehambayo ukuqinisela
ukunyathela kwayo.

<span id="an_10:24">10:24</span> Ndithethise, Yehova, kodwa kube
ngokwesiko, kungabi ngomsindo wakho, hleze undinciphise.

<span id="an_10:25">10:25</span> Phalaza ubushushu bakho phezu
kweentlanga ezingakwaziyo, naphezu kwemizalwane engalinquliyo igama
lakho; ngokuba zimdlile uYakobi, zimdlile zamgqiba, ikriwa lakhe zalenza
laba senkangala.

<span id="an_11:1">11:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_11:2">11:2</span> Waveni amazwi alo mnqophiso, nithethe
kumadoda akwaYuda, nakubemi baseYerusalem;

<span id="an_11:3">11:3</span> uthi kubo, Utsho uYehova, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Mayiqalekiswe indoda engawevayo amazwi alo
mnqophiso,

<span id="an_11:4">11:4</span> ndabawisela umthetho ngawo ooyihlo, mhla
ndabakhuphayo ezweni laseYiputa, ezikweni lesinyithi; ndathi,
Liphulaphuleni ilizwi lam, nenze ngako konke endiniwisela umthetho
ngako: noba ngabantu bam, mna ndibe nguThixo wenu;

<span id="an_11:5">11:5</span> ukuze ndisimise isifungo endasifungela
ooyihlo, ukuba ndibanike ilizwe elibaleka amasi nobusi, njengoko kunjalo
namhla. Ndaphendula mna, ndathi, Amen, Yehova.

<span id="an_11:6">11:6</span> Wathi uYehova kum, Wamemeze la mazwi onke
emizini yakwaYuda, nasezitratweni zaseYerusalem, uthi, Yivani amazwi alo
mnqophiso, niwenze.

<span id="an_11:7">11:7</span> Ngokuba ndaqononondisa ndiqononondisa
koyihlo, mhla ndabakhuphayo ezweni laseYiputa unanamhla, ndiqononondisa
kwakusasa, ndisithi, Liphulaphuleni ilizwi lam.

<span id="an_11:8">11:8</span> Ke abevanga, abayithobanga indlebe yabo;
bahamba elowo ngobungqola bentliziyo yakhe enobubi. Ndesuka ke ndazisa
phezu kwabo onke amazwi alo mnqophiso, ndabawisela umthetho ngawo, ukuba
bawenze; abawenza.

<span id="an_11:9">11:9</span> UYehova wathi kum, Kufunyenwe iyelenqe
phakathi kwamadoda akwaYuda, naphakathi kwabemi baseYerusalem.

<span id="an_11:10">11:10</span> Babuyele kuzo izenzo ezigwenxa zooyise
bamandulo, ababengavumi ukuweva amazwi am; abasuka bona balandela thixo
bambi ukuze babakhonze; indlu kaSirayeli nendlu kaYuda zawaphula
umnqophiso wam endawenza nooyise.

<span id="an_11:11">11:11</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabona,
ndibazisela ububi abangayi kuba nako ukuphuma kubo; bakhale kum,
ndingabaphulaphuli.

<span id="an_11:12">11:12</span> Iya kuhamba ke imizi yakwaYuda nabemi
baseYerusalem, bakhale koothixo abaqhumisela kubo, bangabasindisi
nokubasindisa ngexesha lobubi babo.

<span id="an_11:13">11:13</span> Ngokuba ngangenani lemizi yakho, baba
ngako oothixo bakaYuda; ngangenani lezitrato zaseYerusalem, zaba ngako
izibingelelo enazimisela into elisikizi, izibingelelo zokuqhumisela
kuBhahali.

<span id="an_11:14">11:14</span> Wena ke musa ukubathandazela aba bantu,
ungaphimiseli kuhlahlamba nakuthandaza ngenxa yabo; ngokuba andiyi kuva
ngexesha lokukhala kwabo kum, ngenxa yobubi babo.

<span id="an_11:15">11:15</span> Ifuna ntoni intanda yam endlwini yam,
isenza amayelenqe nje? Izibhambathiso nenyama engcwele zobususa na ububi
bakho kuwe? Ubungandula udlamke.

<span id="an_11:16">11:16</span> UYehova wakubiza ngegama lokuba
ungumnquma oluhlaza, oyimpuluswa, osiqhamo sihle; wafaka isikhuni kuwo,
kukho isandi sengxabatshitshi enkulu, aviveka amasebe awo.

<span id="an_11:17">11:17</span> Ke uYehova wemikhosi, owakutyalayo,
uthethe okubi ngawe, ngenxa yezinto ezimbi zendlu kaSirayeli nezendlu
kaYuda, abazenzeleyo ukuze bandiqumbise ngokuqhumisela uBhahali.

<span id="an_11:18">11:18</span> Ke kaloku uYehova wandazisa, ndazi;
waza wandibonisa oko iintlondi zabo.

<span id="an_11:19">11:19</span> Ndaba njengemana embuna esiwa
ekuxhelweni; bendingazi ukuba bacebe icebo ngam, besithi, Masiwonakalise
umthi kunye neziqhamo zawo, masimnqumle ezweni labaphilileyo, lingabi
sakhunjulwa igama lakhe.

<span id="an_11:20">11:20</span> Yehova wemikhosi, ugwebayo
ngobulungisa, uzicikidayo izintso nentliziyo, mandiyibone impindezelo
yakho kubo; ugokuba ndiyityhilile kuwe imbambano yam nabo.

<span id="an_11:21">11:21</span> Ngako oko, utsho uYehova ngamadoda
aseAnatoni, awungxameleyo umphefumlo wakho, esithi, Uze ungaprofeti
egameni likaYehova, ukuze ungafi ngezandla zethu;

<span id="an_11:22">11:22</span> ngako oko, utsho uYehova wemikhosi
ukuthi, Yabona, ndiya kuwavelela; amadodana aya kufa likrele, oonyana
babo neentombi zabo ziya kufa yindlala.

<span id="an_11:23">11:23</span> Akuyi kubakho masalela kubo, ngokuba
ndiwazisela ububi amadoda aseAnatoti, umnyaka wokuvelelwa kwawo.

<span id="an_12:1">12:1</span> Ulilungisa, Yehova, xa ndibambeneyo nawe;
ndothetha iindawo ezisesikweni zodwa. Kungathuba lini na ukuba indlela
yabangendawo ibe nempumelelo, babe nokuchulumacha bonke abanginiza
benginizile?

<span id="an_12:2">12:2</span> Ubatyele, bendela nokwendela iingcambu;
bayakhula, benze neziqhamo. Usondele emlonyeni wabo, wakude ezintsweni
zabo.

<span id="an_12:3">12:3</span> Wena, Yehova, uyandazi; uyandibona,
uyicikida intliziyo yam enawe. Baqweqwedise njengeegusha, baxhelwe,
ubangcwalisele umhla wokubulawa.

<span id="an_12:4">12:4</span> Kunini na ilizwe linesijwili, umfuno
wamasimi onke womile? Ngenxa yeento ezimbi zabemi balo, ziphephethekile
iinkomo neentaka; ngokuba besithi, Akayi kulibona ikamva lethu.

<span id="an_12:5">12:5</span> Xa ugidime nabeenyawo, bakudinisa,
wothini na ukushiyiselana namahashe? Xa ukholose ngelizwe elinoxolo,
wothini na ekweneni kweYordan?

<span id="an_12:6">12:6</span> Ngokuba nabazalwana bakho, nendlu
kayihlo, banginizile kuwe nabo; bayamemeza emva kwakho nabo ngezwikazi
elikhulu. Musa ukukholwa ngabo, xa bathetha izinto ezilungileyo kuwe.

<span id="an_12:7">12:7</span> Ndiyishiyile indlu yam, ndililahlile
ilifa lam, ndiyinikele intanda yomphefumlo wam esandleni seentshaba
zayo.

<span id="an_12:8">12:8</span> Ilifa lam lisuke laba njengengonyama
yasehlathini kum, lindikhuphele ilizwi lalo; ngenxa yoko ndilithiyile.

<span id="an_12:9">12:9</span> Ilifa lam lukhozi oluthe chokochoko na
kum, ukuba iinkozi zilingungele nje? Yizani, nihlanganise onke
amarhamncwa asendle; waziseni adle.

<span id="an_12:10">12:10</span> Abalusi abaninzi basonakalisile
isidiliya sam, basingqushile isiziba sam somhlaba; basibharhisile
isiziba sam esinqwenelekayo, sayintlango.

<span id="an_12:11">12:11</span> Basibharhisile; sisijwili ngeenxa zonke
kum; sibharhile, kusenkangala kulo lonke ilizwe, ngokuba akubangakho
mntu ukubekela intliziyo oko.

<span id="an_12:12">12:12</span> Eluqayini lonke lwasentlango kufike
ababhuqi; ngokuba ikrele likaYehova liyadla, lithabathela ekupheleni
kwelizwe, lise ekupheleni kwelizwe; akukho luxolo kwinyama yonke.

<span id="an_12:13">12:13</span> Bahlwayela ingqolowa, bavuna ameva;
bazidubile, abafeza lutho. Danani ke lungeniselo lwenu, ngenxa
yobushushu bomsindo kaYehova.

<span id="an_12:14">12:14</span> Utsho uYehova ngabamelwane bam bonke
abanobubi, abachukumisa ilifa endalidlisa abantu bam amaSirayeli,
ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiyabanyothula emhlabeni wabo, ndiyinyothule indlu
yakwaYuda phakathi kwabo.

<span id="an_12:15">12:15</span> Kuya kuthi, emveni kokuba
ndibanyothule, ndibuye ndibe nemfesane kubo, ndibabuyisele elowo elifeni
lakhe, elowo emhlabeni wakhe.

<span id="an_12:16">12:16</span> Kothi, ukuba bathe bazifunda
ngenkuthalo iindlela zabantu bam; ukuba bafunge igama lam, bathi, Ehleli
nje uYehova, njengoko babafundisayo abantu bam ukufunga uBhahali; baze
bakheke phakathi kwabantu bam.

<span id="an_12:17">12:17</span> Ke ukuba bathe abeva, ndolunyothula olu
hlanga, ndilunyothule, ndilutshabalalise; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_13:1">13:1</span> Utsho uYehova kum ukuthi, Hamba uye
uzithengele umbhinqo welinen, uwubeke esinqeni sakho, ke uze ungawufaki
emanzini.

<span id="an_13:2">13:2</span> Ndawuthenga ke umbhinqo ngokwelizwi
likaYehova, ndawubeka esinqeni sam.

<span id="an_13:3">13:3</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum okwesibini,
lisithi,

<span id="an_13:4">13:4</span> Wuthabathe umbhinqo owuthengileyo,
osesinqeni sakho, usuke uye emEfrati, uwufihle khona emfanteni
yengxondorha.

<span id="an_13:5">13:5</span> Ndaya, ndawufihla emEfrati, njengoko
wandiwisela umthetho ngako uYehova.

<span id="an_13:6">13:6</span> Kwathi, ekupheleni kwemihla emininzi,
wathi uYehova kum, Suka uye emEfrati, uwuthabathe khona umbhinqo
endakuwisela umthetho ngawo, ukuba uwufihle khona.

<span id="an_13:7">13:7</span> Ndaya ke emEfrati, ndemba, ndawuthabatha
umbhinqo kuloo ndawo bendiwufihle kuyo, nango wonakele umbhinqo,
ungasenamsebenzi.

<span id="an_13:8">13:8</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_13:9">13:9</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ndiya kwenjenje
ukulonakalisa ikratshi lakwaYuda, ikratshi elikhulu laseYerusalem.

<span id="an_13:10">13:10</span> Aba bantu banobubi, bangavumiyo ukuva
amazwi am, bahambayo ngobungqola bentliziyo yabo, balandela thixo bambi,
ukuze babakhonze, baqubude kubo: baya kuba njengaloo mbhinqo
ungasenamsebenzi.

<span id="an_13:11">13:11</span> Ngokuba njengokuba umbhinqo unamathela
esinqeni sendoda, ndenjenjalo ukuyinamathelisa kum yonke indlu
kaSirayeli, nendlu yonke kaYuda, utsho uYehova; ukuze kum ibe ngabantu,
ibe ligama, ibe yindumiso, ibe sisihombo; ke abevanga.

<span id="an_13:12">13:12</span> Uze uthethe kubo eli lizwi: Utsho
uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yonke imiphanda iyazaliswa
ngewayini. Baya kuthi kuwe, Asazi nokwazi na, ukuba yonke imiphanda
iyazaliswa ngewayini?

<span id="an_13:13">13:13</span> Wothi ke kubo, Utsho uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, ndibazalisa ngokunxila bonke abemi beli lizwe, kwaookumkani
abahlalele uDavide etroneni yakhe, nababingeleli, nabaprofeti, nabemi
bonke baseYerusalem;

<span id="an_13:14">13:14</span> ndibahlekezele elowo kuwabo, ooyise
noonyana kunye, utsho uYehova. Andiyi kuba nalufefe, andiyi kuba
nanceba, andiyi kuba namfesane, ukuba ndingabonakalisi.

<span id="an_13:15">13:15</span> Yivani, nibeke indlebe; musani
ukuzidla, ngokuba uYehova uyathetha.

<span id="an_13:16">13:16</span> Mzukiseni uYehova uThixo wenu,
engekahlisi ubumnyama, zingekabetheki ezintabeni zocolothi iinyawo zenu;
nithembe ukukhanya, ke yena ukwenza ithunzi lokufa, akwenze
isithokothoko.

<span id="an_13:17">13:17</span> Ukuba anithanga nikuve oko, wolila
umphefumlo wam entsithelweni ngenxa yoqhankqalazo lwenu; lityityizele
lityityizela, lihle iinyembezi, iliso lam; ngokuba umhlambi kaYehova
uthinjiwe.

<span id="an_13:18">13:18</span> Yithi kukumkani nakwinkosikazi,
Zithobeni, hlalani phantsi; ngokuba siyehla ezintlokweni zenu isithsaba
sokuhomba kwenu.

<span id="an_13:19">13:19</span> Imizi yelisezantsi ivaliwe, akukho
ungayivulayo; uYuda ufudusiwe ephela; ufudusiwe kanye.

<span id="an_13:20">13:20</span> Phakamisani amehlo enu, nibone abavela
entla. Uphi na umhlambi obuwunikiwe, impahla yakho emfutshane entle?

<span id="an_13:21">13:21</span> Wothini na, xa athe abo ke ubaqhelise
ukuba ngamakholwane akho, wabenza bangabaveleli, bayintloko kuwe? Ayiyi
kukubamba na inimba, njengomfazi ozalayo?

<span id="an_13:22">13:22</span> Naxa uthe entliziyweni yakho, Kungani
na ukuba ndifikelwe zezi zinto? ngobuninzi bobugwenxa bakho utyhilekile
ingubo, zagonyamelwa izithende zakho.

<span id="an_13:23">13:23</span> UmKushi unokuluguqula na ulusu lwakhe,
nengwe inokuwaguqula na amabala ayo? ningaba ke ninako ukulungisa nani,
baqhele ukwenza okubi.

<span id="an_13:24">13:24</span> Ndiya kubaphangalalisa ke, njengomququ
ophephuka nomoya wentlango.

<span id="an_13:25">13:25</span> Liqashiso lakho elo, isabelo sakho
esilinganiselweyo ndim, utsho uYehova; ngokuba undilibele, wakholosa
ngobuxoki.

<span id="an_13:26">13:26</span> Nam ndiya kuyibhenqa ingubo yakho, ibe
phezu kobuso bakho, kubonakale ukucukucezeka kwakho.

<span id="an_13:27">13:27</span> Ukukrexeza kwakho nokukhonya kwakho
amanyala okuhenyuza kwakho ezindulini ezindle, ndiwabonile amazothe
akho. Athi ke wena, Yerusalem! Akuyi kuhlambuluka, ingafanelana.
ingumzuzu ongakanani na.

<span id="an_14:1">14:1</span> Into eyafikayo kuYeremiya, ililizwi
likaYehova, ngendawo yokunqumka kwemvula.

<span id="an_14:2">14:2</span> Linesijwili elakwaYuda; amasango alo athe
matshamatsha, ahlala emhlabeni enezimnyama zokuzila; kuyenyuka ukukhala
kweYerusalem.

<span id="an_14:3">14:3</span> Iingangamsha zabo zithuma abaphantsi
kwazo amanzi; bafika emaquleni, bangafumani manzi; babuya imiphanda yabo
ize, bedanile; bathi nqa, bagqubuthele intloko.

<span id="an_14:4">14:4</span> Ngenxa yomhlaba oqhiphuke umbilini, kuba
kungabangakho mvula ezweni, abalimi badanile, bagqubuthele intloko.

<span id="an_14:5">14:5</span> Ewe, nemazi yexhama iyazala endle,
iyishiye inkonyana, ngokuba kungekho luhlaza.

<span id="an_14:6">14:6</span> Namaesile asendle emi eluqayini, esezela
umoya njengeempungutye; ayaphela amehlo awo, ngokuba kungekho mifuno.

<span id="an_14:7">14:7</span> Ukuba ubugwenxa bethu bungqina ngathi,
Yehova, yenza ngenxa yegama lakho; ngokuba kuninzi ukuphamba kwethu;
sonile kuwe.

<span id="an_14:8">14:8</span> Themba likaSirayeli, Msindisi wakhe
ngexesha lembandezelo, yini na ukuba ube njengomphambukeli kweli lizwe,
ube njengomhambi olalise okobusuku obunye?

<span id="an_14:9">14:9</span> Yini na ukuba ube njengendoda esuke yathi
nka, ube njengegorha elingenakusindisa; kanti uphakathi kwethu, Yehova,
negama lakho sibizwe ngalo. Musa ukusiyekela.

<span id="an_14:10">14:10</span> Utsho uYehova kwaba bantu, ukuthi,
Benjenje ukuthanda ukubhadula; iinyawo zabo abazinqandanga; uYehova
akakholiswa ngabo; kungoku uya kubukhumbula ubugwenxa babo, azivelele
izono zabo.

<span id="an_14:11">14:11</span> Wathi uYehova kum, Musa ukubathandazela
aba bantu, ukuba kulunge kubo.

<span id="an_14:12">14:12</span> Xa bazila ukudla, andiyi kukuphulaphula
ukuhlahlamba kwabo; naxa banyusa amadini anyukayo neminikelo yokudla,
andiyi kukholiswa ngawo; ke ndiya kubaphelisa ngekrele, nangendlala,
nangendyikitya yokufa.

<span id="an_14:13">14:13</span> Ndaza ndathi, Kwowu, Nkosi Yehova,
yabona, abaprofeti bathi kubo, Aniyi kubona krele, nendlala aniyi kuba
nayo; ndiya kuninika uxolo oluyinyaniso kule ndawo.

<span id="an_14:14">14:14</span> Wathi uYehova kum, Abaprofeti baprofeta
ubuxoki egameni lam; andibathumanga, andibawiselanga mthetho,
andithethanga kubo; bona baniprofetela umbono wobuxoki, nokuvumisa,
nento engento, nenkohliso yentliziyo yabo.

<span id="an_14:15">14:15</span> Ngako oko uthi uYehova, ngokusingisele
kubaprofeti abaprofeta egameni lam, ndingabathumanga mna, abathi, Akuyi
kubakho krele nandlala kweli lizwe; uthi, Baya kufa likrele nayindlala
bona abo baprofeti.

<span id="an_14:16">14:16</span> Naba bantu, baprofetela bona, baya kuba
yimilahlwa ezitratweni zaseYerusalem ngenxa yendlala nekrele; kungabikho
ubangcwabayo, bona, nabafazi babo, noonyana babo, neentombi zabo,
ndibaphalazele ngeento zabo ezimbi.

<span id="an_14:17">14:17</span> Ngoko uze uthethe kubo eli lizwi
lokuthi, Amehlo am ahla iinyembezi ubusuku nemini, angaphezi; ngokuba
yaphulwe ngolwaphulo olukhulu inkazana eyintombi yabantu bakowethu,
ngenxeba elibulalayo kakhulu.

<span id="an_14:18">14:18</span> Ukuba ndithe ndaphuma ndaya
emaphandleni, nabo ababuleweyo likrele; ukuba ndithe ndangena kuwo umzi,
nabo abafa yindlala; ngokuba umprofeti kwanombingeleli bayaquleka ezweni
abangalaziyo.

<span id="an_14:19">14:19</span> Umcekise kwaphela na uYuda? Udimele na
yiZiyon umphefumlo wakho? Yini na ukuba usibethe, singabi nakuphiliswa?
Sithembe uxolo, akwabakho nto ilungileyo; sithembe ixesha lokuphiliswa,
nanko ikukudandatheka.

<span id="an_14:20">14:20</span> Siyakwazi, Yehova, okungendawo kwethu,
ubugwenxa boobawo; ngokuba sonile kuwe.

<span id="an_14:21">14:21</span> Ngenxa yegama lakho, musa ukusigiba;
ungayihlazisi itrone yobuqaqawuli bakho. Khumbula, ungawaphuli
umnqophiso wakho nathi.

<span id="an_14:22">14:22</span> Phakathi kothixo abangento beentlanga,
bakho na abanganisa imvula? Izulu lingayinika na imivumbi? Asinguwe na,
Yehova Thixo wethu? Sithembe wena; ngokuba uzenzile wena zonke ezo
zinto.

<span id="an_15:1">15:1</span> Wathi ke uYehova kum, Kungafanelana kumi
ooMoses noSamuweli phambi kwam, umphefumlo wam ubungebheki kwaba bantu.
Bagxothe ebusweni bam, baphume.

<span id="an_15:2">15:2</span> Kuya kuthi, xa bathe kuwe, Siphume siye
ngaphi na? uthi kubo, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Abokufa bafe; abekrele babe
ngabekrele; abendlala babe ngabendlala; abokuthinjwa bathinjwe.

<span id="an_15:3">15:3</span> Ndobavelela ngeentlobo ezine, utsho
uYehova: ikrele, ukuba libulale; izinja, ukuba zirhwiqilize; iintaka
zezulu nezilo zomhlaba, ukuba zidle, ukuba zonakalise.

<span id="an_15:4">15:4</span> Ndobanikela kwizikumkani zonke zehlabathi
ukuba babe yinto yokunqakulwa, ngenxa kaManase unyana kaHezekiya,
ukumkani wakwaYuda, ngenxa yoko wakwenzayo eYerusalem.

<span id="an_15:5">15:5</span> Ewe, ngubani na oya kuba nofefe kuwe,
Yerusalem? ngubani na oya kukukhuza? ngubani na oya kuphambuka, abuze
ukuphila kwakho?

<span id="an_15:6">15:6</span> Wena undilahlile, utsho uYehova, ubuye
umva; ndiya kusolula isandla sam ngakuwe, ndikonakalise; ndidiniwe
kukuzohlwaya.

<span id="an_15:7">15:7</span> Ndiyabachithachitha ngexhayi emasangweni
elizwe, ndibahluthe abantwana abantu bam, ndibatshabalalise, bengabuyi
nje ezindleleni zabo.

<span id="an_15:8">15:8</span> Abahlolokazi babo baziimfidi kum
kunentlabathi yolwandle; ndizisa kubo phezu konina wamadodana umbhuqi
emini enkulu; ndibawisela ngesiquphe inimba nokukhwankqiswa.

<span id="an_15:9">15:9</span> Uyantshwenya ozele abasixhenxe, uphuma
umphefumlo; liyatshona ilanga lakhe kusesemini; udanile, uneentloni;
namasalela abo ndiwanikela ekreleni phambi kweentshaba zabo; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_15:10">15:10</span> Athi ke mna, ma, ukuba uzale umna,
umntu wembambano, umntu wengxabano nehlabathi lonke! Andibolekanga,
andabolekwa; kanti bonke bephela bayanditshabhisa.

<span id="an_15:11">15:11</span> UYehova uthi, Inyaniso, ndiya
kukuqinisela wena kokulungileyo; inyaniso, utshaba ndiya kulubongozisa
kuwe, ngexesha lobubi nangexesha lembandezelo.

<span id="an_15:12">15:12</span> Sikha saphuke na isinyithi, isinyithi
sasentla, nobhedu?

<span id="an_15:13">15:13</span> Ubutyebi bakho nobuncwane bakho
ndobunikela ukuba bube lixhoba, kungengaxabiso, ngenxa yezono zakho
zonke, nasemideni yakho yonke;

<span id="an_15:14">15:14</span> ndibuweze neentshaba zakho, ndibuye
ezweni ongalaziyo; ngokuba kuphenjwe umlilo ngomsindo wam, uvutha phezu
kwenu.

<span id="an_15:15">15:15</span> Wena, Yehova, uyazi, Ndikhumbule,
undivelele, undiphindezelele kubasukeli bam; ekuzekeni kade komsindo
wakho ungandikhukulisi; yazi ukuba ndithwele ihlazo ngenxa yakho.

<span id="an_15:16">15:16</span> Afumaneka amazwi akho, ndawadla; amazwi
akho kum aba yimihlali nemivuyo yentliziyo yam, ngokuba ndabizwa ngegama
lakho, Yehova, Thixo wemikhosi.

<span id="an_15:17">15:17</span> Andihlalanga embuthweni yabahleki,
andidlamkanga nokudlamka; ngenxa yesandla sakho ndahlala ndedwa; ngokuba
undizalisile ngokubhavuma.

<span id="an_15:18">15:18</span> Yini na ukuba umvandedwa wam uhlale
uhleli, nenxeba lam libulale, lingavumi ukuphola? Wohla ube ngumlambo
okhohlisayo na kum, omanzi angahlaliyo na?

<span id="an_15:19">15:19</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ukuba
uthe wabuya, ndokubuyisa, ubuye ume phambi kwam; ukuba uthe wakhupha
okunqabileyo kokungeni, woba njengomlomo wam; abo baya kubuyela kuwe; ke
wena akuyi kubuyela kubo.

<span id="an_15:20">15:20</span> Ndiya kukwenza udonga lobhedu
olunqatyisiweyo kwaba bantu, balwe nawe, bangabi nakukuthini; ngokuba
ndinawe, ukuze ndikusindise mna, ndikuhlangule; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_15:21">15:21</span> Ndiya kukuhlangula esandleni
sabangendawo, ndikukhulule ekubambeni kwabangcangcazelisayo.

<span id="an_16:1">16:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_16:2">16:2</span> Uze ungazeki mfazi, ungabi nanyana
nazintombi kule ndawo.

<span id="an_16:3">16:3</span> Ngokuba uYehova utsho ngoonyana neentombi
ezizalelwa kule ndawo, nangoonina ababazalayo, nangooyise ababazalayo
kweli lizwe, ukuthi,

<span id="an_16:4">16:4</span> Baya kufa zizifo ezibulalayo,
bangambanjazelelwa, bangangcwatywa; baya kuba ngumgquba phezu komhlaba;
baya kuphela likrele nayindlala, nezidumbu zabo zibe kukudla kweentaka
zezulu nokwezilo zomhlaba.

<span id="an_16:5">16:5</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Musa
ukungena endlwini yesijwili, ungayi kumbambazela, ungabakhuzi; ngokuba
ndilususile kwaba bantu uxolo lwam, inceba nemfesane yam; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_16:6">16:6</span> Kuya kufa abakhulu kwanabancinane kweli
lizwe, bangangcwatywa, kungambanjazelwa ngenxa yabo, kungacentwa,
kungachetywa ntloko ngenxa yabo;

<span id="an_16:7">16:7</span> bangaqhekezelwa sonka esijwilini sabo,
ukuba bathuthuzelwe ngenxa yofileyo; bangasezwa ngendebe yentuthuzelo
ngenxa yooyise nangenxa yoonina.

<span id="an_16:8">16:8</span> Uze ungangeni endlwini yesidlo, ukuba
uhlale nabo, udle, usele.

<span id="an_16:9">16:9</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiya kuliphezisa kule ndawo, phambi
kwamehlo enu nangemihla yenu, izwi lemihlali nezwi lemivuyo, izwi
lomyeni nezwi lomtshakazi.

<span id="an_16:10">16:10</span> Ke kaloku kothi, xa uthe wabaxelela aba
bantu la mazwi onke, baza bathi kuwe, Kungenxa yani na ukuba uYehova
abuthethe ngathi bonke obu bubi bukhulu kangaka, buyini na ubugwenxa
bethu, siyini na isono sethu, esone ngaso kuYehova uThixo wethu?

<span id="an_16:11">16:11</span> wothi kubo, Kungenxa yokuba ooyihlo
bendishiyile, utsho uYehova; balandela thixo bambi, babakhonza, baqubuda
kubo; mna bandishiya, umyalelo wam abawugcina;

<span id="an_16:12">16:12</span> nasuka ke nina nenza okubi ngaphezu
kooyihlo; nanko, nilandela elowo ubungqola bentliziyo yakhe enobubi,
ningandiphulaphuli.

<span id="an_16:13">16:13</span> Ndiya kunijulela ngaphandle kweli
lizwe, niye nikhonzele khona apho thixo bambi imini nobusuku; ngokuba
ndingayi kuba natarhu kuni.

<span id="an_16:14">16:14</span> Ngako oko, yabonani, iyeza imihla,
utsho uYehova, ekungayi kuba sathiwa, Ehleli nje uYehova, owabanyusayo
oonyana bakaSirayeli ezweni laseYiputa; ekuya kuthiwa,

<span id="an_16:15">16:15</span> Ehleli nje uYehova, owabanyusayo
oonyana bakaSirayeli ezweni lasentla, nasemazweni onke ebebagxothele
kuwo; ndobabuyisela kowabo umhlaba endawunika ooyise.

<span id="an_16:16">16:16</span> Yabonani, ndithumela ababambisi
beentlanzi abaninzi, beze bababambise, utsho uYehova; emveni koko
ndithumele abazingeli abaninzi, beze babazingele, baphume nabo
ezintabeni zonke, nasezindulini zonke, nasezimfanteni zeengxondorha.

<span id="an_16:17">16:17</span> Ngokuba amehlo am akuzo zonke iindlela
zabo, azisithele kum; abufihlakele ubugwenxa babo phambi kwamehlo am.

<span id="an_16:18">16:18</span> Kuqala, ndobuvuza kabini ubugwenxa babo
nesono sabo ngenxa yokulihlambela kwabo ilizwe lam ngezidumbu zezinto
zabo ezinezothe, belizalisa ilifa lam ngamasikizi abo.

<span id="an_16:19">16:19</span> Yehova, mandla am, nqaba yam, ndawo
yokusabela kwam ngomhla wembandezelo, ziya kuza kuwe iintlanga, zivela
eziphelweni zehlabathi, zithi, Oobawo badla ilifa lobuxoki bodwa,
amampunge la, ekungekho nto inokunceda phakathi kwawo.

<span id="an_16:20">16:20</span> Umntu uya kuzenzela oothixo yini na,
bengengabo oothixo?

<span id="an_16:21">16:21</span> Ngako oko, yabona, ndiyabazisa ngesi
sihlandlo, ndibazise isandla sam nobugorha bam, bazi ukuba igama lam
linguYehova.

<span id="an_17:1">17:1</span> Isono sikaYuda sibhalwe ngenkxola
yesinyithi, sakrolwa ngetsolo ledayiman elucwecweni lwentliziyo yabo,
nasezimpondweni zezibingelelo zenu.

<span id="an_17:2">17:2</span> Njengokubakhumbula kwabo oonyana babo,
bayazikhumbula izibingelelo zabo, nooAshera babo ngasemithini eluhlaza,
ezindulini ezinde.

<span id="an_17:3">17:3</span> Ntaba yam esezweni, ubutyebi bakho
nobuncwane bakho bonke ndibunikela ekuphangweni, neziganga zakho ngenxa
yezono emideni yakho yonke.

<span id="an_17:4">17:4</span> Uya kuliyeka ngokwakho ilifa lakho
endakunikayo, ndikukhonzise kwiintshaba zakho elizweni ongalaziyo;
ngokuba niwuphembile umlilo ngomsindo wam, uvutha usa ephakadeni.

<span id="an_17:5">17:5</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Iqalekisiwe indoda
ekholose ngomntu, eyenza inyama ingalo yayo, intliziyo yayo imke nje
kuYehova;

<span id="an_17:6">17:6</span> ibe njengochushuluzayo enkqantosini,
ingaboni kufika nto ilungileyo; ime engqaqasini, entlango, ezweni
letyuwa elingenammi.

<span id="an_17:7">17:7</span> Isikelelwe indoda ekholose ngoYehova,
enkoloseko ikuYehova;

<span id="an_17:8">17:8</span> kuba yoba njengomthi omiliselwe emanzini,
unabise iingcambu zawo phezu komlambo, ungoyiki xa kuthe kweza
ubushushu; aqhame amagqabi awo, ungakhathali ngomnyaka wokubalela,
ungayeki ukuvelisa iziqhamo.

<span id="an_17:9">17:9</span> Intliziyo inenkohliso ngaphezu kweento
zonke, isisifo esibi; ngubani na onokuyazi?

<span id="an_17:10">17:10</span> Mna, Yehova, ndiyayigocagoca intliziyo,
ndiyazicikida izintso, ukuze ndinike ulowo nalowo ngokwendlela yakhe,
ngokwesiqhamo seentlondi zakhe.

<span id="an_17:11">17:11</span> Njengesikhwatsha esifukamela amaqanda
esingawazalanga, unjalo ozuza ubutyebi ngokungesesikweni; uya kubushiya
phakathi kwemihla yakhe, abe sisidenge ekupheleni kwakhe.

<span id="an_17:12">17:12</span> Wena trone yobuqaqawuli, mongamo
kwasekuqaleni, ndawo yengcwele yethu;

<span id="an_17:13">17:13</span> themba likaSirayeli, Yehova, bonke
abakushiyayo baya kudana. Abatyekayo kum baya kubhalelwa emhlabeni,
ngokuba belishiyile ithende lamanzi aphilileyo, uYehova.

<span id="an_17:14">17:14</span> Ndiphilise, Yehova, ndiphile;
ndisindise, ndisinde; ngokuba indumiso yam nguwe.

<span id="an_17:15">17:15</span> Yabona, bathi, Liphi na ilizwi
likaYehova? malize kalokunje.

<span id="an_17:16">17:16</span> Mna andikubalekelanga ukuba ngumalusi
emva kwakho; andiwunqwenelanga umhla onesifo, wena uyazi; okuphume
emlonyeni wam bekuphambi kobuso bakho.

<span id="an_17:17">17:17</span> Musa ukundiqhiphula umbilini; ulihlathi
lam ngomhla wobubi.

<span id="an_17:18">17:18</span> Mabadane abandisukelayo, mandingadani
mna; mabaqhiphuke umbilini bona, mandingaqhiphuki umbilini mna; bazisele
imini yobubi, ubaphule ngolwaphulo olubini.

<span id="an_17:19">17:19</span> UYehova watsho kum ukuthi, Hamba uye
kuma esangweni loonyana babantu, abangena ngalo ookumkani bakwaYuda,
abaphuma ngalo, nasemasangweni onke aseYerusalem;

<span id="an_17:20">17:20</span> uthi kubo, Liveni ilizwi likaYehova,
ninakumkani bakwaYuda, nani maYuda nonke, nani bemi bonke baseYerusalem,
bangenayo ngala masango.

<span id="an_17:21">17:21</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Zigcineni ngenxa
yemiphefumlo yenu, ningathwali mthwalo ngomhla wesabatha, niwungenise
ngamasango aseYerusalem;

<span id="an_17:22">17:22</span> ningaphumi nomthwalo ezindlwini zenu
ngomhla wesabatha, ningenzi nalinye ishishini. Wungcwaliseni umhla
wesabatha, njengoko ndabawiselayo umthetho ooyihlo.

<span id="an_17:23">17:23</span> Ke abevanga, abazithobanga iindlebe
zabo, bayenza lukhuni intamo yabo, ukuze bangevi, ukuze bangavumi
ntethiso.

<span id="an_17:24">17:24</span> Kothi ke, ukuba nithe nandiphulaphula,
utsho uYehova, anangenisa mthwalo ngamasango alo mzi ngomhla wesabatha,
nawungcwalisa umhla wesabatha, anenza nalinye ishishini ngawo:

<span id="an_17:25">17:25</span> kothi ke kungene ngamasango alo mzi
ookumkani nabathetheli, abahleli etroneni kaDavide, bekhwele
ezinqwelweni nasemahasheni, bona, nabathetheli babo, amadoda akwaYuda,
nabemi baseYerusalem; lo mzi umiwe ngonaphakade,

<span id="an_17:26">17:26</span> Baya kuvela emizini yakwaYuda,
nangeenxa zonke eYerusalem, nasezweni lakwaBhenjamin, nasesithabazini,
nakwelithe thabalala, nakwelisezantsi, bezisa amadini anyukayo,
nemibingelelo, neminikelo yokudla, nentlaka emhlophe; bangenise umbulelo
endlwini kaYehova.

<span id="an_17:27">17:27</span> Ke ukuba anithanga nindiphulaphule,
ukuba niwungcwalise umhla wesabatha, ningathwali mthwalo, ningangeni
ngamasango aseYerusalem ngomhla wesabatha: ndofaka isikhuni emasangweni
ayo, udle iingxande ezinde zaseYerusalem, ungacinywa.

<span id="an_18:1">18:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, lalisithi,

<span id="an_18:2">18:2</span> Suka uhle, uye endlwini yombumbi,
ndikuvise khona amazwi am.

<span id="an_18:3">18:3</span> Ndehla ke, ndaya endlwini yombumbi, nanko
esenza ishishini ezintendeni.

<span id="an_18:4">18:4</span> Sakonakala isitya abesenza ngodongwe,
esandleni sombumbi, wabuya wenza sitya simbi ngalo, njengoko kwakuthe
tye emehlweni ombumbi ukusenza.

<span id="an_18:5">18:5</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_18:6">18:6</span> Andinako na ukuxelisa lo mbumbi ukwenza
kuni, ndlu kaSirayeli? utsho uYehova. Yabonani, njengoko lunjalo udongwe
esandleni sombumbi, ninjalo nina esandleni sam, ndlu kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_18:7">18:7</span> Ngephanyazo ndithetha ngohlanga
nobukumkani, ukuba ndilunyothule, ukuba ndiludilize, ukuba
ndilutshabalalise.

<span id="an_18:8">18:8</span> Ukuba ke olo luhlanga lubuyile ezintweni
zalo ezimbi, olo ndithethe ngalo, ndozohlwaya ngenxa yobubi, ebe
ndisithi ndiza kubenza kulo.

<span id="an_18:9">18:9</span> Ngephanyazo ndithetha ngohlanga
nobukumkani, ukuba ndilwakhe, ukuba ndilutyale;

<span id="an_18:10">18:10</span> kodwa ke ukuba luthi lwenze okubi
emehlweni am, lungaliphulaphuli ilizwi lam, ndozohlwaya ngenxa
yokulungileyo, ebendisithi ndiza kukwenza kulo.

<span id="an_18:11">18:11</span> Ngoku ke khawuthethe kumadoda akwaYuda,
nakubemi baseYerusalem, uthi, Utshilo uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani,
ndinibumbela ububi, ndiceba ngani icebo; khanibuye elowo endleleni yakhe
enobubi, nilungise iindlela zenu neentlondi zenu.

<span id="an_18:12">18:12</span> Ke bona bathi, Kuncamekile; ngokuba
siya kulandela awethu amacebo, senza elowo ubungqola bentliziyo yakhe
enobubi.

<span id="an_18:13">18:13</span> Ngako oko, utsho uYehova ukuthi,
Khanibuze phakathi kweentlanga, ngubani na okhe weva into enje? Yenze
into ebanga amanwele kunene intombi enguSirayeli.

<span id="an_18:14">18:14</span> Ikhephu laseLebhanon liya kulishiya na
iliwa lasezweni? Amanzi anengqele, aqukuqelayo evela kude, aya kutsha
na?

<span id="an_18:15">18:15</span> Ukanti abantu bam bandilibele;
baqhumisela kwizinto ezikhohlakeleyo, zabakhubekisa ezindleleni zabo,
emendweni engunaphakade, ukuze bahambe ngeengqushu, ngendlela
engalungeleliswanga;

<span id="an_18:16">18:16</span> ukuze balenze ilizwe labo ummangaliso
nomsondlo ongunaphakade; bonke abagqitha kulo baya kumangaliswa,
bahlunguzele iintloko.

<span id="an_18:17">18:17</span> Njengomoya wasempumalanga, ndiya
kubaphangalalisa phambi kotshaba; ndibanikele umhlana, ndingabanikeli
ubuso, ngomhla wokusindeka kwabo.

<span id="an_18:18">18:18</span> Bathi ke, Yizani siyile iqhinga
ngoYeremiya; ngokuba awuyi kuphela umyalelo kumbingeleli, necebo
kwisilumko, nelizwi kumprofeti. Yizani simbethe ngolwimi, singawabazeli
ndlebe amazwi akhe onke.

<span id="an_18:19">18:19</span> Ndibazele indlebe, wena Yehova; live
izwi lababambene nam.

<span id="an_18:20">18:20</span> Kuya kuvuzwa ngobubi na esikhundleni
sokulungileyo, ukuba bawumbele isihogo nje umphefumlo wam? Khumbula
ukuma kwam phambi kwakho, ukuba ndithethe okulungileyo ngabo, ukuba
ndibuyise ubushushu bakho kubo.

<span id="an_18:21">18:21</span> Ngako oko banikele oonyana babo
endlaleni, ubalahlele emandleni ekrele, abafazi babo bangabi nabantwana,
babe ngabahlolokazi, amadoda abo abulawe kukufa, amadodana abo abulawe
likrele emfazweni.

<span id="an_18:22">18:22</span> Makuvakale ukukhala ezindlwini zabo, xa
abuzisela amatutu ngesiquphe; ngokuba bambe isihogo sokundibambisa,
iinyawo zam bazifihlela izibatha.

<span id="an_18:23">18:23</span> Ke wena, Yehova, uyawazi onke amaqhinga
abo okundibulala. Musa ukubuxolela ubugwenxa babo ngocamagusho,
ungasicimi isono sabo ebusweni bakho; ukuze bakhubeke phambi kwakho.
Ngexesha lomsindo wakho, yenza kubo.

<span id="an_19:1">19:1</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yiya uthenge
ingqayi yombumbi wezitya zodongwe, uthabathe inxenye yamadoda amakhulu
abantu, neyamadoda amakhulu ababingeleli;

<span id="an_19:2">19:2</span> uphume uye emfuleni wakwaBhen-hinom
olunge nesango leenkamba, umemeze khona amazwi endiya kuwathetha kuwe.

<span id="an_19:3">19:3</span> Wothi, Liveni ilizwi likaYehova, kumkani
bakwaYuda, nani bemi baseYerusalem; utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
wakwaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabonani, le ndawo ndiyizisela ububi, obuya
kubetha zithi nzwi iindlebe zabo bonke ababuvayo;

<span id="an_19:4">19:4</span> ngenxa enokuba bendishiyile mna, bayenza
eyasemzini le ndawo baqhumisela thixweni bambi abangabaziyo, bona,
nooyise, nookumkani bakwaYuda, bayizalisa le ndawo ngegazi labamsulwa.

<span id="an_19:5">19:5</span> Bamakhela uBhahali iziganga, ukuze
babatshise oonyana babo ngomlilo, babe ngamadini anyukayo kuBhahali,
into endingabawiselanga mthetho ngayo, endingayithethanga, engathanga
qatha entliziyweni yam.

<span id="an_19:6">19:6</span> Ngako oko uyabona, iyeza imihla, utsho
uYehova, engasayi kuba sabizwa le ndawo ngokuthi yiTofete, nomfula
wakwaBhen-hinom; kuya kuthiwa nguMfula wokuBulala.

<span id="an_19:7">19:7</span> Ndiya kulithululela iqhinga lakwaYuda
neYerusalem kule ndawo, ndibawise ngekrele phambi kweentshaba zabo,
nangezandla zabawufunayo umphefumlo wabo, ndizinikele izidumbu zabo zibe
kukudla ezintakeni zezulu nasezilweni zomhlaba.

<span id="an_19:8">19:8</span> Ndiya kuwenza lo mzi ube ngummangaliso
nomsondlo; bonke abagqitha kuwo bomangaliswa, benze umsondlo ngazo
izibetho zawo zonke.

<span id="an_19:9">19:9</span> Ndiya kubadlisa inyama yoonyana babo
