nenyama yeentombi zabo, elowo adle inyama yowabo ekungqingweni
nasekucuthweni, eziya kubacutha ngako iintshaba zabo, nabawufunayo
umphefumlo wabo.

<span id="an_19:10">19:10</span> Uze ke uyiqhekeze ingqayi emehlweni
amadoda ahamba nawe, uthi kuwo,

<span id="an_19:11">19:11</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi, Ndiya
kwenjenje ukubaqhekeza aba bantu nalo mzi, njengokuqhekezwa kwezitya
zombumbi, ezingasenakubuya zingcitywe; babangcwabele eTofete,
ngokungabikho ndawo yakungcwaba.

<span id="an_19:12">19:12</span> Ndiya kwenjenjalo kule ndawo, utsho
uYehova, nakubemi bayo, ukuze lo mzi ndiwenze ube njengeTofete.

<span id="an_19:13">19:13</span> Izindlu zeYerusalem nezindlu zookumkani
bakwaYuda zoba yinqambi, njengendawo yeTofete: zonke izindlu,
abaqhumisela phezu kophahla lwazo kuwo wonke umkhosi wasezulwini,
bathululele thixo bambi iminikelo ethululwayo kubo.

<span id="an_19:14">19:14</span> Wabuya uYeremiya eTofete, apho uYehova
abemthumele khona ukuba aprofete; wema entendelezweni yendlu kaYehova,
wathi kubantu bonke,

<span id="an_19:15">19:15</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiwuzisela lo mzi, nemizi yawo yonke,
bonke ububi endibuthethileyo ngawo; ngokuba beyenze lukhuni intamo yabo,
ukuze bangawevi amazwi am.

<span id="an_20:1">20:1</span> Ke kaloku, uPashure unyana kaImere,
umbingeleli, lowo ke ubengumveleli oyinganga endlwini kaYehova, weva
uYeremiya eprofeta la mazwi.

<span id="an_20:2">20:2</span> UPashure wambetha uYeremiya umprofeti,
wamfaka esitokisini esisesangweni lasentla lakwaBhenjamin, elisendlwini
kaYehova.

<span id="an_20:3">20:3</span> Kwathi ngengomso, uPashure wamkhupha
uYeremiya esitokisini. Wathi uYeremiya kuye, UYehova akathi linguPashure
igama lakho; uthi linguNxunguphala ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_20:4">20:4</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabona,
ndikwenza ukuba uzinxunguphalise wena ngokwakho, nabo bonke
abakuthandayo; bawe likrele leentshaba zabo, abone amehlo akho,
ndiwanikele onke amaYuda esandleni sokumkani waseBhabheli, abafudusele
eBhabheli, ababulale ngekrele.

<span id="an_20:5">20:5</span> Ndoyinikela yonke ingqwebo yalo mzi,
nongeniselo lwawo lonke, neento zawo zonke ezinqabileyo; nobuncwane
bonke bookumkani bakwaYuda ndibunikele ezandleni zeentshaba zabo,
zibuphange, zibuthabathe, zibuse eBhabheli.

<span id="an_20:6">20:6</span> Wena Pashure, nabo bonke abahleli
endlwini yakho, niya kuthinjwa; uye eBhabheli, ufele khona, ungcwatyelwe
khona, wena nabakuthandayo bonke, abaprofetele ubuxoki.

<span id="an_20:7">20:7</span> Yehova undirhwebeshile, ndarhwebesheka;
undibambile, wandeyisa, ndaba yintlekisa yonke imini; bonke bephela
bayandigculela.

<span id="an_20:8">20:8</span> Ngokuba ndithi, ndakuthetha, ndikhale,
ndidanduluke, ndithi, Lugonyamelo nobhuqo; ngokuba ilizwi likaYehova
laba sisingcikivo nesicukucezo kum yonke imini.

<span id="an_20:9">20:9</span> Ndithi ndakuthi, Andisayi kumkhankanya,
andisayi kuthetha egameni lakhe: kusuke entliziyweni yam kunge ngumlilo
otshayo, uvalelwe emathanjeni am; ndadinwa kukunyamezela, andaba nako.

<span id="an_20:10">20:10</span> Ngokuba ndivile intlebendwane
yabaninzi, bathi, Kukunxunguphala ngeenxa zonke. Xelani, simxele. Bonke
abafo ababexolelene nam balinde ukuqhwalela kwam; bathi, Mhlawumbi
angarhwebesheka, simeyise, simphindezele.

<span id="an_20:11">20:11</span> Ke uYehova unam, njengegorha
elingcangcazelisayo; ngenxa yoko baya kukhubeka abandisukelayo, abayi
koyisa; baya kudana kakhulu, ngokuba bengenzanga ngengqiqo; ihlazo labo
lingunaphakade, alinakulityalwa.

<span id="an_20:12">20:12</span> Wena ke, Yehova wemikhosi, ulicikidayo
ilungisa, uzibonayo izintso nentliziyo, mandiyibone impindezelo yakho
kubo; ngokuba ndikutyhilele ubambano lwam.

<span id="an_20:13">20:13</span> Vumani kuYehova, mdumiseni uYehova,
ngokuba ewuhlangule umphefumlo wehlwempu esandleni sabenzi bobubi.

<span id="an_20:14">20:14</span> Mawuqalekiswe umhla endazalwa ngawo;
umhla awandizala ngawo uma mawungasikeleleki.

<span id="an_20:15">20:15</span> Mayiqalekiswe indoda, eyamshumayeza
ubawo udaba lokuthi, Uzalelwe umntwana oyinkwenkwe; yamvuyisa kakhulu.

<span id="an_20:16">20:16</span> Loo ndoda mayibe njengemizi
awayibhukuqayo uYehova, akazohlwaya; mayive ukukhala kusasa, ive
kuhlatywa umkhosi emini enkulu;

<span id="an_20:17">20:17</span> ngokuba ingandibulalanga
kwasesizalweni, waza waba lingcwaba lam uma, isizalo sakhe sahlala
sindimithi.

<span id="an_20:18">20:18</span> Ibiyini na ukuba ndiphume esizalweni,
ukuze ndibone ukwaphuka nesingqala, iphele imihla yam kukudana?

<span id="an_21:1">21:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, ekuthumeni kokumkani onguZedekiya ooPashure unyana kaMalekiya,
noZefaniya unyana kaMahaseya, umbingeleli, kuye, ukuthi,

<span id="an_21:2">21:2</span> Khawusibuzele kuYehova, ngokuba
uNebhukadenetsare, ukumkani waseBhabheli, esilwa nathi; mhlawumbi
uYehova wosenzela ngokwemisebenzi yakhe yonke ebalulekileyo, enyuke
esuke kuthi yena.

<span id="an_21:3">21:3</span> Wathi uYeremiya kubo, Notsho kuZedekiya
ukuthi,

<span id="an_21:4">21:4</span> Utsho uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi,
Yabonani, ndiyazijika iimpahla zemfazwe ezisezandleni zenu, enilwa ngazo
nokumkani waseBhabheli, namaKaledi aningqingayo, ngaphandle kodonga,
ndizihlanganisele esazulwini salo mzi.

<span id="an_21:5">21:5</span> Ndiya kulwa nani mna ngesandla
esolukileyo, nangengalo ethe nkqi, ndinomsindo, ndinobushushu,
ndinoburhalarhume obukhulu.

<span id="an_21:6">21:6</span> Ndiya kubabetha abemi balo mzi, abantu
kwaneenkomo; baya kufa yindyikitya yokufa enkulu.

<span id="an_21:7">21:7</span> Emveni koko, utsho uYehova, ndomnikela
uZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda, nabakhonzi bakhe, nabantu abo baseleyo
kulo mzi, endyikityeni yokufa, nasekreleni, nasendlaleni; ndibanikele
esandleni sikaNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, nasesandleni
seentshaba zabo, nasesandleni sabawufunayo umphefumlo wabo; ababethe
ngohlangothi lwekrele; akayi kuba nanceba kubo, akayi kubaconga, akayi
kuba namfesane.

<span id="an_21:8">21:8</span> Ke kwaba bantu wothi, Utsho uYehova
ukuthi, Yabonani, ndibeka phambi kwenu indlela yobomi nendlela yokufa.

<span id="an_21:9">21:9</span> Othe wahlala kulo mzi uya kufa likrele,
nayindlala, nayindyikitya yokufa; ke yena othe waphuma, waphambela
kumaKaledi aningqingayo, uya kuphila umphefumlo wakhe, ube lixhoba kuye.

<span id="an_21:10">21:10</span> Ngokuba ubuso bam kulo mzi ndibumisele
ububi, andibumisele okulungileyo, utsho uYehova; uya kunikelwa esandleni
sokumkani waseBhaheli, awutshise ngomlilo.

<span id="an_21:11">21:11</span> Ke kwindlu yokumkani wakwaYuda wothi,
Yivani ilizwi likaYehova.

<span id="an_21:12">21:12</span> Ndlu kaDavide, utsho uYehova ukuthi,
Thethani amatyala imiso yonke, ophangiweyo nimhlangule esandleni
somcudisi, hleze ubushushu bam buphume njengomlilo, butshise, kungabikho
ucimayo ngenxa yobubi beentlondi zenu.

<span id="an_21:13">21:13</span> Yabonani, ndichasene nani, bemi
bentili, beliwa lehewu, utsho uYehova; nina bathi, Ngubani na oya kuhla
phezu kwethu? ngubani na oya kusingenela emakhaya?

<span id="an_21:14">21:14</span> Ke ndonivelela ngokwesiqhamo seentlondi
zenu, utsho uYehova; ndifake isikhuni ehlathini layo, udle umlilo
ngeenxa zonke kuyo.

<span id="an_22:1">22:1</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yihla uye endlwini
yokumkani wakwaYuda, uthethe khona eli lizwi, uthi,

<span id="an_22:2">22:2</span> Live ilizwi likaYehova, kumkani
wakwaYuda, uhleliyo etroneni kaDavide, wena, nabakhonzi bakho, nabantu
bakho abangenayo ngala masango.

<span id="an_22:3">22:3</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yenzani
okusesikweni nobulungisa, ophangiweyo nimhlangule esandleni somcudisi,
ningamxinzeleli phantsi; ningamgonyameli owasemzini nomhlolokazi
nenkedama; ningaphalazi gazi limsulwa kule ndawo.

<span id="an_22:4">22:4</span> Ngokuba xa nithe nalenza nokulenza eli
lizwi, bongena ngamasango ale ndlu ookumkani, abahlalela uDavide
etroneni yakhe, bekhwele ezinqwelweni nasemahasheni, yena, nabakhonzi
bakhe, nabantu bakhe.

<span id="an_22:5">22:5</span> Ke ukuba nithe anaweva la mazwi,
ndizifungile mna, utsho uYehova, ukuba le ndlu iya kuba linxuwa.

<span id="an_22:6">22:6</span> Ngokuba utshilo uYehova ngendlu yokumkani
wakwaYuda, ukuthi, UlelaseGiliyadi wena kum, uyincopho yeLebhanon;
inyaniso, ndiya kukwenza intlango, imizi engamiweyo.

<span id="an_22:7">22:7</span> Ndiya kukungcwalisela abonakalisi, elowo
abe neempahla zakhe, bagawule imisedare yakho enyuliweyo, bayiphose
emlilweni.

<span id="an_22:8">22:8</span> Kodlula kulo mzi iintlanga ezininzi,
bathi elowo kummelwane wakhe, Kungenxa yani na ukuba uYehova enjenje
kulo mzi mkhulu?

<span id="an_22:9">22:9</span> Bathi ke, Kungenxa yokuba bewushiyile
umnqophiso kaYehova uThixo wabo, baqubuda thixweni bambi, babakhonza.

<span id="an_22:10">22:10</span> Musani ukumlilela ofileyo,
ningahlunguzeli intloko ngenxa yakhe; lilani nilile ngomkileyo; ngokuba
akasayi kubuya abuye, alibone ilizwe lokuzalwa kwakhe.

<span id="an_22:11">22:11</span> Ngokuba utsho ukuthi uYehova, ngoShalum
unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, owaba ngukumkani esikhundleni
sikaYosiya uyise, owaphuma kule ndawo, Akasayikubuya abuyele apha;

<span id="an_22:12">22:12</span> ke uya kufela endaweni abamfudusele
kuyo, angabi sabuya alibone eli lizwe.

<span id="an_22:13">22:13</span> Yeha, oyakhayo indlu yakhe
kungengabulungisa, namagumbi akhe aphezulu kungengokusesikweni;
komkhonzisayo ummelwane wakhe ngelize, angamniki umvuzo wakhe;

<span id="an_22:14">22:14</span> othi, Ndiya kuzakhela indlu ebanzi,
namagumbi aphezulu anombilini; ayigqobhoze iifestile ezininzi, ayifulele
ngemisedare, ayiqabe ngembola!

<span id="an_22:15">22:15</span> Unobukumkani na, xa ushiyisela
ngokwakha ngemisedare? Uyihlo ubengadli, asele, enze okusesikweni
nobulungisa, yini na, kwaza kwalunga kuye?

<span id="an_22:16">22:16</span> Ubeligweba ityala losizana nolihlwempu;
kwaza kwalunga. Asikuko na oko ukundazi? utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_22:17">22:17</span> Ngokuba akabheke ntweni amehlo akho
nentliziyo yakho, kuphela akwinzuzo yakho nakwigazi labamsulwa, ukuze
liphalazwe; asekucudiseni nasekuvikiveni, ukuba wenze oko.

<span id="an_22:18">22:18</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova ngoYehoyakim
unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, ukuthi, Abayi kummbambazelela,
besithi, Yoo, mnakwethu! yoo, dade wethu! Abayi kummbambazelela,
besithi, Yoo, nkosi! Yoo, ndili yakhe!

<span id="an_22:19">22:19</span> Uya kungcwatywa ngokungcwatywa
kwe-esile, akrwiqilizwe, alahlwe kude namasango aseYerusalem.

<span id="an_22:20">22:20</span> Nyuka eLebhanon, ukhale; naseBhashan
khupha izwi lakho, ukhale eHabharim; ngokuba zaphukile zonke izithandane
zakho.

<span id="an_22:21">22:21</span> Ndathetha nawe uchulumachile; wathi
wena, Andiyi kuva. Yindlela yakho leyo kwasebuncinaneni bakho, ukuba
ungaliphulaphuli ilizwi lam.

<span id="an_22:22">22:22</span> Umoya uya kubadla bonke abalusi bakho,
zithinjwe izithandane zakho; wandule ukudana, inene, uve ihlazo, ngenxa
yezinto zakho ezimbi zonke.

<span id="an_22:23">22:23</span> Wena uhleliyo eLebhanon, uyakhelayo
emisedareni indlu yakho, hayi ukugcuma kwakho ekufikelweni kwakho
yinimba, kukuzibhijabhija, njengozalayo.

<span id="an_22:24">22:24</span> Ndihleli nje, utsho uYehova, ukuba
uKoniyahu unyana kaYehoyakim, ukumkani wakwaYuda, ebengumsesane,
wokutywina esandleni sam, sokunene, bendiya kumncothula nakhona;

<span id="an_22:25">22:25</span> ndikunikele esandleni sabawufunayo
umphefumlo wakho, nasesandleni sabo uboyikayo, nasesandleni
sikaNebhukadenetsare, ukumkani waseBhabheli, nasesandleni samaKaledi.

<span id="an_22:26">22:26</span> Ndonijulela kwelinye ilizwe, wena
nonyoko owakuzalayo, apho naningazalelwanga khona; nifele khona.

<span id="an_22:27">22:27</span> Ke lona ilizwe, abaya kuphakamisela
umphefumlo wabo kulo, ukuba babuyele kulo, abasayi kubuyela kulo.

<span id="an_22:28">22:28</span> Lo mfo uKoniyahu ngumphanda
odelekileyo, oza kuhlekezwa na? Uyimpahla engananziweyo na? Kungandawoni
na ukuba bajulelwe, yena nembewu yakhe, baphoswe ezweni abangalaziyo?

<span id="an_22:29">22:29</span> Lizwe, lizwe, lizwe, live ilizwi
likaYehova!

<span id="an_22:30">22:30</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Lo mfo mbaleleni
ekuthini akanabantwana, yindoda engenampumelelo emihleni yayo: ngokuba
akayi kuba nampumelelo umntu wasembewini yakhe, ohlala etroneni
kaDavide, esalawula kwaYuda.

<span id="an_23:1">23:1</span> Yeha ke, abalusi abatshabalalisa
bachithachithe umhlambi wedlelo lam! utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_23:2">23:2</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ngabalusi abo balusa abantu bam, ukuthi, Niwuchithachithile
umhlambi wam, nawubhebhetha, anawuvelela; yabonani, ndiya kunivelela
ngenxa yobubi beentlondi zenu; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_23:3">23:3</span> Ndiya kuwabutha mna amasalela omhlambi
wam emazweni onke endawagxothela kuwo, ndiwabuyisele emakriweni awo,
aqhame, ande;

<span id="an_23:4">23:4</span> ndiwamisele abalusi bawaluse, angabi
soyika, angaqhiphuki umbilini, kungabikho ulahlekayo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_23:5">23:5</span> Yabonani, iyeza imihla, utsho uYehova,
endiya kummisela uDavide iHlumelo elililungisa, libe nguKumkani
ongukumkani, enze yena ngengqiqo, enze okusesikweni nobulungisa
ehlabathini.

<span id="an_23:6">23:6</span> Ngemihla yakhe uya kusindiswa uYuda,
uSirayeli ahlale ekholosile; negama lakhe, aya kubizwa ngalo, leli
lokuba, UYehova-ububulungisa-bethu.

<span id="an_23:7">23:7</span> Ngako oko, yabonani, iyeza imihla, utsho
uYehova, abangasayi kuba sathi, Ehleli nje uYehova, owanyusa oonyana
bakaSirayeli ezweni lamaYiputa;

<span id="an_23:8">23:8</span> baya kuthi, Ehleli nje uYehova,
owayinyusayo, owayizisayo imbewu yendlu yakwaSirayeli, ivela ezweni
lasentla, nasemazweni onke endabagxothela kuwo; bahlale emhlabeni wabo.

<span id="an_23:9">23:9</span> Ngokusingisele kubaprofeti: Yaphukile
intliziyo yam phakathi kwam, athe fehlefehle onke amathambo am. Ndisuke
ndaba njengendoda enxilayo, njengomfo oweyiswe yiwayini; ngenxa
kaYehova, nangenxa yamazwi akhe angcwele.

<span id="an_23:10">23:10</span> Ngokuba ilizwe lizele ngabakrexezi,
ngokuba ngenxa yentshwabulo ilizwe lenza isijwili; omile amakriwa
entlango; usuke wambi umkhondo wabo, ubugorha babo abulunganga.

<span id="an_23:11">23:11</span> Ngokuba umprofeti kwanombingeleli
ngabenzi bobubi; ndizifumene nasendlwini yam izinto zabo ezimbi; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_23:12">23:12</span> Ngako oko indlela yabo kubo iya kuba
njengeendawo ezibuthelezi esithokothokweni; baya kuqhutywa, bawe khona;
ngokuba ndibazisela ububi, umnyaka wokuvelelwa kwabo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_23:13">23:13</span> Kubaprofeti bakwaSamari ndibone
ubufedelele; baprofeta ngoBhahali, belahlekisa abantu bam amaSirayeli.

<span id="an_23:14">23:14</span> Ke kubaprofeti baseYerusalem ndibone
into ebanga amanwele: ukukrexeza, nokuhamba ebuxokini, bomeleze izandla
zabenzi bobubi, kungabuyi mntu ebubini bakhe. Bonke bephela
banjengeSodom kum, nabemi bakhona banjengeGomora.

<span id="an_23:15">23:15</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova wemikhosi,
ngokusingisele kubaprofeti, ukuthi, Yabonani, ndobadlisa umhlonyane,
ndibaseze inyongo; ngokuba kubaprofeti baseYerusalem kuphuma
okungendawo, kuye kulo lonke ilizwe.

<span id="an_23:16">23:16</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi, Musani
ukuwaphulaphula amazwi abaprofeti abaniprofetelayo; banenzela into
engento, bathetha umbono wentliziyo yabo, ongaphumiyo emlonyeni
kaYehova.

<span id="an_23:17">23:17</span> Bamana ukuthi kwabandigibayo, UYehova
uthethile, niya kuba noxolo; nakubo bonke abahambayo ngobungqola
beentliziyo zabo bathi, Aniyi kuhlelwa bubi.

<span id="an_23:18">23:18</span> Ewe, ngubani na kubo ome elucweyweni
lukaYehova, walibona waliva ilizwi lakhe? Ngubani na olibazele indlebe
ilizwi lam, waliva?

<span id="an_23:19">23:19</span> Yabonani, umoya ovuthuzayo kaYehova,
uphume ubushushu, umoya ovuthuzayo osisaqhwithi, uya kuqhwithela
entlokweni yabangendawo.

<span id="an_23:20">23:20</span> Awuyi kubuya umsindo kaYehova, ade
awenze, ade ayimise iminkqangiyelo yentliziyo yakhe; ekupheleni kwemihla
nokugqala nikuqonde oko.

<span id="an_23:21">23:21</span> Andibathumanga abaprofeti abo, kugidime
bona; andithethanga kubo, kanti kuprofete bona.

<span id="an_23:22">23:22</span> Ukuba bebemi elucweyweni lwam, bange
bevakalise amazwi am kubantu bam, bababuyisa endleleni yabo embi,
nasebubini beentlondi zabo.

<span id="an_23:23">23:23</span> NdinguThixo wakufuphi na? utsho
uYehova, ndingabi nguThixo wakude na?

<span id="an_23:24">23:24</span> Wosithela na umntu ezintsithelweni,
ndingamboni na? utsho uYehova. Andizalise amazulu nehlabathi na mna?
utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_23:25">23:25</span> Ndikuvile abakuthethayo abaprofeti,
abaprofeta ubuxoki egameni lam, besithi, Ndiphuphile, ndiphuphile.

<span id="an_23:26">23:26</span> Koda kube nini na kuyile nto
entliziyweni yabaprofeti abaprofeta ubuxoki, abaprofeti benkohliso
yentliziyo yabo?

<span id="an_23:27">23:27</span> Bacinga ngokubalibazisa na abantu bam,
balilibale igama lam ngamaphupha abo, abawalawulayo elowo kummelwane
wakhe, njengoko ooyise balilibalayo igama lam ngoBhahali?

<span id="an_23:28">23:28</span> Umprofeti onephupha makalawule iphupha;
onelizwi lam makathethe ilizwi lam enyanisile. Yintoni na enomququ
nengqolowa? utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_23:29">23:29</span> Alinjengomlilo na ilizwi lam? utsho
uYehova; nanjengesando esihlekeza ingxondorha?

<span id="an_23:30">23:30</span> Ngako oko yabonani, ndichasene
nabaprofeti, utsho uYehova, abawebayo amazwi am elowo kummelwane wakhe.

<span id="an_23:31">23:31</span> Yabonani, ndichasene nabaprofeti, utsho
uYehova, abathabatha ulwimi lwabo, bathi, Utsho.

<span id="an_23:32">23:32</span> Yabonani, ndichasene nabaprofeti
abaprofeta amaphupha abuxoki, utsho uYehova, bawalawule, babalahlekise
abantu bam ngobuxoki babo, nangokugasa kwabo, endingabawiselanga
methetho, abangabancediyo nokubanceda aba bantu: utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_23:33">23:33</span> Ke kaloku, xa bathe bakubuza aba bantu,
nokuba ngumprofeti, nokuba ngumbingeleli, besithi, Siyintoni na isihlabo
sikaYehova? wobaxelela into esiyiyo isihlabo, sithi, Ndiya kunilahla,
utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_23:34">23:34</span> Umprofeti, nombingeleli, nabantu, abaya
kuthi, Isihlabo sikaYehova: ndiya kumvelela loo mntu nendlu yakhe.

<span id="an_23:35">23:35</span> Yitshoni elowo kummelwane wakhe, elowo
kumzalwana wakhe, ukuthi, Utheni na ukuphendula uYehova? utheni na
ukuthetha uYehova?

<span id="an_23:36">23:36</span> Ke sona isihlabo sikaYehova ze ningabi
sasikhankanya; ngokuba liya kuba sisihlabo kwindoda ilizwi layo,
niwajikile nje amazwi kaThixo ophilileyo, uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
wethu.

<span id="an_23:37">23:37</span> Wotsho kumprofeti ukuthi, Utheni na
uYehova ukukuphendula? utheni na uYehova ukuthetha?

<span id="an_23:38">23:38</span> Ke ukuba nithi, Isihlabo sikaYehova:
ngako oko utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ngenxa yokuthetha kwenu elo lizwi
lokuthi, Isihlabo sikaYehova, kanti ndithumele kuni ukuthi, Ize
ningatsho ukuthi, Isihlabo sikaYehova:

<span id="an_23:39">23:39</span> ngako oko, yabonani, ndiya kunilibala
mpela, ndinilahle ebusweni bam nina, nalo mzi ndaninikayo, nina
nooyihlo;

<span id="an_23:40">23:40</span> ndibeke phezu kwenu isingcikivo
esingunaphakade, ihlazo elingunaphakade, elingenakulityalwa.

<span id="an_24:1">24:1</span> UYehova wandibonisa, nanzo iingobozi
ezimbini zamakhiwane, zibekiwe phambi kwetempile kaYehova; emveni kokuba
uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli ebebathimbile ooYekoniya unyana
kaYehoyakim, ukumkani wakwaYuda, nabathetheli bakwaYuda, nengcibi,
nabakhandi, ebasusa eYerusalem, ebasa eBhabheli.

<span id="an_24:2">24:2</span> Enye ingobozi ibinamakhiwane alungileyo
kakhulu, enjengamakhiwane aziintlahlela ekuvuthweni; enye ingobozi
ibinamakhiwane amabi kunene, angenakudliwa ngobubi bawo.

<span id="an_24:3">24:3</span> Wathi ke uYehova kum, Ubona ntoni na,
Yeremiya? Ndathi, Amakhiwane; amakhiwane alungileyo, elunge kunene;
amabi emabi kunene, engenakudliwa ngobubi bawo.

<span id="an_24:4">24:4</span> Kwafika kum ilizwi likaYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_24:5">24:5</span> Utsho uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi,
Njengaloo makhiwane alungileyo, ndiya kwenjenjalo ukubakhangelela
okulungileyo abathinjiweyo bakwaYuda endibagxothileyo kule ndawo, baya
ezweni lamaKaledi.

<span id="an_24:6">24:6</span> Ndiya kulimisela okulungileyo iliso lam
kubo, ndibabuyisele kweli lizwe, ndibakhe, ndingabagungxuli; ndibatyale,
ndingabanyothuli.

<span id="an_24:7">24:7</span> Ndobanika intliziyo yokundazi, ukuba
ndinguYehova, babe ngabantu bam, ndibe nguThixo wabo; ngokuba baya
kubuyela kum nentliziyo yabo yonke.

<span id="an_24:8">24:8</span> Ke, njengamakhiwane amabi angenakudliwa
ngobubi, inene, utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ndiya kumenza abe njalo uZedekiya
ukumkani wamaYuda, nabathetheli bakhe, namasalela aseYerusalem aseleyo
kweli lizwe, nahleliyo ezweni lamaYiputa.

<span id="an_24:9">24:9</span> Ndiya kubanikela kwizikumkani zonke
zehlabathi, ukuba babe yinto yokunqakulisa, babe nobubi, babe
sisingcikivo, nomzekeliso, nento yentsini neyokutshabhiswa ezindaweni
zonke endibagxothela khona.

<span id="an_24:10">24:10</span> Ndolithuma phakathi kwabo ikrele,
nendlala, nendyikitya yokufa, bade bagqitywe, baphele emhlabeni
endawunika bona nooyise.

<span id="an_25:1">25:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya
ngokusingisele ebantwini bonke bakwaYuda, ngomnyaka wesine kaYehoyakim
unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, ongumnyaka wokuqala
kaNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli;

<span id="an_25:2">25:2</span> awalithethayo uYeremiya umprofeti kubantu
bonke bakwaYuda, nakubemi bonke baseYerusalem, esithi,

<span id="an_25:3">25:3</span> Kuthabathela kumnyaka weshumi
elinesithathu kaYosiya unyana ka-Amon, ukumkani wakwaYuda, kuzise kule
mini, le minyaka imashumi mabini anamithathu, bekufika ilizwi likaYehova
kum; bendithetha kuni, ndivuka kwakusasa ndithethe; anivanga noko.

<span id="an_25:4">25:4</span> UYehova wathumela kuni bonke abakhonzi
bakhe abaprofeti, ebathuma evuka kwakusasa; aniphulaphulanga noko,
anizithobanga iindlebe zenu ukuba nive.

<span id="an_25:5">25:5</span> Baye besithi, Khanibuye elowo endleleni
yakhe embi, nasebubini beentlondi zenu; nohlala emhlabeni awaninikayo
uYehova, nina nooyihlo, ngonaphakade kanaphakade;

<span id="an_25:6">25:6</span> ningalandeli thixo bambi, ningabakhonzi,
ningaqubudi kubo, ningandiqumbisi ngezenzo zezandla zenu, ukuze
ndingenzi nto imbi kuni.

<span id="an_25:7">25:7</span> Aniphulaphulanga kum, utsho uYehova;
ukuze nindiqumbise ngezenzo zezandla zenu, kuze kube kubi kuni.

<span id="an_25:8">25:8</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi,
Ngenxa enokuba ningawevanga amazwi am,

<span id="an_25:9">25:9</span> yabonani, ndithumela ukuba ndiyithabathe
yonke imizalwane yelasentla, utsho uYehova; ndithumela
kuNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, umkhonzi wam, ndiyizisele
phezu kweli lizwe, naphezu kwabemi balo, naphezu kwezi ntlanga zonke,
ngeenxa zonke; ndizisingele phantsi, ndizenze ummangaliso nomsondlo,
neempanza ezingunaphakade;

<span id="an_25:10">25:10</span> ndoliphelisa phakathi kwazo izwi
lemihlali nezwi lemivuyo, izwi lomyeni nezwi lomtshakazi, izwi lokusila
nokukhanya kwesibane.

<span id="an_25:11">25:11</span> Eli lizwe lonke liya kubharha, kube
senkangala; ezi ntlanga zimkhonze ukumkani waseBhabheli iminyaka
emashumi asixhenxe.

<span id="an_25:12">25:12</span> Kuya kuthi ke, xa izalisekileyo
iminyaka emashumi asixhenxe, ndimvelele ukumkani waseBhabheli nolo
luhlanga, ngenxa yobugwenxa babo; utsho uYehova. Nelizwe lamaKaledi
ndolenza kube senkangala ngonaphakade,

<span id="an_25:13">25:13</span> ndilizisele elo lizwe onke amazwi am
endawathetha ngalo: into yonke ebhaliweyo kule ncwadi, ayiprofetileyo
uYeremiya ngeentlanga zonke.

<span id="an_25:14">25:14</span> Ngokuba ziya kuwakhonzisa nawo
iintlanga ezininzi nookumkani abakhulu, ndiwavuze ngokwemisebenzi yawo,
nangokwezenzo zezandla zawo.

<span id="an_25:15">25:15</span> Ngokuba utshilo kum uYehova, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Thabatha le ndebe yewayini yobushushu esandleni sam,
useze ngayo iintlanga zonke, endikuthumela kuzo;

<span id="an_25:16">25:16</span> zisele, zihexe, zigeze, ngenxa yekrele
endilithumela phakathi kwazo.

<span id="an_25:17">25:17</span> Ndayithabatha ke indebe esandleni
sikaYehova, ndaziseza zonke iintlanga, awandithumela kuzo uYehova:

<span id="an_25:18">25:18</span> iYerusalem, nemizi yakwaYuda,
nookumkani bayo, nabathetheli bayo, ukuba benziwe iimpanza,
nommangaliso, nomsondlo, nentshabhiso, njengoko kunjalo namhla;

<span id="an_25:19">25:19</span> uFaro ukumkani waseYiputa, nabakhonzi
bakhe, nabathetheli bakhe, nabantu bakhe bonke;

<span id="an_25:20">25:20</span> nomxukuxela wonke, nookumkani bonke
belizwe lakwaUtse, nookumkani bonke belizwe lamaFilisti, neAshkelon,
neGaza, ne-Ekron, namasalela aseAshdode;

<span id="an_25:21">25:21</span> uEdom, noMowabhi, noonyana baka-Amon;

<span id="an_25:22">25:22</span> nookumkani bonke baseTire, nookumkani
bonke baseTsidon, nookumkani bonke besiqhithi esiphesheya kolwandle;

<span id="an_25:23">25:23</span> uDedan, noTema, noBhizi,
noonquthula-iinwele bonke;

<span id="an_25:24">25:24</span> nookumkani bonke bama-Arabhi,
nookumkani bonke bomxukuxela omiyo entlango;

<span id="an_25:25">25:25</span> nookumkani bonke bamaZimri, nookumkani
bonke bamaElam, nookumkani bonke bamaMedi;

<span id="an_25:26">25:26</span> nookumkani bonke belasentla, abakufuphi
nabakude, elowo nomzalwana wakhe, nezikumkani zonke zehlabathi eziphezu
komhlaba; asele emva kwabo ukumkani waseSheshaki.

<span id="an_25:27">25:27</span> Ngoko ke wothi kubo, Utsho uYehova
wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Selani ninxile, nihlanze, niwe,
ningavuki, ngenxa yekrele endilithumela phakathi kwenu.

<span id="an_25:28">25:28</span> Kothi, xa bathe abavuma ukuyithabatha
indebe esandleni sakho ukuba basele, uthi kubo, Utsho uYehova wemikhosi
ukuthi, Niya kusela ngenene.

<span id="an_25:29">25:29</span> Ngokuba, yabonani, ndiqalela emzini
obizwa ngegama lam, ukuhlisa ububi; ningaba msulwa nide nibe msulwa na
ke nina? Aniyi kuba msulwa; ngokuba ikrele ndilibizela bonke abemi
behlabathi; utsho uYehova wemikhosi.

<span id="an_25:30">25:30</span> Ke wena uze ubaprofetele loo mazwi
onke, uthi kubo, UYehova uya kubharhula phezulu, alikhuphe ilizwi lakhe
ekhayeni lakhe eliyingcwele; uya kubharhula alibharhulele ikriwa lakhe;
uya kubahlabela amayeyeye, njengabaxovuli beediliya, bonke abemi
behlabathi.

<span id="an_25:31">25:31</span> Ingxolo iya kufika esiphelweni
sehlabathi, ngokuba uYehova ubambene neentlanga; uya kugweba phakathi
kwenyama yonke; abangendawo ubanikela ekreleni; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_25:32">25:32</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi,
Yabonani, ububi buya kuphuma eluhlangeni, buye eluhlangeni, umoya
omkhulu ovuthuzayo uvuke esinqeni sehlabathi.

<span id="an_25:33">25:33</span> Ababuleweyo nguYehova ngaloo mini,
bathabathele ekupheleni kwehlabathi, bese ekupheleni kwehlabathi,
bangambanjazelelwa, bangahlanganiswa, bangangcwatywa; baya kuba
ngumgquba phezu komhlaba.

<span id="an_25:34">25:34</span> Bhombolozani, balusi, nikhale;
nizigalele ngothuthu, zingangamsha zomhlambi; ngokuba izalisekile imihla
yenu yokuba nisikwe. Ndiya kuniphangalalisa, niwe njengesitya
esinqwenelekayo;

<span id="an_25:35">25:35</span> iphele intsabo kubalusi, nokusinda
kwiingangamsha zomhlambi.

<span id="an_25:36">25:36</span> Yivani ukukhala kwabalusi,
nokubhomboloza kweengangamsha zomhlambi; ngokuba uYehova uyalibhuqa
idlelo labo.

<span id="an_25:37">25:37</span> Athe shwaka amakriwa oxolo, ngenxa
yokuvutha komsindo kaYehova.

<span id="an_25:38">25:38</span> Ulushiyile njengengonyama entsha udada
lwakhe; ngokuba kuthe kwaba senkangala kulo ilizwe labo ngenxa yekrele
elidlavulayo, nangenxa yokuvutha komsindo wakhe.

<span id="an_26:1">26:1</span> Ekuqalekeni kobukumkani bukaYehoyakim
unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, kwafika eli lizwi, liphuma
kuYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_26:2">26:2</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yima entendelezweni
yendlu kaYehova, uthethe kuyo yonke imizi yakwaYuda, eza kuqubuda
endlwini kaYehova, onke amazwi endikuwisela umthetho wokuba uwathethe
kubo; ungaphunguli zwi kuwo.

<span id="an_26:3">26:3</span> Mhlawumbi baya kuva, babuye elowo
endleleni yakhe embi, ndizohlwaye ngenxa yobubi endicinga ukubenza kubo,
ngenxa yobubi beentlondi zabo.

<span id="an_26:4">26:4</span> Uze uthi kubo, Utsho uYehova ukuthi,
Ukuba nithe anandiphulaphula, nihambe ngomyalelo wam, endiwubeke phambi
kwenu,

<span id="an_26:5">26:5</span> anawaphulaphula amazwi abakhonzi bam
abaprofeti, endibathumela kuni, ndibathuma ndivuka kusasa, anaweva:

<span id="an_26:6">26:6</span> ndoyenza le ndlu ibe njengeShilo,
ndiwenze lo mzi ube yinto yokutshabhiswa ezintlangeni zonke zehlabathi.

<span id="an_26:7">26:7</span> Babemva ke uYeremiya ababingeleli,
nabaprofeti, nabantu bonke, ethetha la mazwi endlwini kaYehova.

<span id="an_26:8">26:8</span> Ke kaloku, ekugqibeni kukaYeremiya konke
abewiselwe umthetho nguYehova ukuba akuthethe kubantu bonke, bambamba
ababingeleli, nabaprofeti, nabantu bonke, bathi, Inene, uya kufa.

<span id="an_26:9">26:9</span> Yini na ukuba uprofete egameni
likaYehova, usithi, Le ndlu iya kuba njengeShilo, lo mzi ube linxuwa,
ungabi nabemi? Babizelwa ndawonye bonke abantu kuYeremiya endlwini
kaYehova.

<span id="an_26:10">26:10</span> Baweva abathetheli bakwaYuda la mazwi,
benyuka bemka endlwini yokumkani, baya endlwini kaYehova, bahlala
phantsi ekungeneni kwesango elitsha likaYehova,

<span id="an_26:11">26:11</span> Ababingeleli nabaprofeti bathetha
kubathetheli nakubantu bonke, besithi, Le ndoda ifanelwe sisigwebo
sokufa, ngokuba iprofete ngalo mzi, njengoko nikuvileyo ngeendlebe zenu.

<span id="an_26:12">26:12</span> Wathetha uYeremiya kubathetheli bonke
nakubantu bonke, esithi, UYehova undithume ukuba ndiprofete ngale ndlu
nangalo mzi onke amazwi eniwavileyo.

<span id="an_26:13">26:13</span> Kaloku ke, lungisani iindlela zenu
neentlondi zenu, niliphulaphule ilizwi likaYehova uThixo wenu;
wozohlwaya uYehova ngenxa yobubi abuthethileyo ngani.

<span id="an_26:14">26:14</span> Ke mna, yabonani, ndisesandleni senu;
yenzani kum njengoko kulungileyo, kuthe tye, emehlweni enu.

<span id="an_26:15">26:15</span> Kodwa ke yazini nazi oku: ukuba nithe
nandibulala, inene, nobeka igazi elimsulwa phezu kwenu, naphezu kwalo
mzi, naphezu kwabemi bawo; ngokuba, inyaniso, uYehova undithumele kuni,
ukuba ndiwathethe la mazwi onke ezindlebeni zenu.

<span id="an_26:16">26:16</span> Bathi ke abathetheli nabantu bonke
kubabingeleli nakubaprofeti, Le ndoda ayifanelwe sisigwebo sokufa,
ngokuba ithethe kuthi egameni likaYehova uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_26:17">26:17</span> Kwesuka kwema amadoda kumadoda amakhulu
elo zwe, athetha kulo lonke ibandla labantu, athi,

<span id="an_26:18">26:18</span> UMika waseMoreshete waprofeta ngemihla
kaHezekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda, wathetha kubantu bonke bakwaYuda, esithi,
Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi, IZiyon iya kulinywa ibe yintsimi,
neYerusalem ibe yimiwewe, nentaba yendlu le ibe yimimango enehlathi.

<span id="an_26:19">26:19</span> Bambulala na ke uHezekiya ukumkani
wakwaYuda namaYuda onke? Akoyikanga uYehova na, wambongoza uYehova, waza
uYehova wazohlwaya ngenxa yobubi abebuthethile ngabo? Thina ke, senze na
ububi obukhulu kwimiphefumlo yethu?

<span id="an_26:20">26:20</span> Kwaye kananjalo kuprofeta egameni
likaYehova indoda engu-Uriya unyana kaShemaya, waseKiriyati-yeharim;
waprofeta ngalo mzi nangeli lizwe, ngokwamazwi onke kaYeremiya.

<span id="an_26:21">26:21</span> Waweva ke ukumkani uYehoyakim,
namagorha akhe onke, nabathetheli bonke, amazwi akhe; ukumkani wafuna
ukumbulala. Weva u-Uriya, woyika, wasaba waya eYiputa.

<span id="an_26:22">26:22</span> Ukumkani uYehoyakim wathumela amadoda
eYiputa, uElinatan unyana ka-Akebhore, enamadoda athile, baya eYiputa.

<span id="an_26:23">26:23</span> Bamrhola u-Uriya eYiputa, bamzisa
kukumkani uYehoyakim; wambulala ngekrele, wasiphosa isidumbu sakhe
emangcwabeni oluntu.

<span id="an_26:24">26:24</span> Kodwa isandla sika-Ahikam unyana
kaShafan besinoYeremiya, ukuba anganikelwa esandleni sabantu ukuba
abulawe.

<span id="an_27:1">27:1</span> Ekuqalekeni kobukumkani bukaZedekiya
unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, kwafika eli lizwi kuYeremiya,
liphuma kuYehova, lisithi:

<span id="an_27:2">27:2</span> Utshilo uYehova kum ukuthi, Zenzele
izitropu needyokhwe, uzifake entanyeni yakho.

<span id="an_27:3">27:3</span> Wozithumela kukumkani wakwaEdom,
nakukumkani wakwaMowabhi, nakukumkani woonyana baka-Amon, nakukumkani
waseTire, nakukumkani waseTsidon, ngesandla sabathunywa abeze eYerusalem
kuZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda;

<span id="an_27:4">27:4</span> ubawisele umthetho wokuba bathi
ezinkosini zabo, Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi,
Yitshoni ezinkosini zenu ukuthi,

<span id="an_27:5">27:5</span> Mna ndilenzile ihlabathi, umntu lo,
neenkomo eziphezu kwehlabathi, ngamandla am amakhulu, nangengalo yam
eyolukileyo; ndalinika lowo kuthe tye emehlweni am ukuba ndilinike yena.

<span id="an_27:6">27:6</span> Kaloku ke mna ndiwanikele onke la mazwe
esandleni sikaNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, umkhonzi wam,
kwanamarhamncwa asendle ndiwanikele kuye ukuba amkhonze.

<span id="an_27:7">27:7</span> Ziya kumkhonza zonke iintlanga, yena,
nonyana wakhe, nonyana wonyana wakhe, kude kufike ixesha lelakhe ilizwe;
zimkhonze ke naye iintlanga ezininzi nookumkani abakhulu.

<span id="an_27:8">27:8</span> Kuya kuthi, uhlanga nobukumkani obungayi
kumhonza uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, obungayifakiyo intamo
yabo edyokhweni yokumkani waseBhabheli, ndiluvelele olo luhlanga
ngekrele, nangendlala, nangendyikitya yokufa, utsho uYehova, ndide
ndibagqibe ngesandla sakhe.

<span id="an_27:9">27:9</span> Musani ke nina ukubaphulaphula abaprofeti
benu, nabavumisi benu, namaphupha enu, namatola enu, nabakhafuli benu;
bona abo bathi kuni, Aniyi kumkhonza ukumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_27:10">27:10</span> Ngokuba baniprofetela ubuxoki, ukuze
ndinikhwelelise kude nomhlaba wenu, ndinigxothe, nitshabalale.

<span id="an_27:11">27:11</span> Ke lona uhlanga oluya kuyingenisa
intamo yalo edyokhweni yokumkani waseBhabheli, lumkhonze, ndoluyeka
emhlabeni walo, luwusebenze, luhlale kuwo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_27:12">27:12</span> NakuZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda
ndathetha ngokwaloo mazwi onke, ndathi, Zingeniseni iintamo zenu
edyokhweni yokumkani waseBhabheli, nikhonze yena nabantu bakhe, niphile.

<span id="an_27:13">27:13</span> Yini na ukuba ufe, wena nabantu bakho,
likrele, nayindlala, nayindyikitya yokufa, njengoko akuthethileyo
uYehova ngohlanga olungayi kumkhonza ukumkani waseBhabheli?

<span id="an_27:14">27:14</span> Musani ukuwaphulaphula amazwi
abaprofeti abathetha kuni, besithi, Aniyi kumkhonza ukumkani
waseBhabheli; ngokuba baniprofetela ubuxoki.

<span id="an_27:15">27:15</span> Ngokuba andibathumanga, utsho uYehova;
bona baprofeta ubuxoki egameni lam, ukuze ndinigxothe, nitshabalale,
ninanabaprofeti abo baniprofetelayo.

<span id="an_27:16">27:16</span> Ndathetha kubabingeleli nakwaba bantu
bonke, ndisithi, Utshilo uYehova ukuthi, Musani ukuwaphulaphula amazwi
abaprofeti benu abaniprofetelayo, besithi, Yabona, impahla yendlu
kaYehova iya kubehle ibuyiswe eBhabheli; ngokuba baniprofetela ubuxoki.

<span id="an_27:17">27:17</span> Musani ukubaphulaphula; mkhonzeni
ukumkani waseBhabheli, niphile; yini na ukuba ube linxuwa lo mzi?

<span id="an_27:18">27:18</span> Ke ukuba bangabaprofeti, ke ukuba likho
ilizwi likaYehova kubo, mabambongoze uYehova wemikhosi, ukuze impahla
eseleyo endlwini kaYehova, nasendlwini yokumkani wakwaYuda,
naseYerusalem, ingayi eBhabheli.

<span id="an_27:19">27:19</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova wemikhosi,
ngokusingisele kuzo iintsika, nangalo ulwandle, nangazo iinqwelwana,
nangawo amasalela empahla eseleyo kulo mzi,

<span id="an_27:20">27:20</span> engathatyathwanga nguNebhukadenetsare
ukumkani waseBhabheli, ekumfuduseni kwakhe uYekoniya, unyana
kaYehoyakim, ukumkani wakwaYuda, eYerusalem, ukumsa eBhabheli,
enabanumzana bonke bakwaYuda neYerusalem;

<span id="an_27:21">27:21</span> ewe, utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
wamaSirayeli, ngempahla eseleyo endlwini kaYehova, nasendlwini yokumkani
wakwaYuda, naseYerusalem, ukuthi,

<span id="an_27:22">27:22</span> Iya kusiwa eBhabheli ibe khona, ide ibe
yimini yokuyivelela kwam, utsho uYehova; ndiyinyuse, ndiyibuyisele kule
ndawo.

<span id="an_28:1">28:1</span> Ke kaloku, kwathi ngaloo mnyaka,
ekuqalekeni kobukumkani bukaZedekiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, ngomnyaka
wesine, ngenyanga yesihlanu, wathetha kum uHananiya unyana ka-Azure,
umprofeti waseGibheyon, endlwini kaYehova, emehlweni ababingeleli
nabantu bonke, esithi,

<span id="an_28:2">28:2</span> Utshilo uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Ndiyayaphula idyokhwe yokumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_28:3">28:3</span> Kwangale minyaka mibini izalisekileyo,
ndiya kuyibuyisela kule ndawo yonke impahla yendlu kaYehova,
awayithabathayo kuloo ndawo uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli,
wayisa eBhabheli.

<span id="an_28:4">28:4</span> Ndiya kubabuyisela kule ndawo oYekoniya
unyana kaYehoyakim, ukumkani wakwaYuda, nabafudusiweyo bonke bakwaYuda,
abaye eBhabheli, utsho uYehova; ngokuba ndiya kuyaphula idyokhwe
yokumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_28:5">28:5</span> Wathi uYeremiya umprofeti kuHananiya
umprofeti, emehlweni ababingeleli, nasemehlweni abantu bonke abemiyo
endlwini kaYehova:

<span id="an_28:6">28:6</span> wathi uYeremiya umprofeti, Amen,
makenjenjalo uYehova. Makawamise uYehova amazwi akho owaprofetele ukuba
ayibuyise impahla yendlu kaYehova, nabafudusiweyo bonke eBhabheli, beze
kule ndawo.

<span id="an_28:7">28:7</span> Khawuve eli lizwi ndilithethayo
ezindlebeni zakho, nasezindlebeni zabantu bonke.

<span id="an_28:8">28:8</span> Abaprofeti ababengaphambili kum
nangaphambili kwakho kwasephakadeni, baprofeta imfazwe, nobubi,
nendyikitya yokufa, besingisele kumazwe amaninzi nangezikumkani
ezikhulu.

<span id="an_28:9">28:9</span> Umprofeti lowo uprofeta uxolo, uya
kwaziwa ukuba ungumprofeti othunyiweyo nguYehova okunene, ekwenzekeni
kwelo lizwi lomprofeti lowo.

<span id="an_28:10">28:10</span> Ke kaloku uHananiya umprofeti
wayithabatha idyokhwe entanyeni kaYeremiya umprofeti, wayaphula.

<span id="an_28:11">28:11</span> Wathetha uHananiya emehlweni abantu
bonke, esithi, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ndiya kwenjenje ukuyaphula idyokhwe
kaNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, ngale minyaka mibini iza
kuzaliseka, ezintanyeni zeentlanga zonke. Wemka ke uYeremiya umprofeti,
wahamba indlela yakhe.

<span id="an_28:12">28:12</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya
emva kokuyaphula kukaHananiya umprofeti idyokhwe entanyeni kaYeremiya
umprofeti, lisithi,

<span id="an_28:13">28:13</span> Yiya uthethe kuHananiya, uthi, Utsho
uYehova ukuthi, Uzaphule iidyokhwe zomthi, ke yenza iidyokhwe zesinyithi
esikhundleni sazo.

<span id="an_28:14">28:14</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Ndibeke idyokhwe yesinyithi ezintanyeni zezo ntlanga
zonke, ukuze zimkhonze uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli; ziya
kumkhonza ke; kwanamaramncwa asendle ndiwanikele kuye.

<span id="an_28:15">28:15</span> Wathi uYeremiya umprofeti kuHananiya
umprofeti, Khawuve, Hananiya; uYehova akakuthumanga; wena aba bantu
ubakholosisa ngobuxoki.

<span id="an_28:16">28:16</span> Ngako oko, utsho uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, ndiva kukugxotha ebusweni bomhlaba; uya kufa nonyakanje, ngokuba
uthethe elokukreqa kuYehova.

<span id="an_28:17">28:17</span> Wafa ke uHananiya umprofeti ngaloo
mnyaka, ngenyanga yesixhenxe.

<span id="an_29:1">29:1</span> Ngawo la amazwi encwadi awayithumelayo
uYeremiya umprofeti, eseYerusalem, kumasalela amadoda amakhulu
afudusiweyo, nakubabingeleli, nakubaprofeti, nakubantu bonke,
awayebafudusile eYerusalem uNebhukadenetsare, wabasa eBhabheli

<span id="an_29:2">29:2</span> (emva kokuphuma kukaYekoniya ukumkani,
nenkosikazi, namagosa, nabathetheli bakwaYuda neYerusalem, neengcibi,
nabakhandi eYerusalem);

<span id="an_29:3">29:3</span> awayithumelayo ngesandla sikaElasa unyana
kaShafan, noGemariya unyana kaHilekiya (awabathumelayo uZedekiya
ukumkani wakwaYuda kuNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli eBhabheli),
isithi:

<span id="an_29:4">29:4</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, kwabafudusiweyo bonke, endibafuduse eYerusalem, ukuba basiwe
eBhabheli, ukuthi,

<span id="an_29:5">29:5</span> Yakhani izindlu, nihlale kuzo; tyalani
imiyezo, nidle iziqhamo zayo.

<span id="an_29:6">29:6</span> Zekani abafazi, nizale oonyana neentombi,
nibazekele abafazi oonyana benu, iintombi zenu nizendisele kumadoda,
zizale oonyana neentombi, nande khona, ninganciphi.

<span id="an_29:7">29:7</span> Nize nizamele uxolo lomzi endinifudusele
kuwo, niwuthandazele kuYehova; ngokuba niya kuba noxolo ngoxolo lwawo.

<span id="an_29:8">29:8</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Mabanganilukuhli abaprofeti benu abaphakathi kwenu,
kwanabavumisi benu, ningawaphulaphuli amaphupha enu eniwaphuphayo.

<span id="an_29:9">29:9</span> Ngokuba baniprofetela ubuxoki egameni
lam; andibathumanga; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_29:10">29:10</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Xenikweni
iBhabheli izaliselwe iminyaka emashumi asixhenxe, ndiya kunivelela,
ndilimise kuni ilizwi lam elilungileyo, lokunibuyisela kule ndawo.

<span id="an_29:11">29:11</span> Ngokuba ndiyazazi iingcinga
endizicingayo ngani, utsho uYehova: iingcinga zoxolo, ezingezizo
ezobubi; ukuba ndininike ikamva nethemba.

<span id="an_29:12">29:12</span> Niya kundinqula, nize nithandaze kum,
ndiniphulaphule.

<span id="an_29:13">29:13</span> Niya kundifuna, nindifumane, xa nithe
nandifuna ngentliziyo yenu yonke;

<span id="an_29:14">29:14</span> ndifumaneke kuni; utsho uYehova. Ndiya
kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa kwenu, ndinibuthe ezintlangeni zonke,
nasezindaweni zonke endanigxothela kuzo, utsho uYehova;

<span id="an_29:15">29:15</span> ndinibuyisele endaweni endanifudusa
kuyo, xa nithi, UYehova usivelisele abaprofeti eBhabheli.

<span id="an_29:16">29:16</span> Inene, utsho uYehova ngokusingisele
kukumkani ohleli etroneni kaDavide, nakubantu bonke abahleli kulo mzi,
abazalwana benu, abangaphumanga baye nani ekufudusweni:

<span id="an_29:17">29:17</span> utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi,
Yabonani, ndithuma phakathi kwabo ikrele, nendlala, nendyikitya yokufa,
ndibenze babe njengamakhiwane akruqulayo, angenakudliwa ngokuba mabi
kwawo.

<span id="an_29:18">29:18</span> Ndiya kubasukela ngekrele nangendlala
nangendyikitya yokufa, ndibanikele ukuba babe yinto yokunqakulisa
kwizikumkani zonke zehlabathi, babe yintshwabulo, nommangaliso,
nomsondlo, nesingcikivo, ezintlangeni zonke endabagxothela kuzo;

<span id="an_29:19">29:19</span> ngethuba lokuba bengawaphulaphulanga
amazwi am, utsho uYehova, endawathumela kuni ngabakhonzi bam abaprofeti,
ndibathuma ndivuka kusasa; anivanga noko; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_29:20">29:20</span> Liveni ke ilizwi likaYehova, nina nonke
bafudusiweyo, ndabasusayo eYerusalem, baya eBhabheli.

<span id="an_29:21">29:21</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ngokusingisele kuAhabhi unyana kaKolaya, nakuZedekiya unyana
kaMahaseya, abaniprofetela ubuxoki egameni lam, ukuthi, Yabonani,
ndibanikela esandleni sikaNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli,
ababulale emehlweni enu;

<span id="an_29:22">29:22</span> kuzekelwe kubo ukutshabhisa
ngabafudusiweyo bonke bakwaYuda abaseBhabheli, kuthiwe, UYehova
makakwenze ube njengoZedekiya, nanjengoAhabhi, awabachanabayo emlilweni
ukumkani waseBhabheli;

<span id="an_29:23">29:23</span> ngenxa yokuba benze ubudenge
kwaSirayeli, babakrexeza abafazi babamelwane babo, bathetha amazwi
obuxoki egameni lam, endingabawiselanga methetho ngawo. Ndiyazi mna,
ndilingqina, utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_29:24">29:24</span> Ngokusingisele kuShemaya waseNehelam
wothetha, uthi,

<span id="an_29:25">29:25</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Ngenxa enokuba wena uthumele incwadi egameni lakho
kubantu bonke abaseYerusalem, nakuZefaniya unyana kaMahaseya,
umbingeleli, nakubabingeleli bonke, usithi,

<span id="an_29:26">29:26</span> UYehova ukwenze umbingeleli
esikhundleni sikaYoyada umbingeleli, ukuze kubekho abaveleli endlwini
kaYehova ngenxa kabani wonke obhudayo, ozenza umprofeti, ukuba umfake
esitokisini nasentanjeni.

<span id="an_29:27">29:27</span> Yini na ngoku, ukuba ungamkhalimeli
uYeremiya waseAnatoti, ozenza umprofeti kuni?

<span id="an_29:28">29:28</span> Ngokuba ngenxa yoko uthumele kuthi
eBhabheli, esithi, Inde le nto; yakhani izindlu, nihlale kuzo; tyalani
imiyezo, nidle iziqhamo zayo.

<span id="an_29:29">29:29</span> UZefaniya umbingeleli wayilesa loo
ncwadi ezindlebeni zikaYeremiya umprofeti.

<span id="an_29:30">29:30</span> Kwafika ke ilizwi likaYehova
kuYeremiya, lisithi.

<span id="an_29:31">29:31</span> Thumela kubo bonke abafudusiweyo, uthi,
Utsho uYehova ngokusingisele kuShemaya waseNehelam, ukuthi, Ngenxa
enokuba uShemaya eniprofetele, ndingamthumanga mna, wanikholosisa
ngobuxoki:

<span id="an_29:32">29:32</span> ngako oko utsho uYehova ukuthi,
Yabonani, ndiyamvelela uShemaya waseNehelam nembewu yakhe; akayi kuba
namntu uhleliyo phakathi kwaba bantu; angayi kubona okulungileyo
endikwenzela abantu bam, utsho uYehova; ngokuba ethethe elokukreqa
kuYehova.

<span id="an_30:1">30:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, lalisithi,

<span id="an_30:2">30:2</span> Utsho uYehova, uThixo wakwaSirayeli,
ukuthi, Wabhale encwadini onke amazwi endiwathethileyo kuwe;

<span id="an_30:3">30:3</span> ngokuba, uyabona, kuza imihla, utsho
uYehova, endiya kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa kwabantu bam amaSirayeli namaYuda,
utsho uYehova; ndibabuyisele ezweni endalinika ooyise, ukuba balime.

<span id="an_30:4">30:4</span> Ngawo la ke amazwi, awawathethayo uYehova
ngokusingisele kumaSirayeli, nakumaYuda.

<span id="an_30:5">30:5</span> Utshilo ke uYehova ukuthi, Sive izwi
eligubhisayo; lelinkwantyisayo, asililo eloxolo.

<span id="an_30:6">30:6</span> Khanibuzise nikhangele, ukuba indoda
yakha yamitha na? Yini na ukuba ndibone abafo bonke, izandla zabo
zisemanqeni abo njengomfazi ozalayo, ubuso bonke busuke baluthuthu?

<span id="an_30:7">30:7</span> Athi ke ukuba mkhulu loo mhla! Akukho
unjengawo; lixesha lembandezelo kuYakobi; ke uya kusindiswa kuyo.

<span id="an_30:8">30:8</span> Kothi ke ngaloo mhla, utsho uYehova
wemikhosi, ndiyaphule idyokhwe yakhe entanyeni yakho, ndiziqhawule
izitropu zakho, bangabi samkhonzisa abasemzini;

<span id="an_30:9">30:9</span> bakhonze uYehova uThixo wabo, noDavide
ukumkani wabo, endiya kubavelisela yena.

<span id="an_30:10">30:10</span> Ke wena musa ukoyika, mkhonzi wam
Yakobi, utsho uYehova, ungaqhiphuki umbilini, Sirayeli; ngokuba,
uyabona, ndiya kukusindisa usekude, nembewu yakho ezweni ethinjelwe
kulo, abuye uYakobi, azole, onwabe, angagubhi.

<span id="an_30:11">30:11</span> Ngokuba ndinawe, utsho uYehova, ukuze
ndikusindise; ngokuba ndiya kuzigqibela kuphele iintlanga zonke
endakuphangalalisela kuzo; kodwa andiyi kukugqibela kuphele;
ndokuthethisa ngokusesikweni, ndingathi umsulwa kwakanye.

<span id="an_30:12">30:12</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ukwaphuka
kwakho asikuko nokuba kuyabulala, libuhlungu inxeba lakho.

<span id="an_30:13">30:13</span> Akukho ugweba ityala lakho, upholisa
inxeba; akunaye okubophayo.

<span id="an_30:14">30:14</span> Zonke izithandane zakho zikulibele,
azikukhathalele; ngokuba ndikubethile ngobetho lotshaba, ngentethiso
enobujorha, ngenxa yobuninzi bobugwenxa bakho, ngenxa yokuba zininzi
izono zakho.

<span id="an_30:15">30:15</span> Ukhalelani na ngenxa yokwaphuka kwakho?
Asikuko nokuba uyabulala umvandedwa wakho! Ndizenzile ezo nto kuwe
ngenxa yobuninzi bobugwenxa bakho, nangenxa yokuba zininzi izono zakho.

<span id="an_30:16">30:16</span> Ngako oko bonke abakudlayo baya
kudliwa, nababandezeli bakho bonke bephela baya kuthinjwa, nabadywidi
bakho badywidwe nabaphangi bakho bonke ndibanikele ekuphangweni.

<span id="an_30:17">30:17</span> Ngokuba ndiya kukubopha, ndiyipholise
imivumbo yakho, utsho uYehova; ngokokuba bathi unguGxothiwe, uyiZiyon
engakhathalelwe bani.

<span id="an_30:18">30:18</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabona ndiya
kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa kweentente zikaYakobi, ndibe nemfesane ngenxa
yeminquba yakhe; umzi wakhelwe emmangweni wawo, luhlalwe uxande olude
ngokwesiko lalo.

<span id="an_30:19">30:19</span> Wophuma kuzo umbulelo nezwi
labaqambayo; ndibandise, bangabi mbalwa; ndibazukise, banganciphi.

<span id="an_30:20">30:20</span> Oonyana babo boba njengokwamandulo,
lizimaseke phambi kwam ibandla labo, ndibavelele bonke abaxini babo.

<span id="an_30:21">30:21</span> Ingangamsha yabo iya kuvela kubo,
umlawuli wabo aphume kwaphakathi kwabo; ndimsondeze, afike kum, ngokuba
ngubani na omele intliziyo yakhe, ukuba afike kum? utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_30:22">30:22</span> Niya kuba ngabantu bam, mna ndibe
nguThixo wenu.

<span id="an_30:23">30:23</span> Nango umoya kaYehova ovuthuzayo; nabo
buphuma ubushushu; umoya ovuthuzayo, okhukulisayo, uya kuqhwithela
entlokweni yabangendawo.

<span id="an_30:24">30:24</span> Akuyi kubuya ukuvutha komsindo
kaYehova, ade ayenze, ade ayimise iminkqangiyelo yentliziyo yakhe;
ekupheleni kwemihla niya kukuqonda oko.

<span id="an_31:1">31:1</span> Ngelo xesha, utsho uYehova, ndiya kuba
nguThixo kwimizalwane yonke yakwaSirayeli, yona ibe ngabantu bam.

<span id="an_31:2">31:2</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Bababalwa entlango
abantu abasindileyo ekreleni; ndoya ndiwaphumze amaSirayeli.

<span id="an_31:3">31:3</span> UYehova ubonakele kum kwakude, wathi,
Ndikuthandile ngothando olungunaphakade; ngenxa yoko ndikolulele inceba.

<span id="an_31:4">31:4</span> Ndiya kubuya ndikwakhe, wakheke, ntombi
inguSirayeli; uya kubuya uzihombise, uphathe iingqongqo zakho, uphume
uye ekungqungqeni kwabangqungqayo.

<span id="an_31:5">31:5</span> Uya kubuya utyale izidiliya ezintabeni
zakwaSamari, batyale abatyali, bazidle ngokwabo.

<span id="an_31:6">31:6</span> Ngokuba kuya kubakho umhla, abaya
kumemeza ngawo abalindi ezintabeni zakwaEfrayim, besithi, Sukani nime,
sinyuke siye eZiyon kuYehova, uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_31:7">31:7</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Memelelani
ngoYakobi, nivuye, nitsholoze ngentloko yeentlanga; vakalisani,
dumisani, yithini, Basindise, Yehova, abantu bakho, amasalela
akwaSirayeli.

<span id="an_31:8">31:8</span> Yabona, ndiyabazisa bevela ezweni
lasentla, ndibabuthe eziphelweni zehlabathi; beneemfama neziqhwala,
abamithiyo nabazalayo kunye; besisikhungu esikhulu, bebuyela apha.

<span id="an_31:9">31:9</span> Baya kuza belila, ndibakhokele
betarhuzisa; ndibase emilanjeni yamanzi ngendlela ethe tye, bengakhubeki
kuyo; kuba ndinguyise kuSirayeli, uEfrayim ngowamazibulo am.

<span id="an_31:10">31:10</span> Liveni ilizwi likaYehova, zintlanga,
nilixele eziqithini ezikude, nithi, Umchithachithi kaSirayeli uya
kumbutha, amgcine njengomalusi egcina umhlambi wakhe.

<span id="an_31:11">31:11</span> Ngokuba uYehova ummisele wamkhulula
uYakobi; umhlawulele wamkhulula esandleni sowomeleleyo kunaye.

<span id="an_31:12">31:12</span> Baya kuza bamemelele ezindulini
zaseZiyon, basinge kwizinto ezilungileyo zikaYehova, engqoloweni,
nasewayinini entsha, naseolini, nasemgqekwini weegusha neenkomo;
imiphefumlo yabo ibe njengomyezo onyelwa ngamanzi, uvunde; bangabi
saphinda bathe amandla.

<span id="an_31:13">31:13</span> Iya kwandula intombi ivuye
ekungqungqeni, namadodana namadoda amakhulu kunye; ndisenze isijwili
sabo sibe yimihlali, ndibathuthuzele, ndibavuyise, bangabi nasingqala.

<span id="an_31:14">31:14</span> Ndowuseza uhluthe umphefumlo
wababingeleli ngamafutha, bahluthe abantu bam zizinto zam ezilungileyo;
utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_31:15">31:15</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Kuvakele izwi
eRama, isimema, isililo esikrakra: uRakeli elilela abantwana bakhe,
engavumi ukuthuthuzeleka, ngenxa yabantwana bakhe, ngokuba bengasekho.

<span id="an_31:16">31:16</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Lithintele ilizwi
lakho, lingalili, namehlo akho angabi nanyembezi; ngokuba unomvuzo
umsebenzi wakho, utsho uYehova; baya kubuya ezweni lotshaba.

<span id="an_31:17">31:17</span> Linethemba ikamva lakho, utsho uYehova;
oonyana bakho baya kubuyela emdeni wabo.

<span id="an_31:18">31:18</span> Ndimvile ngenene uEfrayim, ehlunguzela
intloko, esithi, Undiqeqeshile ndaqeqesheka njengethole elingekathambi;
ndibuyise, ndibuye; ngokuba wena, Yehova, unguThixo wam.

<span id="an_31:19">31:19</span> Ngokuba emva kokukutshikilela kwam
ndazohlwaya, emva kokwaziswa kwam ndabetha ethangeni lam; ndadana, ndeva
ihlazo, ngokuba ndithwele isingcikivo sobuncinane bam.

<span id="an_31:20">31:20</span> Ngunyana onqabileyo na kum uEfrayim?
Ngumntwana wokuteketiswa na, le nto ndithi, ndakuthetha ngaye
ndimchasile, ndisuke ndimkhumbule ngakumbi? Ngenxa yoko izibilini zam
ziyasika ngaye; inene, ndiya kuba nemfesane kuye, utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_31:21">31:21</span> Zimiseleni izalathiso, zigxumekeleni
izibonda; yibhekise intliziyo yakho emendweni, endleleni owahamba ngayo.
Buya, ntombi inguSirayeli, buyela emizini yakowenu.

<span id="an_31:22">31:22</span> Kunini na unxaxhanxaxha, ntombi
iphambayo? ngokuba uYehova udala into entsha ehlabathini: inkazana iya
kuphahla indoda.

<span id="an_31:23">31:23</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Basaya kulithetha eli lizwi ezweni lakwaYuda
nasemizini yakhona, ekukubuyiseni kwam ukuthinjwa kwabo, lokuthi,
UYehova makakusikelele, khaya lobulungisa, ntaba yobungcwele.

<span id="an_31:24">31:24</span> Aya kuma khona amaYuda nemizi yawo
yonke kunye; abalimi, nabahamba emathanga benemihlambi yabo.

<span id="an_31:25">31:25</span> Ngokuba ndiyawuseza uhluthe umphefumlo
otyhafileyo; ndowanelisa umphefumlo wonke othe amandla.

<span id="an_31:26">31:26</span> Kwakubanjalo, ndavuka, ndakhangela;
ubuthongo bam bebumnandi kum.

<span id="an_31:27">31:27</span> Yabona, kuza imihla, utsho uYehova,
endiya kuyihlwayela indlu kaSirayeli nendlu kaYuda ngembewu yomntu,
nangembewu yenkomo.

<span id="an_31:28">31:28</span> Kuya kuthi njengoko ndabaphaphelayo
ukuba ndinyothule, ukuba ndidilize, ukuba ndigungxule, ukuba
nditshabalalise, ukuba ndenze kube kubi: ngokunjalo ndibaphaphele ukuba
ndakhe, ukuba ndityale; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_31:29">31:29</span> Ngaloo mihla abasayi kuba sathi, Ooyise
badle iidiliya ezimuncu, amazinyo oonyana aba buthelezi;

<span id="an_31:30">31:30</span> ke elowo uya kufa ngenxa yobakhe
ubugwenxa; umntu wonke odla iidiliya ezimuncu, nguye omazinyo aya kuba
buthelezi.

<span id="an_31:31">31:31</span> Yabona, kuza imihla, utsho uYehova,
endiya kwenza umnqophiso omtsha nendlu kaSirayeli nendlu kaYuda;

<span id="an_31:32">31:32</span> ungabi njengomnqophiso endawenza noyise
ngomhla endababambayo ngesandla, ukuba ndibakhuphe ezweni leYiputa;
umnqophiso wam abasuka bawaphula bona, nangani bendiyindoda yabo; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_31:33">31:33</span> Nguwo ke lo umnqophiso, endiya kuwenza
nendlu kaSirayeli emva kwaloo mihla, utsho uYehova: ndiya kuwubeka
umyalelo wam embilinini yabo, ndiwubhale ezintliziyweni zabo, ndibe
nguThixo wabo, babe ngabantu bam;

<span id="an_31:34">31:34</span> bangabi safundisa elowo ummelwane
wakhe, elowo umzalwana wakhe, besithi, Mazini uYehova; ngokuba bonke
bephela baya kundazi, kuthabathela kwabancinane kuse kwabakhulu, utsho
uYehova; ngokuba ndiya kubuxolela ubugwenxa babo, ndingabi sasikhumbula
isono sabo.

<span id="an_31:35">31:35</span> Utsho uYehova, uMniki welanga, ukuba
libe sisikhanyiso emini; uMniki wemimiselo yenyanga neenkwenkwezi, ukuba
zibe sisikhanyiso ebusuku; uMlatyuzisi wolwandle, ukuba agqume amaza
alo; ugama lakhe linguYehova wemikhosi:

<span id="an_31:36">31:36</span> ukuthi, Ukuba ithe yasuka loo mimiselo
phambi kwam, utsho uYehova, yophela nayo ke imbewu kaSirayeli ingabi
luhlanga phambi kwam ngamaxa onke.

<span id="an_31:37">31:37</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ukuba lingaba
nokulinganiswa izulu phezulu, zibe nokugocwagocwa iziseko zehlabathi
phantsi, nam ke ndoba ndiya kuyicekisa yonke imbewu kaSirayeli, ngenxa
yento yonke abayenzileyo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_31:38">31:38</span> Yabona, kuza imihla, utsho uYehova, oya
kuthi umzi lowo wakhelwe uYehova, kuthabathele enqabeni ende kaHananeli,
kuse esangweni lembombo;

<span id="an_31:39">31:39</span> lubuye luphume ulutya lokulinganisela,
luthi gca phezu kwenduli kaGarebhe, lujikele eGoha.

<span id="an_31:40">31:40</span> Yonke intili yezidumbu neyothuthu,
namasimi onke asa esihlanjeni seKidron, asa embombeni yesango lamahashe
ngasempumalanga, ibe ngcwele kuYehova, ingabi sanyothulwa, ingabi
sagungxulwa naphakade.

<span id="an_32:1">32:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, ngomnyaka weshumi kaZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda; loo mnyaka ke
ngumnyaka weshumi elinesibhozo kaNebhukadenetsare.

<span id="an_32:2">32:2</span> Oko ke impi yokumkani waseBhabheli
ibiyingqingile iYerusalem, uYeremiya umprofeti evalelwe entendelezweni
yentolongo, yendlu yokumkani wakwaYuda.

<span id="an_32:3">32:3</span> Kuba ebevalelwe kuyo nguZedekiya ukumkani
wakwaYuda, esithi, Yini na ukuba uthi ukuprofeta kwakho, Utsho uYehova
ukuthi, Yabona, ndiyawunikela lo mzi esandleni sokumkani waseBhabheli,
ukuba awuthimbe;

<span id="an_32:4">32:4</span> angasindi esandleni samaKaledi uZedekiya
ukumkani wakwaYuda; uya kunikelwa okunene esandleni sokumkani
waseBhabheli; umlomo wakhe uthethe nomlomo wakhe, amehlo akhe abone
amehlo akhe;

<span id="an_32:5">32:5</span> amse uZedekiya eBhabheli, abe khona ndide
ndimvelele, utsho uYehova; xa nithe nalwa namaKaledi, aniyi kuba
nampumelelo.

<span id="an_32:6">32:6</span> Wathi uYeremiya, Kwafika ilizwi
likaYehova kum, lisithi,

<span id="an_32:7">32:7</span> Yabona, uHanameli, unyana kaShalum
uyihlokazi, uza kuwe, esithi, Yithenge intsimi yam eseAnatoti; ngokuba
kulunge nawe ukuyithenga uyikhulule ngentlawulelo.

<span id="an_32:8">32:8</span> Weza ke kum entendelezweni yentolongo
uHanameli, unyana kabawokazi, ngokwelizwi likaYehova, wathi kum,
Khawuyithenge intsimi yam eseAnatoti, esezweni lakwaBhenjamin; ngokuba
lilunge nawe ilifa, kokwakho ukuyikhulula ngokumisela; zithengele. Ndazi
ke ukuba lilizwi likaYehova elo.

<span id="an_32:9">32:9</span> Ndayithenga ke intsimi kuHanameli, unyana
kabawokazi, eseAnatoti, ndamlinganisela imali leyo, iishekele ezilishumi
zesilivere ezineeshekele ezisixhenxe.

<span id="an_32:10">32:10</span> Ndakubhala ke encwadini, ndayitywina,
ndangqinisa amangqina, ndayilinganisela imali ngesikali.

<span id="an_32:11">32:11</span> Ndayithabatha ke incwadi yentengo, leyo
itywiniweyo inomthetho nemimiselo, naleyo ivulekileyo;

<span id="an_32:12">32:12</span> ndayinikela incwadi yentengo kuBharuki
unyana kaNeriya, unyana kaMaseya, emehlweni kaHanameli okabawokazi,
nasemehlweni amangqina lawo abhalileyo encwadini yentengo, nasemehlweni
amaYuda onke abehleli entendelezweni yentolongo.

<span id="an_32:13">32:13</span> Ndamwisela uBharuki umthetho emehlweni
abo, ndisithi,

<span id="an_32:14">32:14</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Thabatha ezi ncwadi, incwadi yentengo le
itywiniweyo, nencwadi le ivulekileyo, uzibeke esityeni somdongwe, ukuze
zihlale imihla emininzi.

<span id="an_32:15">32:15</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Kuya kubuya kuthengwe izindlu, namasimi, nezidiliya,
kweli lizwe.

<span id="an_32:16">32:16</span> Ndathandaza kuYehova emveni
kokuyinikela kwam incwadi yentengo kuBharuki unyana kaNeriya, ndathi,

<span id="an_32:17">32:17</span> Awu, Nkosi yam Yehova, yabona, walenza
izulu nehlabathi ngamandla akho amakhulu, nangengalo yakho eyolukileyo;
akukho nto ikunqabeleyo.

<span id="an_32:18">32:18</span> Unguwenza inceba kumawaka, uphindezela
ubugwenxa booyise esondweni loonyana babo emva kwabo; uloThixo mkhulu,
uligorha, ugama lakhe linguYehova wemikhosi;

<span id="an_32:19">32:19</span> ucebo likhulu, uzenzo zincamisileyo
ngamandla; umehlo avulekileyo phezu kweendlela zonke zoonyana babantu,
ukuba umnike ulowo ngokweendlela zakhe, nangokweziqhamo zezenzo zakhe;

<span id="an_32:20">32:20</span> wamisayo imiqondiso nezimanga ezweni
laseYiputa, unanamhla, nakumaSirayeli nakwabanye abantu, wazenzela
igama, njengoko kunjalo namhla.

<span id="an_32:21">32:21</span> Wabakhupha abantu bakho amaSirayeli
ezweni leYiputa ngemiqondiso, nangezimanga, nangesandla esithe nkqi,
nangengalo eyolukileyo, nangoloyikiso olukhulu.

<span id="an_32:22">32:22</span> Wabanika eli lizwe wabafungelayo
ooyise, ukuba ubanike ilizwe elibaleka amasi nobusi.

<span id="an_32:23">32:23</span> Beza ke balihlala; kodwa
abaliphulaphula izwi lakho, abahamba ngomyalelo wakho; konke
owabawiselayo umthetho ngako ukuba bakwenze, abakwenza; wabahlisela ke
bonke obu bubi.

<span id="an_32:24">32:24</span> Yabona, iindonga zokungqinga zifikile
kulo mzi, ukuba ziwuthimbe; umzi ke unikelwe esandleni samaKaledi alwayo
nawo ngekrele, nangendlala, nangendyikitya yokufa. Ilizwi owalithethayo
lenzekile; nali ulibona.

<span id="an_32:25">32:25</span> Ke wena, Nkosi yam Yehova, uthe kum,
Zithengele intsimi ngemali, ungqinise amangqina; wakubona ukuba umzi lo
unikelwe esandleni samaKaledi.

<span id="an_32:26">32:26</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya,
lisithi,

<span id="an_32:27">32:27</span> Yabona, ndinguYehova, uThixo wenyama
yonke; kukho nto indinqabeleyo na?

<span id="an_32:28">32:28</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabona,
ndiyawunikela lo mzi esandleni samaKaledi, nasesandleni
sikaNebhukadenetsare, ukumkani waseBhabheli, ukuba awuthimbe;

<span id="an_32:29">32:29</span> eze amaKaledi alwayo nalo mzi, awufake
isikhuni, awutshise nezindlu abeqhumisela kuBhahali phezu kophahla
lwazo, bathululela thixweni bambi iminikelo ethululwayo, ukuze
bandiqumbise.

<span id="an_32:30">32:30</span> Ngokuba oonyana bakaSirayeli noonyana
bakaYuda baye besenza ububi bodwa emehlweni am kwasebuncinaneni babo;
ngokuba oonyana bakaSirayeli ngabaqumbisi bodwa kum, ngezenzo zezandla
zabo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_32:31">32:31</span> Ngokuba lo mzi waba sisisulu somsindo
wam nobushushu bam, kususela kwimini owakhiwa ngayo, kude kube yile
mini; ukuze ndiwususe ebusweni bam,

<span id="an_32:32">32:32</span> ngenxa yobubi bonke boonyana
bakaSirayeli noonyana bakaYuda, ababenzileyo ukuba bandiqumbise, bona,
nookumkani babo, nabathetheli babo, nababingeleli babo, nabaprofeti
babo, namadoda akwaYuda, nabemi baseYerusalem.

<span id="an_32:33">32:33</span> Bandinikela ikhosi, abandinikela ubuso;
bafundiswa, befundiswa kwakusasa, abaphulaphula ububa bakuvume
ukuqeqeshwa.

<span id="an_32:34">32:34</span> Babeka izinto zabo ezinezothe endlwini
ebizwa ngegama lam, ukuze bayenze inqambi;

<span id="an_32:35">32:35</span> bamakhela uBhahali iziganga
ezisemfuleni wakwaBhen-hinom, ukuze babacandisele uMoleki oonyana babo
neentombi zabo, into endingabawiselanga mthetho ngayo, engathanga qatha
entliziyweni yam, ukuba bawenze loo masikizi, ukuze bawenze one amaYuda.

<span id="an_32:36">32:36</span> Kukaloku ke, ngako oko utsho uYehova,
uThixo kaSirayeli, ngokusingisele kulo mzi, enithi, Unikelwe esandleni
sokumkani waseBhabheli ngekrele, nangendlala, nangendyikitya yokufa:
ukuthi,

<span id="an_32:37">32:37</span> Yabona, ndiyababutha emazweni onke,
endabagxothela kuwo ngomsindo wam, nangobushushu bam, nangoburhalarhume
obukhulu; ndobabuyisela kule ndawo, ndibahlalise bekholosile.

<span id="an_32:38">32:38</span> Baya kuba ngabantu bam, mna ndibe
nguThixo wabo;

<span id="an_32:39">32:39</span> ndibanike intliziyo enye, nendlela
enye, ukuze bandoyike imihla yonke, kulunge kubo, nakoonyana babo emva
kwabo.

<span id="an_32:40">32:40</span> Ndiya kubenzela umnqophiso
ongunaphakade, ukuba ndingabuyi ekubalandeleni, ukuba ndibenzele
okulungileyo, ndibeke ukundoyika entliziyweni yabo, ukuze bangandishiyi.

<span id="an_32:41">32:41</span> Ndoba nemihlali ngabo, ndibenzele
okulungileyo, ndibatyale kweli lizwe ndinyanisile, ngentliziyo yam yonke
nangomphefumlo wam wonke.

<span id="an_32:42">32:42</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Njengoko
ndabaziselayo aba bantu bonke obu bubi bukhulu kangaka, ndiya
kwenjenjalo ukubazisela konke okulungileyo endikuthethayo ngabo.

<span id="an_32:43">32:43</span> Kuya kuthengwa amasimi kweli lizwe
nithi, Kusenkangala, alinabantu nankomo, linikelwe esandleni samaKaledi.

<span id="an_32:44">32:44</span> Baya kuthenga amasimi ngemali,
bawabhale encwadini, itywinwe; bathabathe amangqina ezweni
lakwaBhenjamin, nangeenxa zonke kwiYerusalem, nasemizini yakwaYuda,
nasemizini yasezintabeni, nasemizini yasezithabazini, nasemizini
yelasezantsi; ngokuba ndiya kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa kwabo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_33:1">33:1</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya
okwesibini, esavalelwe entendelezweni yentolongo, lisithi,

<span id="an_33:2">33:2</span> Utsho uYehova, uMenzi woku; uYehova,
uMyili woku, ukuba akuzimase; ugama lakhe linguYehova, ukuthi,

<span id="an_33:3">33:3</span> Ndinqule, ndikuphendule, ndikuxelele
izinto ezinkulu ezinqabileyo, ongazaziyo.

<span id="an_33:4">33:4</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli,
ngazo izindlu zalo mzi, nangezindlu zokumkani bakwaYuda ezidiliziweyo
ngenxa yeendonga zokungqinga, nangenxa yekrele;

<span id="an_33:5">33:5</span> bakubona ukuba baza kulwa namaKaledi,
bazizalisa ngezidumbu zabantu, endibabulalayo ngomsindo wam
nangobushushu bam, ekungenxa yezinto zabo zonke ezimbi, ukuba
ndibusithelise ubuso bam kulo mzi:

<span id="an_33:6">33:6</span> ukuthi, Yabona, ndiwubopha ngezinto
ezibotshwayo, eziphilisayo, ndibaphilise, ndibatyhilele ukuphuphuma
koxolo nenyaniso.

<span id="an_33:7">33:7</span> Ndiya kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa kukaYuda
nokuthinjwa kukaSirayeli, ndibakhe njengokwasekuqaleni.

<span id="an_33:8">33:8</span> Ndobahlambulula ebugwenxeni babo bonke,
abone ngabo kum; ndibuxolele ubugwenxa babo bonke, bone ngabo kum,
bakreqa ngabo kum.

<span id="an_33:9">33:9</span> Lo mzi uya kuba ligama lemihlali kum,
indumiso nesihombo kwiintlanga zonke zehlabathi, eziya kukuva konke
okulungileyo endikwenzayo kuwo, zinkwantye, zigungqe ngenxa yokulunga
konke, nangenxa yoxolo lonke, endiwenzela lona.

<span id="an_33:10">33:10</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Kuya kubuva
kuviwe kule ndawo, nitshoyo ukuthi, Ilinxuwa, ayinabantu, ayinankomo,
emizini yakwaYuda, nasezitratweni zaseYerusalem, ekusenkangala kuzo,
ezingenabantu, ezingenabemi, ezingenankomo:

<span id="an_33:11">33:11</span> kuviwe izwi lemihlali nezwi lemivuyo;
izwi lomyeni nezwi lomtshakazi; izwi labathi, Bulelani kuYehova
wemikhosi, ngokuba elungile uYehova, ngokuba ingunaphakade inceba yakhe;
abazisa imibulelo endlwini kaYehova. Ngokuba ndiya kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa
kwelizwe, limiwe njengokwasekuqaleni; utshilo uYehova.

<span id="an_33:12">33:12</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi, Kule
ndawo ilinxuwa, ingenamntu, ingenankomo, nasemizini yayo yonke, kuya
kubuya kubekho ikriwa labalusi, ababuthela imihlambi yabo kulo.

<span id="an_33:13">33:13</span> Emizini yasezintabeni, nasemizini
yasezithabazini, nasemizini yelasezantsi, nasezweni lakwaBhenjamin,
nangeenxa zonke eYerusalem, nasemizini yakwaYuda, iya kubuya igqithe
imihlambi phantsi kwezandla zoyibalayo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_33:14">33:14</span> Yabona, kuza imihla, utsho uYehova,
endiya kulimisa ilizwi elilungileyo, endalithethayo kwindlu kaSirayeli
nakwindlu kaYuda.

<span id="an_33:15">33:15</span> Ngaloo mihla nangelo xesha, ndiya
kumhlumisela uDavide iHlumelo loBulungisa, eliya kwenza ngokwesiko
nobulungisa ezweni.

<span id="an_33:16">33:16</span> Ngaloo mihla lona liya kusindiswa
elakwaYuda, ihlale ikholosile iYerusalem, ukubizwa kwayo kuthiwe,
UYehova-ububulungisa-bethu.

<span id="an_33:17">33:17</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, UDavide
akayi kunqunyukelwa ndoda yakuhlala etroneni yendlu kaSirayeli;

<span id="an_33:18">33:18</span> banganqunyukelwa ndoda ababingeleli
abangabaLevi, yakunyusa amadini anyukayo ebusweni bam, iqhumisele
ngeminikelo yokudla, yenze imibingelelo imihla yonke.

<span id="an_33:19">33:19</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya,
lisithi,

<span id="an_33:20">33:20</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ukuba nithe
nawaphula umnqophiso wam wemini, nomnqophiso wam wobusuku, ukuze
kungabikho mini nabusuku ngexesha elililo:

<span id="an_33:21">33:21</span> woba uya kwaphulwa nawo umnqophiso wam
noDavide umkhonzi wam, ukuba angabi nanyana ungukumkani etroneni yakhe;
kwanabaLevi ababingeleli, abalungiselela mna.

<span id="an_33:22">33:22</span> Njengokuba ungenakubalwa umkhosi
wezulu, ingenakulinganiselwa intlabathi yolwandle, ndiya kwenjenjalo
ukuyandisa imbewu yomkhonzi wam uDavide, nabaLevi abalungiselela mna.

<span id="an_33:23">33:23</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya,
lisithi,

<span id="an_33:24">33:24</span> Akukuboni na abakuthethayo aba bantu,
besithi, Imizalwane yomibini, awayinyulayo uYehova, uyicekisile yona?
Babagiba ke abam abantu, ngokokude bangabi saba luhlanga phambi kwabo.

<span id="an_33:25">33:25</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ukuba awumi
umnqophiso wam wemini nowobusuku, ukuba imimiselo yezulu neyehlabathi
andiyimisanga,

<span id="an_33:26">33:26</span> ndoba ndiya kuyicekisa nembewu kaYakobi
noDavide umkhonzi wam; ukuba embewini yakhe ndingabi sathabatha
abayilawulayo imbewu ka-Abraham noIsake noYakobi, ngokuba ndiya
kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa kwabo, ndibe nemfesane kubo.

<span id="an_34:1">34:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, akubon’ ukuba uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, enempi
yakhe yonke, nezikumkani zonke zelizwe eliselulawulweni lwesandla sakhe,
nezizwe zonke, uyalwa neYerusalem nemizi yayo yonke: lalisithi,

<span id="an_34:2">34:2</span> Utsho uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi,
Yiya, uthethe kuZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda, uthi kuye, Utsho uYehova
ukuthi, Yabona, ndiyawunikela lo mzi esandleni sokumkani waseBhabheli,
ukuba awutshise ngomlilo.

<span id="an_34:3">34:3</span> Ke wena akuyi kusinda esandleni sakhe;
inene, uya kubanjwa, unikelwe esandleni sakhe, amehlo akho awabone
amehlo okumkani waseBhabheli, umlomo wakhe uthethe nomlomo wakho, uve
nawe eBhabheli.

<span id="an_34:4">34:4</span> Kodwa live ilizwi likaYehova, Zedekiya
kumkani wakwaYuda; utsho uYehova ngawe, ukuthi, Akuyi kufa likrele,

<span id="an_34:5">34:5</span> Uya kufa unoxolo; ngokutshiselwa
kooyihlo, ookumkani bamandulo ababekho ngaphambi kwakho, baya
kwenjenjalo ukukutshisela; bakumbambazelele, besithi, Athi ke mna,
nkosi! Ngokuba mna ndilithethile ilizwi; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_34:6">34:6</span> Wawathetha ke uYeremiya umprofeti loo
mazwi onke kuZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda, eYerusalem,

<span id="an_34:7">34:7</span> yakubon’ ukuba impi yokumkani
waseBhabheli iyalwa neYerusalem, nemizi yonke yakwaYuda eseleyo,
neLakishe, neAzeka; ngokuba kwakusele yona emizini yakwaYuda, iyimizi
enqatyisiweyo.

<span id="an_34:8">34:8</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, emveni kokwenza kokumkani uZedekiya umnqophiso nabantu bonke
baseYerusalem, wokuvakalisa kubo inkululeko:

<span id="an_34:9">34:9</span> owokuba elowo andulule ikhoboka lakhe,
elowo ikhobokazana lakhe elingumHebhere, elingumHebherekazi, elikhulule,
kungabikho umkhonzisayo umYuda umzalwana wakhe.

<span id="an_34:10">34:10</span> Baphulaphula ke abathetheli bonke
nabantu bonke, abangenayo emnqophisweni wokuba elowo andulule ikhoboka
lakhe, elowo ikhobokazana lakhe, elikhulule, angabi sabakhonzisa;
baphulaphula ke, babandulula.

<span id="an_34:11">34:11</span> Emveni koko bajika, bawabuyisa
amakhoboka namakhobokazana ababewandulule bewakhulule, bawaxinzelela
ekubeni ngamakhoboka namakhobokazana.

<span id="an_34:12">34:12</span> Kwafika ke ilizwi likaYehova
kuYeremiya, livela kuYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_34:13">34:13</span> Utsho uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli,
ukuthi, Mna ndenza umnqophiso nooyihlo, mini ndabakhupha ezweni
laseYiputa, endlwini yobukhoboka;

<span id="an_34:14">34:14</span> ndathi, Ekupheleni kweminyaka
esixhenxe, ize nindulule elowo umzalwana wakhe ongumHebhere,
owazithengisayo kuwe; wokukhonza iminyaka emithandathu, umndulule kuwe,
umkhulule; ke ooyihlo abandiphulaphulanga, abandithobelanga ndlebe.

<span id="an_34:15">34:15</span> Nina ke nibuyile namhla, nenza okuthe
tye emehlweni am ngokuvakalisa inkululeko, elowo kummelwane wakhe, nenza
umnqophiso phambi kwam endlwini ebizwe ngegama lam;

<span id="an_34:16">34:16</span> nasuka najika, nalihlambela igama lam,
nabuyisa elowo ikhoboka lakhe, elowo ikhobokazana lakhe, enaniwandulule,
niwakhulule ngokuthanda kwawo; nawaxinzelela ekubeni ngamakhoboka
namakhobokazana kuni.

<span id="an_34:17">34:17</span> Ngako oko, utsho uYehova ukuthi,
Anindiphulaphulanga ngokuvakalisa inkululeko, elowo kumzalwana wakhe,
elowo kummelwane wakhe; yabonani, ndivakalisa kuni inkululeko, utsho
uYehova, yokuya ekreleni, nasendlaleni, nasendyikityeni yokufa,
ndininikele kwizikumkani zonke zehlabathi, ukuze nibe yinto
yokunqakulisa.

<span id="an_34:18">34:18</span> Ndiya kuwenza amadoda awugqithileyo
umnqophiso wam, angawagcinanga amazwi omnqophiso awawenzayo phambi kwam,
abe lelo thole alicanda kubini, acanda phakathi kwezahlulo zenyama yalo.

<span id="an_34:19">34:19</span> Abathetheli bakwaYuda, nabathetheli
baseYerusalem, namagosa, nababingeleli, nabantu bonke belizwe abacandayo
phakathi kwezahlulo zethole,

<span id="an_34:20">34:20</span> ndiya kubanikela ezandleni zeentshaba
zabo, nasezandleni zabafuna umphefumlo wabo, zidliwe izidumbu zabo
ziintaka zezulu nangamarhamncwa omhlaba.

<span id="an_34:21">34:21</span> UZedekiya ke ukumkani wakwaYuda,
nabathetheli bakhe, ndiya kubanikela esandleni sabafuna umphefumlo wabo,
nasesandleni sempi yokumkani waseBhabheli, yona leyo yemkayo kuni.

<span id="an_34:22">34:22</span> Yabona, ndiwisa umthetho, utsho
uYehova, wokuba ndibabuyisele kulo mzi, balwe nawo, bawuthimbe,
bawutshise ngomlilo, ndiyenze amanxuwa imizi yakwaYuda, ingemiwa.

<span id="an_35:1">35:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, ngemihla kaYehoyakim unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda,
lalisithi,

<span id="an_35:2">35:2</span> Yiya endlwini yamaRekabhi, uthethe nawo,
uwangenise endlwini kaYehova, kwelinye igumbi, uwaseze iwayini.

<span id="an_35:3">35:3</span> Ndamthabatha ke uYazaniya unyana
kaYeremiya, unyana kaHabhatsiniya, nabazalwana bakhe, noonyana bakhe
bonke, nendlu yonke yamaRekabhi;

<span id="an_35:4">35:4</span> ndabangenisa endlwini kaYehova, egumbini
koonyana bakaHanan unyana kaIgedaliya, umfo wakwaThixo, elisecaleni
kwegumbi labathetheli, eliphezu kwegumbi likaMahaseya unyana kaShalum,
umgcini-mnyango.

<span id="an_35:5">35:5</span> Ndabeka phambi koonyana bendlu
yamaRekabhi iindebe ezizele yiwayini, neebhekile, ndathi kubo, Selani
iwayini.

<span id="an_35:6">35:6</span> Bathi bona, Asiyiseli iwayini: ngokuba
uYonadabhi unyana kaRekabhi, ubawo, wasiwisela umthetho wokuthi, Ze
ningaseli wayini, nina, noonyana benu, naphakade;

<span id="an_35:7">35:7</span> ningakhi zindlu, ningahlwayeli mbewu,
ningatyali sidiliya, ningabi nazo ezo zinto; ke nohlala ezintenteni
yonke imihla yenu, ukuze niphile imihla emininzi phezu komhlaba,
eningabaphambukeli kuwo.

<span id="an_35:8">35:8</span> Siliphulaphule ke izwi likaYonadabhi
unyana kaRekabhi, ubawo, kuko konke awasiwisela umthetho ngako, ukuba
singaseli wayini yonke imihla yethu, thina, nabafazi bethu, noonyana
bethu, neentombi zethu;

<span id="an_35:9">35:9</span> wokuba singakhi nazindlu zokuba sihlale
kuzo, singabi nazidiliya, nantsimi, nambewu.

<span id="an_35:10">35:10</span> Sihleli ezintenteni, seva, senza ngako
konke awasiwisela umthetho ngako uYonadabhi ubawo.

<span id="an_35:11">35:11</span> Ke kaloku kwathi, ekunyukeni
kukaNebhukadenetsare, ukumkani waseBhabheli, esiza kweli lizwe, sathi,
Yizani singene eYerusalem ngenxa yempi yamaKaledi, nangenxa yempi
yama-Aram; sahlala ke eYerusalem apha.

<span id="an_35:12">35:12</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya,
lisithi,

<span id="an_35:13">35:13</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yiya, uthi kumadoda akwaYuda nakubemi baseYerusalem,
Anikuvumi na ukuqeqeshwa, ukuba niwaphulaphule amazwi am? utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_35:14">35:14</span> Agciniwe amazwi kaYonadabhi, unyana
kaRekabhi, awabawisela oonyana bakhe ukuba bangaseli wayini; abaseli
unanamhla, bawuphulaphula ke umthetho kayise. Ke mna ndathetha kuni,
ndithetha, ndivuka kusasa; anindiphulaphulanga.

<span id="an_35:15">35:15</span> Ndabathumela kuni bonke abakhonzi bam,
abaprofeti, ndibathuma, ndivuka kusasa, ndisithi, Khanibuye, elowo
endleleni yakhe embi, nilungise iintlondi zenu, ningalandeli thixo
bambi, ukuze nibakhonze; nohlala ke emhlabeni endawunika nina nooyihlo.
Ke anizithobanga iindlebe zenu, anindiphulaphulanga.

<span id="an_35:16">35:16</span> Inene, oonyana bakaYonadabhi unyana
kaRekabhi bawugcinile umthetho kayise, awabawiselayo; ke bona aba bantu
abandiphulaphuli.

<span id="an_35:17">35:17</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova, uThixo
wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiwazisela amaYuda
nabemi bonke baseYerusalem bonke obu bubi ndathethayo ngabo; ngenxa
yokuba ndathetha kubo, abeva; ndababiza, abasabela.

<span id="an_35:18">35:18</span> UYeremiya wathi kwindlu yamaRekabhi,
Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Ngenxa enokuba
niwuphulaphule umthetho kaYonadabhi uyihlo, nayigcina yonke imithetho
yakhe, nenza ngako konke awaniwisela umthetho ngako;

<span id="an_35:19">35:19</span> ngako oko utsho uYehova wemikhosi,
uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, UYonadabhi, unyana kaRekabhi, akayi
kunqunyukelwa ndoda yakuma phambi kwam yonke imihla.

<span id="an_36:1">36:1</span> Kwathi, ngomnyaka wesine kaYehoyakim
unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, lafika eli lizwi kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, lisithi,

<span id="an_36:2">36:2</span> Thabathela kuwe incwadi esongwayo,
uwabhale kuyo onke amazwi endawathetha kuwe ngamaSirayeli, nangamaYuda,
nangeentlanga zonke, kususela kwimini endathethayo kuwe, uthabathele
emihleni kaYosiya, ude uze kule mini.

<span id="an_36:3">36:3</span> Mhlawumbi indlu kaYuda ingabuphulaphula
bonke ububi endicinga ukubenza kubo, ukuze babuye elowo endleleni yakhe
embi, ndibuxolele ubugwenxa babo nesono sabo.

<span id="an_36:4">36:4</span> UYeremiya wabiza uBharuki unyana
kaNeriya, wawabhala encwadini esongwayo uBharuki, ephuma emlonyeni
kaYeremiya, onke amazwi kaYehova, awawathethayo kuye.

<span id="an_36:5">36:5</span> UYeremiya wamwisela uBharuki umthetho,
esithi, Mna ndivalelwe, andinako ukuya endlwini kaYehova.

<span id="an_36:6">36:6</span> Yiya wena, uwalese encwadini esongwayo,
leyo uyibhalileyo, ephuma emlonyeni wam, amazwi kaYehova, ezindlebeni
zabantu endlwini kaYehova ngomhla wokuzila ukudla; uwalese
nasezindlebeni zamaYuda onke, avela emizini yawo.

<span id="an_36:7">36:7</span> Mhlawumbi ukutarhuzisa kwabo kungawa
phambi koYehova, babuye elowo endleleni yakhe embi; ngokuba mkhulu
umsindo nobushushu, abuthethileyo uYehova ngaba bantu.

<span id="an_36:8">36:8</span> Wenza ke uBharuki unyana kaNeriya
njengako konke abemwisele umthetho uYeremiya umprofeti, wokuba awalese
encwadini amazwi kaYehova endlwini kaYehova.

<span id="an_36:9">36:9</span> Kwathi ngomnyaka weshumi kaYehoyakim
unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, ngenyanga yesithoba, bamema uzilo
lokudla phambi koYehova kubantu bonke baseYerusalem, nakubantu bonke
ababevele emizini yakwaYuda, beza eYerusalem.

<span id="an_36:10">36:10</span> UBharuki wawalesa encwadini amazwi
kaYeremiya endlwini kaYehova, egumbini likaGemariya unyana kaShafan,
umbhali, entendelezweni ephezulu, ekungeneni kwesango elitsha lendlu
kaYehova, ezindlebeni zabantu bonke.

<span id="an_36:11">36:11</span> Waweva uMikaya unyana kaGemariya,
unyana kaShafan, onke amazwi kaYehova encwadini,
