<span id="an_36:12">36:12</span> wehla waya endlwini yokumkani, egumbini
lombhali. Nabo, behleli khona abathetheli bonke: ooElishama umbhali,
noDelaya unyana kaShemaya, noElinatan unyana ka-Akebhore, noGemariya
unyana kaShafan, noZedekiya unyana kaHananiya, nabathetheli bonke.

<span id="an_36:13">36:13</span> UMikaya wabaxelela onke amazwi
abewavile ekuleseni kukaBharuki encwadini, ezindlebeni zabantu.

<span id="an_36:14">36:14</span> Bonke abathetheli bathumela kuBharuki
uYehudi unyana kaNetaniya, unyana kaShelemiya, unyana kaKushi, besithi,
Incwadi esongwayo leyo ulese kuyo ezindlebeni zabantu, yiphathe
ngesandla sakho, uze. UBharuki unyana kaNeriya wayiphatha ke incwadi
esongwayo ngesandla sakhe, weza kubo.

<span id="an_36:15">36:15</span> Bathi kuye, Khawuhlale phantsi, uyilese
ezindlebeni zethu. Wayilesa ke uBharuki ezindlebeni zabo.

<span id="an_36:16">36:16</span> Kwathi, bakuweva onke loo mazwi,
bankwantya, elowo ebheka kowabo; bathi kuBharuki, Simelwe kukumxelela
ukumkani onke la mazwi.

<span id="an_36:17">36:17</span> Bambuza uBharuki, besithi,
Khawusixelele, utheni na ukuwabhala onke la mazwi ephuma emlonyeni
wakhe?

<span id="an_36:18">36:18</span> Wathi uBharuki kubo, Wawathetha kum
onke la mazwi aphuma emlonyeni wakhe, ndawabhala encwadini le ngeinki.

<span id="an_36:19">36:19</span> Bathi abathetheli kuBharuki, Hamba uye
kuzimela, wena noYeremiya, kungazi mntu apho nikhona.

<span id="an_36:20">36:20</span> Bangena ke kukumkani entendelezweni,
beyibeke incwadi esongwayo egumbini likaElishama umbhali, bawaxela
ezindlebeni zokumkani onke amazwi lawo.

<span id="an_36:21">36:21</span> Ukumkani wathuma uYehudi, ukuba
ayithabathe incwadi esongwayo; wayithabatha ke egumbini likaElishama
umbhali. UYehudi wayilesa ezindlebeni zokumkani, nasezindlebeni
zabathetheli bonke abamele ngakukumkani.

<span id="an_36:22">36:22</span> Ke kaloku ukumkani wayehleli endlwini
yasebusika ngenyanga yesithoba, kubasiwe elukhambeni phambi kwakhe.

<span id="an_36:23">36:23</span> Kwathi, xa uYehudi abelese imiqolo
emithathu nokuba mine, wayiqwenga ukumkani ngesitshetshe sombhali,
wayiphosa emlilweni obuselukhambeni, yada yatsha yagqibela yonke incwadi
esongwayo, emlilweni obuselukhambeni.

<span id="an_36:24">36:24</span> Abankwantyanga, abazikrazulanga iingubo
zabo ukumkani nabakhonzi bakhe, ababeweva loo mazwi onke.

<span id="an_36:25">36:25</span> Noko ke bambongozayo ukumkani
ooElinatan noDelaya noGemariya, ukuba angayitshisi incwadi esongwayo,
akabaphulaphula.

<span id="an_36:26">36:26</span> Ukumkani wabawisela umthetho ooYerameli
unyana kakumkani, noSeraya unyana ka-Azeriyeli, noShelemiya unyana
ka-Abhedeli, ukuba bambambe uBharuki umbhali noYeremiya umprofeti;
uYehova wabazimeza.

<span id="an_36:27">36:27</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya,
emveni kokuba ukumkani abeyitshisile incwadi esongwayo, namazwi
abewabhalile uBharuki, ephuma emlonyeni kaYeremiya, lisithi,

<span id="an_36:28">36:28</span> Buya, uthabathe enye incwadi esongwayo,
ubhale kuyo onke amazwi okuqala, abesencwadini esongwayo yokuqala,
awayitshisayo uYehoyakim ukumkani wakwaYuda.

<span id="an_36:29">36:29</span> Uze uthi kuYehoyakim ukumkani
wakwaYuda, Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Wena uyitshisile le ncwadi isongwayo,
usithi, Yini na ukuba ubhale kuyo ukuthi, Ukumkani waseBhabheli uya kuza
eze, alonakalise eli lizwe, aphelise umntu nenkomo kulo?

<span id="an_36:30">36:30</span> Ngako oko, utsho uYehova ngokusingisele
kuYehoyakim ukumkani wakwaYuda, ukuthi, Akuyi kubakho bani wakwakhe
kuye, uhlalayo etroneni kaDavide; isidumbu sakhe siya kulahlelwa
ebushushwini belanga emini, naseqabakeni ebusuku.

<span id="an_36:31">36:31</span> Ndiya kumvelela yena, nembewu yakhe,
nabakhonzi bakhe, ngobugwenxa babo; ndibuzisele bona, nabemi
baseYerusalem, namadoda akwaYuda, bonke ububi endabuthethayo kubo; ke
abaphulaphula.

<span id="an_36:32">36:32</span> UYeremiya wathabatha enye incwadi
esongwayo, wayinika uBharuki unyana kaNeriya, umbhali; wawabhala kuyo,
ephuma emlonyeni kaYeremiya, onke amazwi encwadi awayitshisayo
uYehoyakim ukumkani wakwaYuda ngomlilo. Kongezelelwa kuwo amazwi
amaninzi, anjengawo.

<span id="an_37:1">37:1</span> Ke kaloku ukumkani uZedekiya unyana
kaYosiya waba ngukumkani esikhundleni sikaKoniyahu unyana kaYehoyakim,
owenziwa ukumkani ezweni lakwaYuda nguNebhukadenetsare ukumkani
waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_37:2">37:2</span> Akawaphulaphula naye, nabakhonzi bakhe,
nabantu belizwe, amazwi kaYehova awawathethayo ngoYeremiya umprofeti.

<span id="an_37:3">37:3</span> Ukumkani uZedekiya wathuma ooYehukali
unyana kaShelemiya, noZefaniya unyana kaMahaseya, umbingeleli,
kuYeremiya umprofeti, esithi, Khawusithandazele kuYehova uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_37:4">37:4</span> UYeremiya ke ubengena ephuma phakathi
kwabantu, bengekamfaki entolongweni.

<span id="an_37:5">37:5</span> Ke kaloku impi kaFaro ibiphume eYiputa;
aziva iindaba zayo amaKaledi abeyingqinga iYerusalem, esuka emka
eYerusalem.

<span id="an_37:6">37:6</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya
umprofeti, lisithi,

<span id="an_37:7">37:7</span> Utsho uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi,
Yitshoni kukumkani wakwaYuda, onithume ukuza kubuzisa kum, ukuthi,
Yabonani, impi kaFaro ephume isiza ukuninceda, iya kubuyela ezweni layo
eYiputa;

<span id="an_37:8">37:8</span> abuye ke amaKaledi, alwe nalo mzi,
awuthimbe, awutshise ngomlilo.

<span id="an_37:9">37:9</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Musani
ukuzikhohlisa ngokwenu, nisithi, Aya kumka kanye kuthi amaKaledi;
ngokuba akayi kumka.

<span id="an_37:10">37:10</span> Inene, nibe ningafanelana niyixabele
impi yonke yamaKaledi alwayo nani, kwasala kuyo amadoda aziingxwelera;
abeya kuvuka elowo ententeni yakhe, awutshise lo mzi ngomlilo.

<span id="an_37:11">37:11</span> Kwathi, ekumkeni kwempi yamaKaledi
eYerusalem ngenxa yempi kaFaro,

<span id="an_37:12">37:12</span> waphuma uYeremiya eYerusalem, esiya
ezweni lakwaBhenjamin, ukuba athabathe khona isahlulelo sakhe phakathi
kwabantu.

<span id="an_37:13">37:13</span> Kwathi, esesangweni lakwaBhenjamin,
ekhona nomphathi-balindi, ogama linguIriya unyana kaShelemiya, unyana
kaHananiya, wambamba uYeremiya umprofeti, esithi, Uphambela kumaKaledi.

<span id="an_37:14">37:14</span> Wathi uYeremiya, Uyaxoka; andiphambeli
kumaKaledi. Ke akamphulaphula; uIriya wambamba uYeremiya, wamsa
kubathetheli.

<span id="an_37:15">37:15</span> Abathetheli bamqumbela uYeremiya,
bambetha, bamfaka endlwini yababanjwa, endlwini yombhali uYonatan;
ngokuba babeyenze intolongo.

<span id="an_37:16">37:16</span> Xa uYeremiya ebengenile endlwini
engumhadi, ezingontsini, wahlala khona uYeremiya imihla emininzi.

<span id="an_37:17">37:17</span> Uthe ke ukumkani uZedekiya wathumela,
wamthabatha; ukumkani wambuza endlwini yakhe ngasese, wathi, Kukho lizwi
na liphuma kuYehova? Wathi uYeremiya, Likho; wathi, Uya kunikelwa
esandleni sokumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_37:18">37:18</span> Wathi uYeremiya kukumkani uZedekiya,
Ndone ngantoni na kuwe, nakubakhonzi bakho, nakwaba bantu, ukuba
nindifake entolongweni nje?

<span id="an_37:19">37:19</span> Baphi na ke abaprofeti benu
ababeprofeta kuni, besithi, Ukumkani waseBhabheli akayi kunifikela nina,
nalo eli lizwe?

<span id="an_37:20">37:20</span> Kaloku ke khawuphulaphule, nkosi yam
kumkani, makuwe phambi kwakho ukutarhuzisa kwam; musa ukundibuyisela
endlwini kaYonatan umbhali, hleze ndifele khona.

<span id="an_37:21">37:21</span> Ukumkani uZedekiya wawisa umthetho;
bambeka uYeremiya entendelezweni yabalindi, bamnika intenda yesonka
imihla ngemihla esitratweni saboji, sada saphela sonke isonka phakathi
komzi. UYeremiya wahlala ke entendelezweni yabalindi.

<span id="an_38:1">38:1</span> Ke kaloku uShefatiya unyana kaMatan,
noGedaliya unyana kaPashure, noYukali unyana kaShelemiya, noPashure
unyana kaMalekiya, baweva amazwi abewathetha uYeremiya kubantu bonke,
esithi,

<span id="an_38:2">38:2</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Ohlala kulo mzi
wofa likrele, nayindlala, nayindyikitya yokufa; ophuma aye kumaKaledi
wophila, ube lixhoba kuye umphefumlo wakhe, aphile.

<span id="an_38:3">38:3</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Lo mzi uya
kunikelwa esandleni sempi yokumkani waseBhabheli, awuthimbe.

<span id="an_38:4">38:4</span> Bathi ke abathetheli kukumkani,
Mayibulawe le ndoda, ngokuba ngokwenjenje iwisa izandla zamadoda okulwa,
aseleyo kulo mzi, nezandla zabantu bonke, ngokuthetha kubo amazwi anje;
ngokuba le ndoda ayilungxamele uxolo lwaba bantu, ingxamele ububi babo.

<span id="an_38:5">38:5</span> Wathi ukumkani uZedekiya, Yabonani,
usezandleni zenu; ngokuba ukumkani engenakuthini engenani.

<span id="an_38:6">38:6</span> Bamthabatha uYeremiya, bamphosa emhadini
kaMalekiya unyana wokumkani, obusentendelezweni yabalindi; bamhlisa
uYeremiya ngezintya emhadini, lowo ungenamanzi, unodaka; watshona
eludakeni uYeremiya.

<span id="an_38:7">38:7</span> Weva uEbhedi-meleki umKushi, indoda
elithenwa, ebisendlwini yokumkani, ukuba bamfake emhadini uYeremiya;
ukumkani ke ubehleli esangweni lakwaBhenjamin.

<span id="an_38:8">38:8</span> Waphuma uEbhedi-meleki endlwini
yokumkani, wathetha kukumkani, esithi,

<span id="an_38:9">38:9</span> Nkosi yam, kumkani, la madoda enze into
embi ngako konke akwenzileyo kuYeremiya umprofeti lo, amphosa emhadini;
uya kufa yindlala kuloo ndawo akuyo, ngokuba akusekho sonka kulo mzi.

<span id="an_38:10">38:10</span> Ukumkani wamwisela umthetho
uEbhedi-meleki umKushi, esithi, Thabatha apha amadoda angamashumi
amathathu asesandleni sakho umrhole uYeremiya umprofeti emhadini,
engekafi.

<span id="an_38:11">38:11</span> UEbhedi-meleki wathabatha amadoda lawo
asesandleni sakhe, waya endlwini yokumkani ngaphantsi kwendlu
yobuncwane, wathabatha khona amadlavu eengubo ezikrazukileyo
nawezonakeleyo, wawathobela kuYeremiya emhadini ngezintya.

<span id="an_38:12">38:12</span> Wathi uEbhedi-meleki umKushi
kuYeremiya, Khawubeke la madlavu eengubo ezikrazukileyo nawezonakeleyo
phantsi kwamakhwapha akho ngaphantsi kwezintya. Wenjenjalo uYeremiya.

<span id="an_38:13">38:13</span> Bamrhola uYeremiya ngezintya, bamnyusa
emhadini; uYeremiya wahlala entendelezweni yabalindi.

<span id="an_38:14">38:14</span> Wathuma ukumkani uZedekiya,
wamthabathela kuye uYeremiya umprofeti, ekungeneni emnyango wesithathu
osendlwini kaYehova. Wathi ukumkani kuYeremiya, Ndiya kukubuza indawo;
uze ungafihli nto kum.

<span id="an_38:15">38:15</span> Wathi uYeremiya kuZedekiya, Ukuba
ndithe ndakuxelela, akuyi kundibulala undibulale na? Nokuba ndithe
ndakucebisa, akuyi kundiphulaphula.

<span id="an_38:16">38:16</span> Ukumkani uZedekiya wamfungela uYeremiya
ngasese, esithi, Ehleli nje uYehova, owasenzela lo mphefumlo, inene,
andiyi kukubulala, andiyi kukunikela ezandleni zaloo madoda awufunayo
umphefumlo wakho.

<span id="an_38:17">38:17</span> Wathi uYeremiya kuZedekiya, Utsho
uYehova, uThixo wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Ukuba uthe waphuma
ukuphuma oku, waya kubathetheli bokumkani waseBhabheli, wophila
umphefumlo wakho, nalo mzi ungatshiswa ngomlilo; uphile wena nendlu
yakho;

<span id="an_38:18">38:18</span> ke ukuba uthe akwaphuma uye
kubathetheli bokumkani waseBhabheli, lo mzi wonikelwa esandleni
samaKaledi, awutshise ngomlilo, wena ke ungasindi esandleni sawo.

<span id="an_38:19">38:19</span> Ukumkani uZedekiya wathi kuYeremiya,
Ndinesithukuthezi ngamaYuda aphambele kumaKaledi, hleze andinikele
esandleni sawo, afekethe ngam.

<span id="an_38:20">38:20</span> Wathi uYeremiya, Akayi kukunikela.
Khawuliphulaphule izwi likaYehova, ngokoko ndilithethileyo kuwe; kolunga
kuwe, uphile umphefumlo wakho.

<span id="an_38:21">38:21</span> Ke ukuba uthe akwavuma ukuphuma, nali
ilizwi andibonise lona uYehova, lokuthi,

<span id="an_38:22">38:22</span> Yabona, bonke abafazi abaseleyo
endlwini yokumkani wakwaYuda, baya kukhutshwa basiwe kubathetheli
bokumkani waseBhabheli, bathi abafazi abo, Amadoda axolelene nawe
akuxhokonxile, akweyisile; zitshonile nje emgxobhozweni iinyawo zakho,
wona abuya umva.

<span id="an_38:23">38:23</span> Ke bonke abafazi bakho noonyana bakho
baya kukhutshwa, basiwe kumaKaledi, ungasindi wena esandleni sawo; ke
wena uya kubanjwa sisandla sokumkani waseBhabheli, utshisise lo mzi
ngomlilo.

<span id="an_38:24">38:24</span> UZedekiya wathi kuYeremiya, La mazwi
makangaziwa mntu, ukuze ungafi.

<span id="an_38:25">38:25</span> Xa ke bathe beva abathetheli ukuba
ndithethe nawe, beza kuwe, bathi kuwe, Khawusixelele oko ukuthethileyo
kukumkani; musa ukukufihla kuthi, asiyi kukubulala; kwanakuthethileyo
ukumkani kuwe:

<span id="an_38:26">38:26</span> wothi kubo, Ndiwise utarhuziso lwam
phambi kokumkani, ukuba angandibuyiseli endlwini kaYonatan, ndifele
khona.

<span id="an_38:27">38:27</span> Beza kuYeremiya bonke abathetheli,
bambuza; wabaxelela ngokwaloo mazwi onke abewise umthetho ngawo
ukumkani. Bathi tu, bemka kuye; ngokuba ayivakalanga le nto.

<span id="an_38:28">38:28</span> Wahlala uYeremiya entendelezweni
yabalindi, kwada kwangumhla eyathinjwa ngawo iYerusalem.

<span id="an_39:1">39:1</span> Kwathi, xenikweni iYerusalem ibithinjiwe
(ngomnyaka wesithoba kaZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda, ngenyanga yeshumi,
akubon’ ukuba ufikile eYerusalem uNebhukadenetsare nempi yakhe yonke,
bayingqinga;

<span id="an_39:2">39:2</span> ngomnyaka weshumi elinamnye kaZedekiya,
ngenyanga yesine, ngolwesithoba enyangeni leyo, wagqojozwa umzi),

<span id="an_39:3">39:3</span> bafika bonke abathetheli bokumkani
waseBhabheli, bahlala esangweni laphakathi: ooNergale-sharetsere,
noSamgare-nebho, noSarsekim umthetheli wamathenwa, noNergale-sharetsere
umthetheli wezazi, nabanye abathetheli bonke bokumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_39:4">39:4</span> Kwathi, akubabona uZedekiya ukumkani
wakwaYuda namadoda onke okulwa, babaleka, baphuma ngobusuku phakathi
komzi ngendlela yomyezo wokumkani, ngesango eliphakathi kweendonga,
baphuma ngendlela yeArabha.

<span id="an_39:5">39:5</span> Impi yamaKaledi yabasukela, yamfikela
uZedekiya ezinkqantosini zaseYeriko; yamthabatha, yenyuka naye, yamsa
kuNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, eRibhela ezweni laseHamati;
athethwa khona amatyala akhe.

<span id="an_39:6">39:6</span> Ukumkani waseBhabheli wababulala oonyana
bakaZedekiya eRibhela emehlweni akhe; nabanumzana bonke bakwaYuda
wababulala ukumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_39:7">39:7</span> Wamtyhaphaza amehlo uZedekiya, wamkhonkxa
ngamakhamandela obhedu, ukuba asiwe eBhabheli.

<span id="an_39:8">39:8</span> AmaKaledi ayitshisa ngomlilo indlu
yokumkani nezindlu zabantu, azidiliza neendonga zaseYerusalem.

<span id="an_39:9">39:9</span> Amasalela abantu abaseleyo phakathi
komzi, amaphamba aphambelayo kuye, kwanamasalela abantu abaseleyo,
wabafudusela eBhabheli uNebhuzaradan umthetheli wabasiki;

<span id="an_39:10">39:10</span> ke inxenye yabantu abazizisweli,
abangenanto iyinto, uNebhuzaradan, inkulu yabasiki, wayishiya ezweni
lakwaYuda, wayinika izidiliya namasimi ngaloo mhla.

<span id="an_39:11">39:11</span> Ke kaloku, uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani
waseBhabheli wawisa umthetho ngoYeremiya ngesandla sikaNebhuzaradan,
umthetheli wabasiki, esithi,

<span id="an_39:12">39:12</span> Mthabathe, umise amehlo akho kuye,
ungenzi nto imbi kuye; wothi, njengoko akuthethayo kuwe, wenjenjalo
kuye.

<span id="an_39:13">39:13</span> Ke bathuma ooNebhuzaradan umthetheli
wabasiki, noNebhushazebhan umthetheli wamathenwa, noNergale-sharetsere
umthetheli wezazi, nabathetheli bonke bokumkani waseBhabheli;

<span id="an_39:14">39:14</span> bathuma bamthabatha uYeremiya
entendelezweni yabalindi, bamnikela kuGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, unyana
kaShafan, ukuba amkhuphe amse ekhaya. Wahlala ke phakathi kwabantu.

<span id="an_39:15">39:15</span> Ke kaloku, kwaye kufike ilizwi
likaYehova kuYeremiya, akuba evalelwe entendelezweni yabalindi, lisithi,

<span id="an_39:16">39:16</span> Yiya uthi kuEbhedi-meleki umKushi,
Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabona, amazwi am
ndiwazisela ububi kulo mzi, andiwaziseli okulungileyo; aya kwenzeka
phambi kwakho ngaloo mhla.

<span id="an_39:17">39:17</span> Ke ndokuhlangula ngaloo mhla, utsho
uYehova, unganikelwa esandleni samadoda onxungupheleyo ngawo.

<span id="an_39:18">39:18</span> Ngokuba, inene, ndiya kukusiza, ungawi
likrele; uya kuba lixhoba kuwe umphefumlo wakho, ngokuba ukholose ngam;
utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_40:1">40:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya, livela
kuYehova, emveni kokuba ebendululwe eRama nguNebhuzaradan, umthetheli
wabasiki, ekumthabatheni kwakhe ekhonkxiwe ngemixokelelwane phakathi
kwabafudusiweyo bonke baseYerusalem nabakwaYuda, ababefuduselwa
eBhabheli.

<span id="an_40:2">40:2</span> Umthetheli wabasiki wamthabatha ke
uYeremiya, wathi kuye, UYehova uThixo wakho wathetha obu bubi ngale
ndawo;

<span id="an_40:3">40:3</span> uYehova wabufikisa, wenza njengoko
wakuthethayo; ngokuba nonayo kuYehova, analiphulaphula izwi lakhe,
yabakho ke le nto kuni.

<span id="an_40:4">40:4</span> Kaloku ke yabona, ndiyayicombulula namhla
imixokelelwane esezandleni zakho. Ukuba kuthe kwalunga emehlweni akho
ukuya nam eBhabheli, yiza, ndolimisa iliso lam kuwe; ukuba kuthe kwakubi
emehlweni akho ukuya nam eBhabheli, yeka ke. Uyabona, ilizwe lonke
liphambi kwakho; ukuya apho kuthe kwalunga kwathi tye emehlweni akho,
oko kokwakho, yiya khona.

<span id="an_40:5">40:5</span> Uthe ke engekabuyi, wathi, Buyela
kuGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, unyana kaShafan, owenziwa umveleli
ngukumkani waseBhabheli emizini yakwaYuda, uhlale naye phakathi
kwabantu; okanye uye apho kuthe tye emehlweni akho ukuya khona.
Umthetheli wabasiki wamnika umxhesho nesipho, wamndulula.

<span id="an_40:6">40:6</span> UYeremiya waya kuGedaliya unyana
ka-Ahikam eMizpa, wahlala naye phakathi kwabantu ababesele elizweni.

<span id="an_40:7">40:7</span> Ke kaloku beva bonke abathetheli bezimpi
ezisendle, bona namadoda abo, ukuba ukumkani waseBhabheli umenze
umveleli welizwe uGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, nokuba umenze umveleli
wamadoda, nabafazi, nabantwana, nezisweli zelizwe,
kwababengafuduselwanga eBhabheli.

<span id="an_40:8">40:8</span> Beza ke kuGedaliya eMizpa, inguIshmayeli
unyana kaNetaniya, noYohanan noYonatan oonyana bakaKareba, noSeraya
unyana kaTanumete, noonyana bakaEfayi waseNetofa, noYezaniya umntu
waseMahaka, bona namadoda abo.

<span id="an_40:9">40:9</span> UGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, unyana
kaShafan, wabafungela namadoda abo, esithi, Musani ukoyika ukuwakhonza
amaKaledi; hlalani kweli lizwe, nimkhonze ukumkani waseBhabheli, kulunge
kuni.

<span id="an_40:10">40:10</span> Yabonani, ndihleli eMizpa, ukuze ndime
phambi kwamaKaledi, aya kuza kuthi; ke nina hlanganisani iwayini,
neziqhamo zasehlotyeni, neoli, nibeke ezityeni zenu, nihlale emizini
yenu, enithe nayithimba.

<span id="an_40:11">40:11</span> NamaYuda onke abe ekwelakwaMowabhi,
nakoonyana baka-Amon, nakwelakwaEdom, nabasemazweni onke, eva ukuba
ukumkani waseBhabheli umise amasalela kwaYuda, nokuba umenze umveleli
wawo uGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, unyana kaShafan.

<span id="an_40:12">40:12</span> Abuya ke onke amaYuda, ezindaweni zonke
abegxothelwe kuzo, eza elizweni lakwaYuda kuGedaliya eMizpa, abutha
iwayini neziqhamo zasehlotyeni, zazininzi kakhulu.

<span id="an_40:13">40:13</span> Ke kaloku uYohanan unyana kaKareha,
nabathetheli bonke bezimpi ababesemaphandleni, beza kuGedaliya eMizpa.

<span id="an_40:14">40:14</span> Bathi kuye, Uhleli usazi na ukuba
uBhahalisi, ukumkani woonyana baka-Amon, uthume uIshmayeli unyana
kaNetaniya, ukuba akubulale? Ke uGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam ubengakholwa
ngabo.

<span id="an_40:15">40:15</span> UYohanan unyana kaKareha wathetha
kuGedaliya ngasese eMizpa, wathi, Makhe ndiye ndimbulale uIshmayeli
unyana kaNetaniya, kungazi mntu; yini na ukuba ade abulale wena,
achithwachithwe amaYuda onke ahlanganisene kuwe, atshabalale amasalela
akwaYuda?

<span id="an_40:16">40:16</span> UGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam wathi
kuYohanan unyana kaKareha, Musa ukuyenza loo nto; ngokuba uthetha
ubuxoki ngoIshmayeli.

<span id="an_41:1">41:1</span> Kwathi ngenyanga yesixhenxe, weza
uIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya, unyana kaElishama, wasembewini yokumkani,
wakubathetheli bokumkani, enamadoda alishumi, kuGedaliya unyana
ka-Ahikam eMizpa; badla isonka ndawonye eMizpa apho.

<span id="an_41:2">41:2</span> Wesuka uIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya,
namadoda alishumi abenaye, wamxabela uGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, unyana
kaShafan, ngekrele; wambulala ke obenziwe umveleli ngukumkani
waseBhabheli ezweni eli;

<span id="an_41:3">41:3</span> namaYuda onke abenaye, abenoGedaliya
eMizpa, namaKaledi awafunyanwayo khona, angamadoda okulwa, wawabulala
uIshmayeli.

<span id="an_41:4">41:4</span> Kwathi ke ngomhla wesibini emva
kokubulawa kukaGedaliya, kungazi mntu,

<span id="an_41:5">41:5</span> kwafika amadoda evela kwaShekem naseShilo
nakwaSamari, amadoda angamashumi asibhozo, eguye iindevu, ezikrazule
iingubo, ezicentile, eneminikelo yokudla nentlaka emhlophe ezandleni
zawo, eyizisa endlwini kaYehova.

<span id="an_41:6">41:6</span> Waphuma eMizpa uIshmayeli unyana
kaNetaniya, waya kuwakhawulela, emana ehamba elila. Kwathi, akufika
kuwo, wathi kuwo, Yizani kuGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam.

<span id="an_41:7">41:7</span> Kwathi, akufika phakathi komzi,
wawabulala uIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya, wawalahlela emhadini phakathi,
yena namadoda lawo abenaye.

<span id="an_41:8">41:8</span> Ke kwafumaneka kuwo amadoda alishumi,
awathi kuIshmayeli, Musa ukusibulala, ngokuba sinezisele endle
ezinengqolowa, nerhasi, neoli, nobusi. Wawayeka ke, akawabulala phakathi
kwabazalwana bawo.

<span id="an_41:9">41:9</span> Ke kaloku umhadi, apho uIshmayeli
wazilahlela kuwo ngakuGedaliya zonke izidumbu zamadoda abewabulele (lowo
wawenzayo ukumkani uAsa ngenxa kaBhahesha ukumkani wakwaSirayeli),
uIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya wawuzalisa ngababuleweyo.

<span id="an_41:10">41:10</span> UIshmayeli wawathimba onke amasalela
abantu abaseMizpa, iintombi zokumkani, nabantu bonke ababesele eMizpa,
abenziwe umveleli wabo uGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam nguNebhuzaradan,
umthetheli wabasiki; wabathimba ke uIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya,
wahamba, wawelela koonyana baka-Amon.

<span id="an_41:11">41:11</span> Weva uYohanan unyana kaKareha,
nabathetheli bonke bezimpi ezibe zinaye, bonke ububi awabenzayo
uIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya;

<span id="an_41:12">41:12</span> bawathabatha onke amadoda, baya kulwa
noIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya, bamfumana ngasemanzini amakhulu
aseGibheyon.

<span id="an_41:13">41:13</span> Kwathi, bonke abantu abanoIshmayeli,
bakumbona uYohanan unyana kaKareha, nabathetheli bezimpi ezinaye,
bavuya;

<span id="an_41:14">41:14</span> bajika bonke abantu abebathimbe eMizpa
uIshmayeli, babuya baya kuYohanan unyana kaKareha.

<span id="an_41:15">41:15</span> Ke uIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya
wasinda, enamadoda asibhozo, ebusweni bukaYohanan, waya koonyana
baka-Amon.

<span id="an_41:16">41:16</span> Wawathabatha uYohanan unyana kaKareha,
nabathetheli bonke bezimpi ababenaye, onke amasalela abantu,
awababuyisayo kuIshmayeli unyana kaNetaniya eMizpa, emveni kokuba
ebembulele uGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, amagorha, amadoda okulwa,
nabafazi, nabantwana, namathenwa, abewabuyisile eGibheyon.

<span id="an_41:17">41:17</span> Baya bahlala endlwini yabaphambukeli
kaKimham engaseBhetelehem, ukuba baye kungena eYiputa, ngenxa
yamaKaledi.

<span id="an_41:18">41:18</span> Ngokuba babewoyika, ngokuba uIshmayeli
unyana kaNetaniya ebembulele uGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, owayenziwe
umveleli welizwe ngukumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_42:1">42:1</span> Basondela bonke abathetheli bezimpi:
ooYohanan unyana kaKareha, noYezaniya unyana kaHoshaya, nabantu bonke,
bethabathela komncinane base komkhulu.

<span id="an_42:2">42:2</span> Bathi kuYeremiya umprofeti, Ukutarhuzisa
kwethu makhe kuwe phambi kwakho, usithandazele kuYehova uThixo wakho,
uthandazele la masalela onke; ngokuba sisele sambalwa, besibaninzi,
njengoko asibonayo amehlo akho;

<span id="an_42:3">42:3</span> uYehova uThixo wakho asixelele indlela
esingahamba ngayo, nento esingayenzayo.

<span id="an_42:4">42:4</span> Wathi uYeremiya umprofeti kubo, Ndivile;
yabonani, ndiya kuthandaza kuYehova uThixo wenu ngokwamazwi enu; kuthi
onke amazwi aniphendule ngawo uYehova, ndinixelele; andiyi kunivimba
lizwi.

<span id="an_42:5">42:5</span> Bathi bona kuYeremiya, UYehova makabe
lingqina elinyanisileyo, elithembekayo, ngathi, ukuba asithanga senze
ngokwelizwi lonke, awokuthuma lona kuthi uYehova uThixo wakho.

<span id="an_42:6">42:6</span> Nokuba lilungile, nokuba libi, siya
kuliphulaphula ilizwi likaYehova uThixo wethu, esikuthumela kuye; ukuze
kulunge kuthi, xa siliphulaphulayo ilizwi likaYehova uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_42:7">42:7</span> Kwathi ekupheleni kwemihla elishumi,
kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya.

<span id="an_42:8">42:8</span> Wabiza uYohanan unyana kaKareha,
nabathetheli bonke bezimpi ababenaye, nabantu bonke, bathabathela
komncinane, besa komkhulu.

<span id="an_42:9">42:9</span> Wathi kubo, Utsho uYehova, uThixo
kaSirayeli, enindithumele kuye, ukuba ndiwise ukutarhuzisa kwenu phambi
kwakhe, ukuthi,

<span id="an_42:10">42:10</span> Ukuba nithe nahlala kweli lizwe,
ndonakha, ndinganigungxuli; ndonityala, ndinganinyothuli; ngokuba
ndiyazohlwaya ngenxa yobubi endibenzileyo kuni.

<span id="an_42:11">42:11</span> Musani ukumoyika ukumkani waseBhabheli,
lowo nimoyikayo; musani ukumoyika, utsho uYehova; ngokuba ndinani, ukuba
ndinisindise, ndinihlangule esandleni sakhe.

<span id="an_42:12">42:12</span> Ndiya kunenzela imfesane, abe nemfesane
kuni, anibuyisele emhlabeni wakowenu.

<span id="an_42:13">42:13</span> Ke ukuba nithe, Asisayi, kuhlala kweli
lizwe, analiphulaphula izwi likaYehova uThixo wenu, nathi,

<span id="an_42:14">42:14</span> Hayi, thina siya kuya ezweni leYiputa,
ukuze singabonani namfazwe, singaliva nezwi lesigodlo, singalambeli
sonka, sihlale khona ke:

<span id="an_42:15">42:15</span> ngako oko kaloku liveni ilizwi
likaYehova, masalela akwaYuda. Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Ukuba nithe nabubhekisa kwaphela ubuso benu eYiputa,
naya kuphambukela khona, ikrele,

<span id="an_42:16">42:16</span> eniloyikayo, lonifikela nakhona ezweni
leYiputa; nendlala leyo, ninesithukuthezi ngayo, yothi nama kuni
ukunilandela eYiputa, nifele khona.

<span id="an_42:17">42:17</span> Namadoda onke, abubhekise ubuso bawo
eYiputa, ukuba aphambukele khona, aya kufa likrele, nayindlala,
nayindyikitya yokufa, kungasali nanye kuwo, isindayo ebubini
endiwazisela bona.

<span id="an_42:18">42:18</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Njengoko waphalazekayo umsindo wam nobushushu bam
phezu kwabemi baseYerusalem, buya kwenjenjalo ukuphalazeka ubushushu bam
phezu kwenu ekuyeni kwenu eYiputa; nibe yintshwabulo, nesimanga,
nentshabhiso, nesingcikivo, ningabi sayibona le ndawo.

<span id="an_42:19">42:19</span> UYehova uthethile kuni, masalela
akwaYuda; musani ukuya eYiputa; yazini nazi, ukuba ndiqononondisile
ukuthetha kuni namhla.

<span id="an_42:20">42:20</span> Ngokuba niyikhohlisile imiphefumlo
yenu. Xa nindithumele kuYehova uThixo wenu, nisithi, Sithandazele
kuYehova uThixo wethu; njengoko konke awokuthetha kuthi uYehova uThixo
wethu, sixelele njengoko, sokwenza;

<span id="an_42:21">42:21</span> ndinixelele ke namhla. Ke
aniliphulaphulanga ilizwi likaYehova uThixo wenu ngako konke
awandithumelayo ngako kuni.

<span id="an_42:22">42:22</span> Kungokunje yazini ukuba niya kufa
likrele, nayindlala, nayindyikitya yokufa, kuloo ndawo ningxamele ukuya
kuyo, ukuba niphambukele kuyo.

<span id="an_43:1">43:1</span> Kwathi, akugqiba uYeremiya ukuwathetha
ebantwini bonke amazwi onke kaYehova uThixo wabo, awamthuma wona uYehova
uThixo wabo kubo, onke la mazwi,

<span id="an_43:2">43:2</span> batsho ooAzariya unyana kaHoshaya,
noYohanan unyana kaKareha, namadoda onke akhukhumeleyo, ukuthi
kuYeremiya, Uthetha ubuxoki; uYehova uThixo wethu akakuthumanga kuthi,
ukuba uthi, Ze ningayi eYiputa niphambukele khona;

<span id="an_43:3">43:3</span> uBharuki ke, unyana kaNeriya, uya
kuxhokonxa ngakuthi, kuba efuna ukuba sinikelwe esandleni samaKaledi,
ukuba asibulale, ukuba asifudusele eBhabheli.

<span id="an_43:4">43:4</span> UYohanan unyana kaKareha, nabo bonke
abathetheli bezimpi, nabantu bonke, abaliphulaphula ilizwi likaYehova
lokuba bahlale elizweni lakwaYuda.

<span id="an_43:5">43:5</span> UYohanan unyana kaKareha, nabo bonke
abathetheli bezimpi, bawathabatha onke amasalela akwaYuda, abebuye evela
ezintlangeni zonke abegxothelwe kuzo, ukuba aye kuphambukela ezweni
lakwaYuda:

<span id="an_43:6">43:6</span> amadoda, nabafazi, nabantwana, neentombi
zokumkani, nemiphefumlo yonke abeyishiye uNebhuzaradan, umthetheli
wabasiki, kuGedaliya unyana ka-Ahikam, unyana kaShafan, noYeremiya
umprofeti, noBharuki unyana kaNeriya.

<span id="an_43:7">43:7</span> Baya ke elizweni laseYiputa, ngokuba
babengaliphulaphulanga izwi likaYehova; baya bafika eTapanesi.

<span id="an_43:8">43:8</span> Kwafika ilizwi likaYehova kuYeremiya
eTapanesi, lisithi,

<span id="an_43:9">43:9</span> Thabatha ngesandla sakho amatye amakhulu,
uwaqhusheke eludakeni endaweni yokutshisa izitena, esemnyango wendlu
kaFaro eTapanesi, emehlweni amadoda akwaYuda.

<span id="an_43:10">43:10</span> Uze uthi kuwo, Utsho uYehova wemikhosi,
uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiya kuthumela ndithabathe
uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, umkhonzi wam, ndiyibeke itrone
yakhe ngaphezu kwala matye ndiwaqhushekileyo; aneke isivatho sakhe
esihle ngaphezu kwawo.

<span id="an_43:11">43:11</span> Uya kufika alibethe ilizwe leYiputa,
owokufa afe, owokuthinjwa athinjwe, owekrele abe ngowekrele.

<span id="an_43:12">43:12</span> Ndiya kufaka isikhuni ezindlwini
zoothixo baseYiputa, azitshise zona, abathimbe bona, azithi wambu
ngelizwe leYiputa, njengokuba umalusi ezithi wambu ngengubo yakhe;
aphume kulo enoxolo.

<span id="an_43:13">43:13</span> Uya kuwaqhekeza amatye amisiweyo
aseBhete-shemeshe, asezweni leYiputa, azitshise ngomlilo izindlu
zoothixo baseYiputa.

<span id="an_44:1">44:1</span> Ilizwi elafikayo kuYeremiya
ngokusingisele kumaYuda onke ahleliyo ezweni laseYiputa, ahleli
eMigidoli, naseTapanesi, naseNofu, nasezweni lasePatrosi, lalisithi:

<span id="an_44:2">44:2</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Nibubonile ububi bonke endayizisela bona iYerusalem,
nemizi yonke yakwaYuda. Niyabona, ingamanxuwa ngayo le mini, akukho
umiyo kuyo;

<span id="an_44:3">44:3</span> ngenxa yobubi ababenzayo, ukuze
bandiqumbise ngokuya kuqhumisela nokukhonza thixo bambi, ababengabazi
bona, nani, nooyihlo.

<span id="an_44:4">44:4</span> Ndathumela kuni bonke abakhonzi bam
abaprofeti, ndibathuma ndivuka kusasa, ndisithi, Musani ukukha niyenze
le nto ingamasikizi, ndiyithiyileyo.

<span id="an_44:5">44:5</span> Noko ke abevanga, abayithobanga indlebe
yabo, ukuba babuye ebubini babo, bangaqhumiseli thixweni bambi.

<span id="an_44:6">44:6</span> Baphalazeka ke ubushushu bam nomsindo
wam, watshisa emizini yakwaYuda nasezitratweni zeYerusalem; yaba
linxuwa, yabharha, njengoku kunjalo namhla.

<span id="an_44:7">44:7</span> Kaloku utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yini na ukuba niyenzele ububi obukhulukangaka
imiphefumlo yenu, bokunqumla kuni indoda nomfazi, umntwana nosebeleni,
kwelakwaYuda, kungasali masalela kuni;

<span id="an_44:8">44:8</span> ngokundiqumbisa ngezenzo zezandla zenu,
ngokuqhumisela thixweni bambi ezweni laseYiputa, eneza kuphambukela
kulo; ukuze nizinqumle ngokwenu, nibe yintshabhiso nesingcikivo
ezintlangeni zonke zehlabathi?

<span id="an_44:9">44:9</span> Nizilibele na izinto ezimbi zooyihlo;
izinto ezimbi zookumkani bakwaYuda, nezinto ezimbi zabafazi babo,
nezinto ezimbi zenu ngokwenu, nezinto ezimbi zabafazi benu, abazenzayo
ezweni lakwaYuda nasezitratweni zeYerusalem?

<span id="an_44:10">44:10</span> Unanamhla abatyumkanga, aboyikanga,
abahambanga ngomyalelo wam nangemimiselo yam, endayibeka phambi kwenu
naphambi kooyihlo.

<span id="an_44:11">44:11</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova wemikhosi,
uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabonani, ubuso bam ndiya kububhekisa kuni,
ukuba kube kubi, anqunyulwe onke amaYuda.

<span id="an_44:12">44:12</span> Ndiya kuwathabatha amasalela akwaYuda,
abubhekisileyo ubuso bawo ekuyeni ezweni laseYiputa ukuba aphambukele
khona, agqitywe onke; aya kuwa ezweni leYiputa; aya kugqityelwa likrele
nayindlala, kuthabathele kwabancinane kuse kwabakhulu; aya kufa likrele
nayindlala, abe yintshwabulo, nommangaliso, nentshabhiso, nesingcikivo.

<span id="an_44:13">44:13</span> Ndiya kubavelela abahleli ezweni
leYiputa, njengoko ndayivelelayo iYerusalem ngekrele, nangendlala,
nangendyikitya yokufa.

<span id="an_44:14">44:14</span> Akuyi kubakho usindayo, usalayo,
kumasalela akwaYuda, abeze kuphambukela khona ezweni leYiputa, ukuba
abuyele ezweni lakwaYuda, elo lizwe ayiphakamisele kulo imiphefumlo yawo
ukubuyela kulo, ukuba ahlale khona; ngokuba abayi kubuya, ingengabasinda
ngokubhungca.

<span id="an_44:15">44:15</span> Amphendula uYeremiya onke amadoda,
abesazi ukuba abafazi bawo baqhumisela thixweni bambi, nabafazi bonke
ababemi esikhungwini esikhulu, nabantu bonke ababehleli ezweni leYiputa,
ePatrosi, ngokuthi,

<span id="an_44:16">44:16</span> Ilizwi elo ulithethileyo kuthi egameni
likaYehova, asiyi kukuphulaphula ngalo.

<span id="an_44:17">44:17</span> Inene, siya kuwenza onke amazwi
aphumileyo emlonyeni wethu, okuqhumisela kukumkanikazi wezulu,
simthululele iminikelo ethululwayo, njengoko sakwenzayo, thina noobawo,
ookumkani bethu nabathetheli bethu, emizini yakwaYuda, nasezitratweni
zaseYerusalem; sahlutha ke sisonka, salunga, asabona bubi.

<span id="an_44:18">44:18</span> Kususela koko sayekayo ukuqhumisela
kukumkanikazi wezulu, nokumthululela iminikelo ethululwayo, saswela
iinto zonke, sagqityelwa likrele nayindlala.

<span id="an_44:19">44:19</span> Xa ke thina bafazi siqhumiselayo
kukumkanikazi wezulu, simthululelayo iminikelo ethululwayo, simenzela
izonkana zokuba eyilwa, simthululela iminikelo ethululwayo, amadoda ethu
akakho na kuthi?

<span id="an_44:20">44:20</span> Wathetha uYeremiya kubantu bonke,
kumadoda nakubafazi, kubantu bonke abamphendulayo ngelo lizwi, wathi,

<span id="an_44:21">44:21</span> Ukuqhumisela oko enaqhumisela ngako
emizini yakwaYuda nasezitratweni zaseYerusalem, nina nooyihlo, ookumkani
benu nabathetheli benu, nabantu belizwe, akakukhumbulanga na uYehova?
Akuthanga qatha na entliziyweni yakhe oko?

<span id="an_44:22">44:22</span> UYehova akaba saba nako ukuthwala,
ngenxa yeentlondi zenu ezimbi, ngenxa yamasikizi enawenzayo; lasuka
ilizwe lenu labharha, kwaba senkangala, langummangaliso nentshabhiso,
lingenammi, njengoko kunjalo namhla.

<span id="an_44:23">44:23</span> Ngenxa yokuqhumisela kwenu, nangenxa
yokona kwenu kuYehova, analiphulaphula izwi likaYehova, anahamba
ngomyalelo wakhe, nangemimiselo yakhe, nangezingqino zakhe: ngenxa yoko
bunihlele obo bubi, njengoko kunjalo namhla.

<span id="an_44:24">44:24</span> Wathi uYeremiya kubantu bonke,
nakubafazi bonke, Liveni ilizwi likaYehova, nonke maYuda asezweni
leYiputa;

<span id="an_44:25">44:25</span> utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Nina nabafazi benu niyathetha ngomlomo wenu,
nangezandla zenu nikuzalise, nisithi, Masenze izibhambathiso zethu,
esabhambathisa ngazo, zokuqhumisela kukumkanikazi wezulu, simthululele
iminikelo ethululwayo:

<span id="an_44:26">44:26</span> zimiseni nizimise kambe izibhambathiso
zenu; zenzeni nizenze kambe izibhambathiso zenu. Ngako oko liveni ilizwi
likaYehova, nonke maYuda, ahleliyo ezweni leYiputa: Yabonani, ndifunge
igama lam elikhulu, utsho uYehova, inene, aliyi kuba sabizwa igama lam
ngumlomo kabani wakwaYuda ezweni lonke leYiputa, esithi, Ihleli nje
iNkosi.

<span id="an_44:27">44:27</span> Yabonani, ndiwaphaphela ukuba kube
kubi, kungalungi, agqityelwe onke amadoda akwaYuda ezweni laseYiputa,
likrele nayindlala, ade aphele.

<span id="an_44:28">44:28</span> Baya kubuya ezweni leYiputa abasinde
ekreleni, baye ezweni lakwaYuda bembalwa; alazi onke amasalela akwaYuda,
azileyo ezweni leYiputa ukuba aphambukele kulo, ukuba liliphi na ilizwi
eliya kuma khona: lelam, lelabo, kusini na.

<span id="an_44:29">44:29</span> Nangu ke umqondiso kuni, utsho uYehova,
wokuba ndiya kunivelela kule ndawo, ukuze nazi ukuba amazwi am aya kuma,
animele ububi.

<span id="an_44:30">44:30</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani,
ndiyamnikela uFaro-hofra, ukumkani weYiputa, esandleni seentshaba zakhe,
esandleni sabafuna umphefumlo wakhe, njengoko ndamnikelayo uZedekiya
ukumkani wakwaYuda esandleni sikaNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli,
utshaba lwakhe, olube lufuna umphefumlo wakhe.

<span id="an_45:1">45:1</span> Ilizwi awalithethayo uYeremiya umprofeti
kuBharuki unyana kaNeriya, ekuwabhaleni kwakhe encwadini la mazwi,
ephuma emlonyeni kaYeremiya, ngomnyaka wesine kaYoyakim unyana kaYosiya,
ukumkani wakwaYuda, lalisithi,

<span id="an_45:2">45:2</span> Utsho uYehova, uThixo kaSirayeli, kuwe,
Bharuki, ukuthi, Wena uthi, Athi ke mna!

<span id="an_45:3">45:3</span> Ngokuba uYehova wongeza isingqala
kumvandedwa wam; ndidiniwe kukuncwina kwam, andifumani kuphumla.

<span id="an_45:4">45:4</span> Yithi ke kuye, Utsho uYehova ukuthi,
Yabona, into endiyakhileyo ndiyayigungxula, into endiyityeleyo
ndiyayinyothula; lihlabathi lonke ke elo.

<span id="an_45:5">45:5</span> Wena uzifunela izinto ezinkulu; musa
ukuzifuna. Ngokuba, uyabona, ndiyizisela ububi inyama yonke, utsho
uYehova; ke ndikunika umphefumlo wakho ube lixhoba lakho, ezindaweni
zonke oya kuya kuzo.

<span id="an_46:1">46:1</span> Into eyafikayo kuYeremiya umprofeti,
ililizwi likaYehova ngokusingisele kwiintlanga.

<span id="an_46:2">46:2</span> ElingeYiputa, ngokusingisele kwimpi
kaFaro-neko ukumkani weYiputa, ebisemlanjeni ongumEfrati, eKarkemishe,
awayixabelayo uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, ngomnyaka wesine
kaYehoyakim unyana kaYosiya, ukumkani wakwaYuda, lalisithi:

<span id="an_46:3">46:3</span> Lungisani ingweletshetshe nekhaka, yiyani
kulwa.

<span id="an_46:4">46:4</span> Bophani amahashe ezinqwelweni zokulwa,
khwelani nina bamahashe; zimiseni ninezigcina-ntloko, khazimlisani
izikhali, ninxibe iingubo zentsimbi.

<span id="an_46:5">46:5</span> Yini? ndibona ntoni? Baqhiphuka umbilini,
babuya umva; amagorha abo aqotyiwe; basaba intsabo kanye, bangabi
saphethula; kukunxunguphala ngeenxa zonke; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_46:6">46:6</span> Makangasabi onamendu, lingasindi igorha;
ngasentla, ngasemlanjeni ongumEfrati, bakhubeke bawa.

<span id="an_46:7">46:7</span> Ngubani na lo unyuka njengoMnayile,
umanzi azamazama njengemilambo?

<span id="an_46:8">46:8</span> IYiputa iyenyuka njengoMnayile, amanzi
ayo ayazamazama njengemilambo. Ithi, Ndiya kunyuka, ndiya kuwugubungela
umhlaba; ndiya kuyitshabalalisa imizi nabemi bayo.

<span id="an_46:9">46:9</span> Qakathani, mahashe; nidlongozele,
zinqwelo zokulwa. Makaphume amagorha, amaKushi namaPuti aphethe
ingweletshetshe, namaLudi, aphethe atyede isaphetha.

<span id="an_46:10">46:10</span> Le mini yeyeNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi;
yimini yempindezelo, yokuphindezela kubabandezeli bakhe; lidle lihluthe
ikrele, lisele lidikwe ligazi labo; ngokuba inombingelelo iNkosi,
uYehova wemikhosi, ezweni lasentla, emlanjeni ongumEfrati.

<span id="an_46:11">46:11</span> Nyuka uye eGiliyadi, thabatha amafutha
aqholiweyo, nkazanandini, ntombi iyiYiputa; ufumana usandisa oomathunga;
akunakubotshwa.

<span id="an_46:12">46:12</span> Iintlanga zikuvile ukucukucezwa kwakho,
ukukhala kwakho kwazalisa ihlabathi; ngokuba igorha likhubeka egorheni,
omabini awa ndaweni-nye.

<span id="an_46:13">46:13</span> Ilizwi awalithethayo uYehova kuYeremiya
umprofeti, ngokuza kukaNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, ukuba
alixabele ilizwe laseYiputa, lalisithi:

<span id="an_46:14">46:14</span> Xelani eYiputa, nivakalise eMigidoli,
nivakalise eNofu naseTapanesi; yithini, Misa, xhoba; ngokuba ikrele liya
kudla ngeenxa zonke kuwe.

<span id="an_46:15">46:15</span> Yini na ukuba ziqwelwe iimbalasane
zakho? Azimanga, ngokuba uYehova uzingqulile.

<span id="an_46:16">46:16</span> Ukhubekisa abaninzi, ewe, omnye uwela
omnye; bathi, Sukani, masibuyele ebantwini bakowethu, ezweni esazalelwa
kulo, ngenxa yekrele elidlavulayo.

<span id="an_46:17">46:17</span> Badanduluka khona, bathi, UFaro
ukumkani weYiputa utshabile; ulidlulisile ixesha elimisiweyo.

<span id="an_46:18">46:18</span> Ndihleli nje, utsho ukumkani, ogama
lakhe linguYehova wemikhosi, ukuthi, Inene, uya kuza enjengeTabhore
phakathi kweentaba, enjengeKarmele ngaselwandle.

<span id="an_46:19">46:19</span> Zenzele iimpahla zemfuduka, mmi, ntombi
iyiYiputa; ngokuba iNofu iya kuba linxuwa, itshiswe, ingabi nammi.

<span id="an_46:20">46:20</span> IYiputa lithokazi elihle kakhulu;
isibawu sasentla siyeza, siyeza.

<span id="an_46:21">46:21</span> Kanjalo imikhosi yayo eqeshiweyo
phakathi kwayo injengamathole asesitalini; inene, nayo leyo ijikile,
iyasaba kunye, ayimi; ngokuba uyifikele umhla wokusindeka kwayo, ixesha
lokuvelelwa kwayo.

<span id="an_46:22">46:22</span> Isandi sayo sinjengokuhamba kwenyoka;
ngokuba bahamba ngobukroti, bayifikele ngezixengxe njengabagawuli
bemithi.

<span id="an_46:23">46:23</span> Bagawula ihlathi layo, utsho uYehova,
nokuba lithe shinyi; ngokuba baninzi ngaphezu kweenkumbi, abanakubalwa.

<span id="an_46:24">46:24</span> Intombi eyiYiputa ihlazekile, inikelwe
esandleni sabantu belasentla.

<span id="an_46:25">46:25</span> Uthi uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, Yabona, ndiyamvelela uAmon waseNo, noFaro, neYiputa,
noothixo bayo, nobukumkani bayo, kwauFaro nabakholose ngaye.

<span id="an_46:26">46:26</span> Ndobanikela esandleni sabafuna
umphefumlo wabo, esandleni sikaNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli,
nasesandleni sabakhonzi bakhe; emveni koko imiwe njengokwemihla
yamandulo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_46:27">46:27</span> Ke wena musa ukoyika, mkhonzi wam
Yakobi; ungaqhiphuki umbilini, Sirayeli; ngokuba, uyabona, ndiya
kukusindisa kwakude, nembewu yakho ezweni ethinjelwe kulo, abuye
uYakobi, azole, onwabe, angagubhi.

<span id="an_46:28">46:28</span> Musa ukoyika, wena mkhonzi wam Yakobi,
utsho uYehova; ngokuba ndinawe; ngokuba ndiya kuzigqibela kuphele
iintlanga zonke endikugxothele kuzo. Ke wena andiyi kukugqibela kuphele;
ndokuthethisa ngokusesikweni; andiyi kuthi umsulwa.

<span id="an_47:1">47:1</span> Into eyafikayo kuYeremiya umprofeti,
ililizwi likaYehova ngokusingisele kumaFilisti, uFaro engekayixabeli
iGaza, yaye iyile:

<span id="an_47:2">47:2</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabona, kunyuka
entla amanzi angumlambo ongumkhukula, ontywilisela ilizwe nenzaliseko
yalo, imizi nabemi bayo; sikhale isintu, babhomboloze bonke abemi
belizwe.

<span id="an_47:3">47:3</span> Ngenxa yesingqi sokunyathela kwamanqina
eembalasane zamahashe akhe, ngenxa yokugoqoza kweenqwelo zakhe zokulwa,
ngokuxokozela kweevili zakhe, ooyise abasabheki koonyana ngokuwa
kwezandla;

<span id="an_47:4">47:4</span> ngenxa yemini eza kuwabhuqa onke
amaFilisti, eza kunqumla eTire neTsidon bonke abasale banceda; ngokuba
uYehova uyawabhuqa amaFilisti, amasalela onxweme lwaseKafetori.

<span id="an_47:5">47:5</span> Isezileni iGaza, itshabalele iAshkelon,
amasalela entili yabo.

<span id="an_47:6">47:6</span> Kunini na uzicenta? Awu! Krele
likaYehova, kunini na ungaphezi? Rhoxela esingxotyeni sakho; phumla,
uthi cwaka.

<span id="an_47:7">47:7</span> Ungathini na ukupheza, uYehova ekuwisele
umthetho nje? EAshkelon naselunxwemeni lolwandle, apho ukuyalele.

<span id="an_48:1">48:1</span> Ngokusingisele kwelakwaMowabhi, utsho
uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi: Yeha iNebho, ngokuba
ibhuqiwe. Ihlazisiwe, ithinjiwe iKiriyatayim; ihlazekile, iqhiphuke
umbilini ingxonde leyo.

<span id="an_48:2">48:2</span> Iqhayiya lakwaMowabhi alisekho; eHeshbhon
bacebe ububi ngaye, bathi, Yizani simnqumle, angabi luhlanga. Nawe,
Mademena, uya kudaka; ikrele liya kukulandela.

<span id="an_48:3">48:3</span> Phulaphulani ukukhala eHoronayim! Yimbuqo
nokwaphuka okukhulu!

<span id="an_48:4">48:4</span> UMowabhi waphukile, iimbedlenge zakhe
zivakala zikhala.

<span id="an_48:5">48:5</span> Ngokuba ekunyukeni eqhineni laseLuhoti,
baya kulila, balile; ngokuba ekuhleni eHoronayim ababandezelwa baya
kuvakala bekhaliswa kukwaphulwa.

<span id="an_48:6">48:6</span> Sabani, sizani imiphefumlo yenu, yibani
njengoze entlango.

<span id="an_48:7">48:7</span> Ngenxa enokuba ukholose ngezenzo zakho
nangobuncwane bakho, nawe uya kuthinjwa, aphume afuduswe uKemoshe,
ababingeleli bakhe nabathetheli bakhe kunye.

<span id="an_48:8">48:8</span> Uya kufika umbhuqi emizini yonke,
kungasindi mzi, idake intili, litshabalale ihewu, njengoko watshoyo
uYehova.

<span id="an_48:9">48:9</span> Mnikeni amaphiko uMowabhi; ngokuba
wophuma ebaleka, imizi yakhe ibe ngamanxuwa, ingemiwa.

<span id="an_48:10">48:10</span> Makaqalekiswe owenza umsebenzi kaYehova
ngokudangala, aqalekiswe onqanda ikrele lakhe egazini.

<span id="an_48:11">48:11</span> Wonwaba uMowabhi kwasebuncinaneni
bakhe, wee tywa phezu kweentsipho zakhe; akakhutshelwanga kwesinye
isitya, akahambanga efuduswa; ngenxa yoko isongo sakhe sihleli kuye,
nevumba lakhe aliguqukanga.

<span id="an_48:12">48:12</span> Ngako oko, yabonani, kuza imihla, utsho
uYehova, endiya kuthumela abathululi kuye, bamthulule, bazikhuphele
izitya zakhe, bayiqhekeze imiphanda yakhe.

<span id="an_48:13">48:13</span> Uya kudana uMowabhi nguKemoshe,
njengoko yadanayo indlu kaSirayeli yiBheteli, inkoloseko yayo.

<span id="an_48:14">48:14</span> Ningathini na ukuthi, Singamagorha,
singamadoda anobukroti emfazweni?

<span id="an_48:15">48:15</span> Uyabhuqwa uMowabhi, imizi yakhe
iyenyukwa, amadodana akhe anyuliweyo athobela ekusikweni; utsho uKumkani
ogama lakhe linguYehova wemikhosi.

<span id="an_48:16">48:16</span> Kusondele, kuza kufika, ukusindeka
kukaMowabhi; ububi bakhe buyangxama kakhulu.

<span id="an_48:17">48:17</span> Hlunguzelani iintloko ngaye, nonke nina
ningeenxa zonke kuye, nonke nina nilaziyo igama lakhe. Yithini, Yoo!
Itheni na ukwaphuka intonga yonamandla, uluthi lokuhomba.

<span id="an_48:18">48:18</span> Yihla eluzukweni, uhlale phantsi
kwelinenxano, mmi, ntombi yaseDibhon; ngokuba umbhuqi kaMowabhi unyuke
weza kuwe, uzonakalisile iinqaba zakho.

<span id="an_48:19">48:19</span> Yima ngasendleleni, ubonisele, mmi
waseArohere; buza kwindoda esabileyo nakwintokazi esindileyo; yithi,
Kukho ntoni na?

<span id="an_48:20">48:20</span> UMowabhi uhlazekile, ngokuba uqhiphuke
umbilini; bhombolozani nikhale; xelani eArnon, nithi, Ubhuqiwe uMowabhi.

<span id="an_48:21">48:21</span> Umgwebo ulifikele ilizwe lehewu, iHolon
neYatsa neMefahati;

<span id="an_48:22">48:22</span> neDibhon, neNebho,
neBhete-dibhelatayim;

<span id="an_48:23">48:23</span> neKiriyatayim, neBhete-gamuli,
neBhete-mehon;

<span id="an_48:24">48:24</span> neKeriyoti, neBhotsera, nemizi yonke
yelizwe lakwaMowabhi, ekude kwanekufuphi.

<span id="an_48:25">48:25</span> Luxakaxiwe uphondo lukaMowabhi, ingalo
yakhe yaphulwe; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_48:26">48:26</span> Mnxiliseni, ngokuba ezikhulisile
kuYehova; akhahleleke uMowabhi emhlanzweni wakhe, abe yintlekisa naye.

<span id="an_48:27">48:27</span> Wayengeyintlekisa na kuwe uSirayeli?
Wayefunyenwe phakathi kwamasela, kusini na, ukuba uhlunguzele intloko,
xa sukuba ubuthetha ngaye?

<span id="an_48:28">48:28</span> Shiyani imizi, nihlale ezingxondorheni,
bemi bakwaMowabhi, nibe njengevukuthu elakhela phesheya, eludinini
lomwonyo.

<span id="an_48:29">48:29</span> Silivile ikratshi likaMowabhi. Asikuko
nokuba likratshi: ukuzidla kwakhe, ikratshi lakhe, ukukratsha kwakhe,
nokuphakama kwentliziyo yakhe.

<span id="an_48:30">48:30</span> Mna ndiyakwazi ukuphuphuma komsindo
wakhe, nokuphololoza kwakhe into engeyiyo; utsho uYehova; benza into
engekhoyo.

<span id="an_48:31">48:31</span> Ngako oko ndiyabhomboloza ngenxa
kaMowabhi, ndikhale ngenxa kaMowabhi wonke ephela; bayancwina ngenxa
yamadoda aseKir-heres.

<span id="an_48:32">48:32</span> Ngaphezu kokulila kweYazere ndiya
kulilela wena, mdiliya waseSibhema, omasebe awela ulwandle, ada aya
kufika elwandle lwaseYazere; ekuvunweni kweziqhamo nasekuvunweni
kweediliya zakho kugaleleke umbhuqi.

<span id="an_48:33">48:33</span> Isukile imivuyo nemigcobo entsimini
echumayo, naselizweni lakwaMowabhi; ndiyiphelisile iwayini emkhombeni;
abayi kuxovula benamayeyeye; amayeyeye abo aya kuba ngamayeyeye
angelutho.

<span id="an_48:34">48:34</span> Ukukhala eHeshbhon kuse e-Elale, kuse
eYahazi; balikhuphile izwi labo, kuthabathele eTsohare kwesa eHoronayim,
nase-Egelati yesithathu; ngokuba kwanamanzi aseNimrim aya kuthi qoko.

<span id="an_48:35">48:35</span> Ndiya kumphelisa kwaMowabhi, utsho
uYehova, onyuka isiganga ukuba aqhumisele koothixo bakhe.

<span id="an_48:36">48:36</span> Ngako oko intliziyo yam iyalila
njengogwali ngenxa kaMowabhi; intliziyo yam iyalila njengogwali ngenxa
yamadoda aseKir-heres; ngako oko indyebo ababeyizuzile itshabalele.

<span id="an_48:37">48:37</span> Kuba zonke iintloko zigugulwe, zonke
iindevu zichetyiwe; ezandleni zonke ziintlanga, ezinqeni ziingubo
ezirhwexayo.

<span id="an_48:38">48:38</span> Phezu kwezindlu zonke zakwaMowabhi
nasezitratweni zakhe kukumbambazela kodwa; ngokuba ndimaphule uMowabhi
njengesitya esingananziweyo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_48:39">48:39</span> Bayabhomboloza; hayi, ukuqhiphuka
kwakhe umbilini! Hayi, ukunikela kukaMowabhi ikhosi kukudana!
Uyintlekisa, uyoyikwa ngabo bonke abangeenxa zonke kuye.

<span id="an_48:40">48:40</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Uyabona,
utshaba luyatshwebeleza njengexhalanga, lolule amaphiko alo phezu
koMowabhi.

<span id="an_48:41">48:41</span> Ithinjiwe iKeriyoti, zihluthiwe
iimboniselo. Ngaloo mini intliziyo yamagorha akwaMowabhi iya kuba
njengentliziyo yomfazi onenimba;

<span id="an_48:42">48:42</span> atshabalale uMowabhi, angabi ngaba ntu,
ngokuba ebezikhulisile kuYehova.

<span id="an_48:43">48:43</span> Ufikelwe lunkwantyo, nomgongxo,
nesibatha, mmi wakwaMowabhi; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_48:44">48:44</span> Osaba unkwantyo uya kweyela
emgongxweni; ophuma emgongxweni uya kubanjiswa sisibatha; ngokuba ndiya
kumzisela yena uMowabhi umnyaka wokuvelelwa kwakhe; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_48:45">48:45</span> Phantsi komthunzi weHeshbhon kuya kuma
abasabi abangenamandla; ngokuba kuya kuphuma umlilo eHeshbhon,
nelangatye phakathi kwaSihon, udle ummandla wakwaMowabhi nokakayi
lwabengxolo.

<span id="an_48:46">48:46</span> Yeha, wena Mowabhi! Batshabalele abantu
bakaKemoshe, ngokuba, oonyana bakho baya kuthatyathwa bethinjiwe,
neentombi zakho zisiwe ekuthinjweni.

<span id="an_48:47">48:47</span> Ke ndiya kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa
kukaMowabhi ekupheleni kwemihla; utsho uYehova. Uze wafika apha umgwebo
wakwaMowabhi.

<span id="an_49:1">49:1</span> Ngokusingisele koonyana baka-Amon, utsho
uYehova ukuthi: USirayeli akananyana na, akanandlalifa na? Yini na ukuba
ukumkani wabo amdle ilifa uGadi, abantu babo beme emizini yakhe?

<span id="an_49:2">49:2</span> Ngako oko, yabonani, kuza imihla, utsho
uYehova, endiya kuhlaba umkhosi wemfazwe kwiRabha yoonyana baka-Amon,
ibe ngumwewe wenxuwa, amagxamesi ayo atshiswe ngomlilo, uSirayeli abadle
ilifa ababemdle ilifa; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_49:3">49:3</span> Bhomboloza, Heshbhon, ngokuba ibhuqiwe
iAyi; khalani, magxamesi aseRabha, bhinqani ezirhwexayo; mbambazelani
niququzele kunye ezintangweni; ngokuba ukumkani wayo uya kuthinjwa,
kunye nababingeleli bakhe nabathetheli bakhe.

<span id="an_49:4">49:4</span> Uqhayiselani na ngazo iintili? Intili
yakho ichumile, ntombi iliphamba, yakholosayo ngobuncwane bayo, isithi,
Ndiya kuzelwa ngubani na?

<span id="an_49:5">49:5</span> Yabona, ndiya kukuzisela unkwantyo, itsho
iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi, luphuma kwabangeenxa zonke kuwe; nigxothwe,
elowo angabheki nokubheka, kungabikho ungababuthayo abaphalaphalayo.

<span id="an_49:6">49:6</span> Emveni koko ndiya kukubuyisa ukuthinjwa
koonyana baka-Amon; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_49:7">49:7</span> Ngokusingisele kuEdom, utsho uYehova
wemikhosi ukuthi: Akusekho bulumko na kwaTeman? Liphelile na icebo
kwiingqondi? Buphalele na ubulumko bazo?

<span id="an_49:8">49:8</span> Sabani, jikani, hlalani enkolontyweni,
bemi bakwaDedan; ngokuba ukusindeka kwakhe uEsawu ndimzisele, ixesha
lokumvelela kwam.

<span id="an_49:9">49:9</span> Ukuba abavuni beediliya bakufikele, abayi
kushiya lubhikico; ukuba amasela eza ebusuku, aya konakalisa ade anele.

<span id="an_49:10">49:10</span> Ngokuba mna ndimhlubile uEsawu,
ndizityhilile iindawo zakhe ezisitheleyo, angabi nako ukuzimela. Imbewu
yakhe iya kubhuqwa, abazalwana bakhe nabamelwane bakhe abakho.

<span id="an_49:11">49:11</span> Shiya iinkedama zakho; ndiya
kuziphilisa, bakholose ngam abahlolokazi bakho.

<span id="an_49:12">49:12</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabona,
ababengenalungelo lakuyisela indebe, inene baya kuyisela; wena ke ungoya
kuba msulwa, ube msulwa na? Akuyi kuba msulwa, ngokuba inene uya kusela.

<span id="an_49:13">49:13</span> Ngokuba ndizifungile mna, utsho
uYehova, ndathi, IBhotsera iya kuba ngummangaliso, nesingcikivo,
nenxuwa, nentshabhiso; nemizi yayo yonke ibe ngamanxuwa angunaphakade.

<span id="an_49:14">49:14</span> Ndive udaba luphuma kuYehova, kuthunywe
isigidimi ezintlangeni sokuthi, Zihlanganiseni, nimfikele, nisuke nilwe.

<span id="an_49:15">49:15</span> Ngokuba, uyabona, ndikwenze wamncinane
ezintlangeni, wadeleka phakathi kwezizwe.

<span id="an_49:16">49:16</span> Ukududuzelisa kwakho kukulukuhlile,
ukukhukhumala kwentliziyo yakho, wena uhleli ezimfanteni zengxondorha,
wena ubambe intlomo yenduli. Ngokuba uthe wayakhela phezulu
njengexhalanga indlu yakho, ndokuthoba apho; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_49:17">49:17</span> Uya kuba ngummangaliso uEdom; bonke
abadlula kuye baya kumangaliswa, benze umsondlo, ngenxa yokubethwa
kwakhe konke.

<span id="an_49:18">49:18</span> Njengoko kwabanjalo ekubhukuqekeni
kweSodom neGomora nemimelwane yayo, utsho uYehova, akuyi kuhlala mntu
khona, akuyi kuphambukela nyana womntu khona.

<span id="an_49:19">49:19</span> Yabona, utshaba luya kunyuka
njengengonyama ephuma ekweneni kweYordan, luye ekhayani eliyingxondorha;
ngokuba ndiya kumgxotha ngephanyazo kulo; osukuba enyuliwe, ndimenzele
umveleli; ngokuba ngubani na onjengam? ngubani na oya kundimema? ngubani
na loo malusi uya kuma phambi kwam?

<span id="an_49:20">49:20</span> Ngako oko yivani icebo likaYehova,
alicebileyo ngoEdom, neengcinga zakhe, azicingileyo ngabemi bakwaTeman;
inene, baya kuzikrwiqiliza ezincinane zomhlambi; inene, liya
kumangaliswa zizo ikriwa lazo.

<span id="an_49:21">49:21</span> Ihlabathi liyanyikima sisithonga sokuwa
kwabo; isandi sokukhala kwabo sivakala eLwandle oluBomvu.

<span id="an_49:22">49:22</span> Yabona, utshaba luyanyuka
njengexhalanga, lutshwebeleza, luwolule amaphiko alo phezu kweBhotsera;
intliziyo yamagorha ekwaEdom ngaloo mini iya kuba njengentliziyo yomfazi
onenimba.

<span id="an_49:23">49:23</span> Ngokusingisele kwiDamasko: Ihlazekile
iHamati neArpadi; ngokuba kuviwe iindaba ezimbi; bancamile;
njengaselwandle, banesithukuthezi, abanako ukuzola.

<span id="an_49:24">49:24</span> IDamasko ithe dakumba, ijikile yasaba;
ifikelwe kukothuka, ibanjwe yimbandezelo nayinimba njengozalayo.

<span id="an_49:25">49:25</span> Hayi, ukushiywa komzi wendumiso, umzi
wemihlali yam!

<span id="an_49:26">49:26</span> Ngako oko aya kuwa amadodana ayo
ezitratweni zawo, amadoda onke okulwa athi shwaka ngaloo mini; utsho
uYehova wemikhosi.

<span id="an_49:27">49:27</span> Ndiya kuphemba umlilo eludongeni
lweDamasko, udle iingxande ezinde zikaBhen-hadade.

<span id="an_49:28">49:28</span> Ngokusingisele kumaKedare,
nakwizikumkani zaseHatsore, awazibulalayo uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani
waseBhabheli, utsho uYehova ukuthi: Sukani nime, nyukani niye
kumaKedare, nibabhuqe abasempumalanga.

<span id="an_49:29">49:29</span> Iintente zabo nemihlambi yabo
boyithabatha; namalengalenga abo, neempahla zabo zonke, neenkamela zabo,
bozisusa zibe zezabo; bamemeze kubo, bathi, Kukunxunguphala ngeenxa
zonke.

<span id="an_49:30">49:30</span> Sabani, balekani kakhulu, hlalani
enkolontyweni, bemi baseHatsore, utsho uYehova; ngokuba
uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli ecebe icebo ngani, wacinga
ingcinga ngani.

<span id="an_49:31">49:31</span> Sukani nime, nyukani niye kuhlanga
oluchulumachileyo, oluhleli lukholosile, utsho uYehova; uhlanga
olungenazingcango namivalo, oluhleli lodwa.

<span id="an_49:32">49:32</span> Iinkamela zabo maziphangwe, ingxokolo
yemfuyo yabo ibe ngamaxhoba, ndibachithachithe kwimimoya yonke
onquthula-iinwele, ndibazisele ukusindeka, kuphuma kumacala onke; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_49:33">49:33</span> IHatsore iya kuba sisikhundla
seempungutye, kube senkangala kude kuse ephakadeni. Akuyi kuhlala bani
khona, kungaphambukeli nyana womntu khona.

<span id="an_49:34">49:34</span> Into eyafikayo kuYeremiya umprofeti,
ililizwi likaYehova ngokusingisele kwelakwaElam ekuqaleni kobukumkani
bukaZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda, yayisithi:

<span id="an_49:35">49:35</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi,
Yabonani, ndiyasaphula isaphetha sakwaElam, intlahlela yobugorha babo;

<span id="an_49:36">49:36</span> ndiya kulizisela elakwaElam imimoya
emine ephuma eziphelweni ezine zezulu, ndibachithachithe kuloo mimoya
yonke, kungabikho luhlanga bangayi kufika kulo abaziindlodlo zakwaElam.

<span id="an_49:37">49:37</span> Ndomqhiphukisa umbilini uElam phambi
kweentshaba zakhe, naphambi kwabafuna imiphefumlo yabo; ndibazisele
ububi, ukuvutha komsindo wam; utsho uYehova. Ndothuma emva kwabo ikrele,
ndide ndibagqibe,

<span id="an_49:38">49:38</span> Ndiya kumisa itrone yam kwaElam,
ndimtshabalalise khona ukumkani nabathetheli; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_49:39">49:39</span> Kuya kuthi ke ekupheleni kwemihla,
ndikubuyise ukuthinjwa kukaElam; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_50:1">50:1</span> Ilizwi awalithethayo uYehova
ngokusingisele kwiBhabheli, ngokusingisele kwilizwe lamaKaledi,
ngoYeremiya umprofeti, lalisithi:

<span id="an_50:2">50:2</span> Xelani ezintlangeni, nivakalise,
niphakamise ibhanile. Vakalisani, musani ukufihla; yithini, Ithinjiwe
iBhabheli, uhlazekile uBhele, uqhiphuke umbilini uMerodaki, zihlazekile
izithixo zabo, ziqhiphuke umbilini izigodo zabo.

<span id="an_50:3">50:3</span> Ngokuba kunyuke kweza kubo uhlanga
lwasentla, oluya kwenza ilizwe labo kube senkangala, lingabi nammi,
kuthabathele emntwini kuse ezinkomeni, kubalekwe kumkiwe.

<span id="an_50:4">50:4</span> Ngaloo mihla nangelo xesha, utsho
uYehova, baya kuza oonyana bakaSirayeli kunye noonyana bakaYuda, behamba
belila, baye bamquqele uYehova uThixo wabo.

<span id="an_50:5">50:5</span> Baya kubuza iZiyon, babheke khona,
besithi, Yizani, nithelele kuYehova ngomnqophiso ongunaphakade ongayi
kulityalwa.

<span id="an_50:6">50:6</span> Abantu bam baba ngumhlambi weegusha
ezilahlekileyo; abalusi babo babandwendwisela ezintabeni
eziphambanisayo, behamba besuka entabeni, baye endulini, bayilibale
indawo yabo yokubutha kwabo.

<span id="an_50:7">50:7</span> Bonke ababafumanayo babadla; ababandezeli
babo bathi, Asinatyala, ngethuba lokuba bonile kuYehova, ikriwa
lobulungisa, ithemba loyise, uYehova.

<span id="an_50:8">50:8</span> Balekani, niphume phakathi kweBhabheli;
mabaphume ezweni lamaKaledi, babe njengeenkunzi zeebhokhwe ezikhokela
umhlambi.

<span id="an_50:9">50:9</span> Ngokuba, yabonani, ndixhoxha, ndinyuse,
ndise eBhabheli isikhungu seentlanga ezinkulu, ziphuma ezweni lasentla,
ziyakhele uluhlu. Iya kuthinjwa apho, iintolo zaso zibe njengezegorha
eliligcisa, elingabuyi lilambatha.

<span id="an_50:10">50:10</span> Loba lixhoba elamaKaledi; bonke
abalithimbayo baya kuhlutha; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_50:11">50:11</span> Nakuba nivuya njalo, nakuba nidlamkile,
baphangi belifa lam, nakuba nidloba njengethokazi elibhulayo, nilila
njengeembalasane zamahashe:

<span id="an_50:12">50:12</span> uya kudana kakhulu unyoko; uya kuba
neentloni onizalayo. Yabonani, olokugqibela ezintlangeni luya kuba
yintlango, umqwebedu, inkqantosi.

<span id="an_50:13">50:13</span> Ngenxa yoburhalarhume bukaYehova
ayisayi kumiwa; kuya kuba senkangala kuyo yonke iphela. Bonke abadlulayo
eBhabheli baya kumangaliswa, benze umsondlo ngenxa yokubethwa kwayo
konke.

<span id="an_50:14">50:14</span> Yakheleni uluhlu iBhabheli ngeenxa
zonke, nonke batyedi besaphetha; tolani kuyo, ningashiyi lutolo; ngokuba
yonile kuYehova.

<span id="an_50:15">50:15</span> Dumani ngayo ngeenxa zonke; izinikele;
ziwile iingqoqo zayo, zidilikile iindonga zayo; ngokuba yimpindezelo
kaYehova. Phindezelani kuyo; njengokwenza kwayo, yenzani kuyo.

<span id="an_50:16">50:16</span> Nqumlani umhlwayeli eBhabheli, nophethe
irhengqa ngexesha lokuvuna. Ngenxa yekrele elidlavulayo elowo ubheka
ebantwini bakowabo, elowo usabela ezweni lakowabo.

<span id="an_50:17">50:17</span> Uyigusha elusali uSirayeli; ubhejethwe
ziingonyama. Ngukumkani waseAsiriya owaqala wamdla; ngoku, owokugqibela
umqobi wamathambo akhe nguNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_50:18">50:18</span> Ngako oko, utsho uYehova wemikhosi,
uThixo kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Yabonani, ndiyamvelela ukumkani waseBhabheli
nelizwe lakhe, njengoko ndamvelelayo ukumkani waseAsiriya.

<span id="an_50:19">50:19</span> Ndiya kumbuyisela uSirayeli ekriweni
lakhe, adle eKarmele naseBhashan, uhluthe umphefumlo wakhe ezintabeni
zakwaEfrayim nezaseGiliyadi.

<span id="an_50:20">50:20</span> Ngaloo mihla nangelo xesha, utsho
uYehova, buya kufunwa ubugwenxa bukaSirayeli, bungabikho; nezono
zikaYuda zingafumaneki; ngokuba ndiya kubaxolela endibasalisileyo.

<span id="an_50:21">50:21</span> Ilizwe lakwaNkani-ziphindwe-kabini,
nyuka uye kulo kanye, kubemi belakwaKohlwaywa; bharhisa usingele phantsi
emva kwabo, utsho uYehova; wenze ngako konke endakuwisela umthetho
ngako.

<span id="an_50:22">50:22</span> Isithonga semfazwe siselizweni,
nokwaphuka okukhulu.

<span id="an_50:23">50:23</span> Hayi, ukuxakaxwa, ukwaphulwa kwesando
sehlabathi lonke! Hayi, ukwenziwa kweBhabheli ummangaliso phakathi
kweentlanga!

<span id="an_50:24">50:24</span> Ndikuthiyele, wabanjiswa nokubanjiswa,
Bhabheli, ungazi ke wena; ufunyenwe, wathinjwa nokuthinjwa, ngokuba ulwe
noYehova.

<span id="an_50:25">50:25</span> UYehova uyivulile indlu yezixhobo
zakhe, wazikhupha iimpahla zokubhavuma kwakhe; ngokuba inomsebenzi
iNkosi, uYehova wemikhosi, ezweni lamaKaledi.

<span id="an_50:26">50:26</span> Yizani kulo, nivale ngeenxa zonke;
vulani amaqonga alo; lifumbeni ngokwezidimbilili, nilisingele phantsi,
kungasali nento kulo.

<span id="an_50:27">50:27</span> Hlabani zonke iinkunzi zalo ezintsha
zeenkomo; mazithotyelwe ekuxhelweni, Yeha ke bona! Ngokuba iyeza imini
yabo, ixesha lokuvelelwa kwabo.

<span id="an_50:28">50:28</span> Phulaphulani! Nabo abasabayo,
abasindayo ezweni laseBhabheli, ukuba baxele eZiyon impindezelo kaYehova
uThixo wethu, impindezelo yetempile yakhe.

<span id="an_50:29">50:29</span> Bahlabeleni umkhosi abatoli, beze
eBhabheli, bonke abatyedi besaphetha; yingqingeni ngeenxa zonke.
Makungabikho usindayo; yivuzeni ngokomsebenzi wayo; ngako konke
eyakwenzayo, yenzani ngako kuyo; ngokuba ikhukhumele kuYehova,
koyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_50:30">50:30</span> Ngako oko aya kuwa ezitratweni zayo
amadodana ayo, athi shwaka ngaloo mini onke amadoda ayo okulwa; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_50:31">50:31</span> Yabona, ndikuchasile, wena
ukhukhumeleyo, itsho iNkosi uYehova wemikhosi; ngokuba ifikile imini
yakho, ixesha lokukuvelela kwam.

<span id="an_50:32">50:32</span> Wokhubeka okhukhumeleyo, awe,
kungabikho umvusayo; ndiphembe umlilo emizini yakhe, utshe ngeenxa zonke
kuye.

<span id="an_50:33">50:33</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi,
Babecudiswa oonyana bakaSirayeli noonyana bakaYuda kunye; bonke
ababathimbayo bayagcinisa ukubabamba, abavumi ukubandulula.

<span id="an_50:34">50:34</span> UMkhululi wabo obamiselayo womelele,
ugama lakhe linguYehova wemikhosi; uya kubambana abambane nobambana
nabo, ukuze aliphumze ihlabathi, agungqise abemi baseBhabheli.

<span id="an_50:35">50:35</span> Ikrele maliwafikele amaKaledi, nabemi
baseBhabheli, nabathetheli bayo, nezilumko zayo; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_50:36">50:36</span> Ikrele malibafikele abaphololozi bento
engeyiyo, babe zizimathane; ikrele maliwafikele amagorha, aqhiphuke
umbilini.

<span id="an_50:37">50:37</span> Ikrele maliwafikele amahashe ayo,
neenqwelo zayo zokulwa, nomxukuxela wonke ophakathi kwayo, babe
ngabafazi; ikrele malibufikele ubuncwane bayo, ukuba buphangwe.

<span id="an_50:38">50:38</span> Ukubalela makuwafikele amanzi ayo,
ukuba atshe. Ngokuba lilizwe lemifanekiso eqingqiweyo; bazigezise
ngezinto ezothusayo.

<span id="an_50:39">50:39</span> Ngako oko kuya kuhlala khona
amarhamncwa omqwebedu neempungutye, kuhlale iinciniba khona, lingabi
samiwa naphakade, lingabi sahlalwa izizukulwana ngezizukulwana.

<span id="an_50:40">50:40</span> Njengoko wayibhukuqayo uThixo iSodom
neGomora, nemimelwane yayo, utsho uYehova, akuyi kuhlala bani khona,
akuyi kuphambukela nyana womntu khona.

<span id="an_50:41">50:41</span> Yabonani, kuza abantu, bevela entla,
uhlanga ke olukhulu; nookumkani abaninzi bayaxhoxhwa, bevela eziphelweni
zehlabathi.

<span id="an_50:42">50:42</span> Baphethe isaphetha nenkcula,
bazizijorha, abanamfesane; ilizwi labo liguguma njengolwandle, bakhwele
emahasheni, bekuxhobele njengendoda yokulwa, ntombi iyiBhabheli.

<span id="an_50:43">50:43</span> Uve iindaba zabo ukumkani waseBhabheli,
zasuka zawa izandla zakhe; imbandezelo imbambile, uyazibhijabhija
njengozalayo.

<span id="an_50:44">50:44</span> Yabonani, utshaba luya kunyuka
njengengonyama, luphume ekweneni kweYordan, luye ekhayeni
eliyingxondorha; ngokuba ndiya kumgxotha ngephanyazo kulo, osukuba
enyulwe, ndimenzele umveleli walo; ngokuba ngubani na onjengam? ngubani
na oya kundimema? ngubani na loo malusi uya kuma phambi kwam?

<span id="an_50:45">50:45</span> Ngako oko, liveni icebo likaYehova,
alicebileyo ngeBhabheli, neengcinga zakhe, azicingileyo ngelizwe
lamaKaledi; esithi, Inene, baya kuzikrwiqiliza ezincinane zomhlambi;
inene, liya kumangaliswa zizo ikriwa lazo.

<span id="an_50:46">50:46</span> Ngenxa yelizwi elithi, Ibanjiwe
iBhabheli, liyanyikima ihlabathi; kuvakala isikhalo ezintlangeni.

<span id="an_51:1">51:1</span> Utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabonani,
ndixhoxhela iBhabheli, nabahleli ngaphakathi kwabasukela phezulu kum,
umoya womonakalisi.

<span id="an_51:2">51:2</span> Ndiya kuthumela eBhabheli abasemzini,
abaya kuyela; balithi qongqololo ilizwe layo; ngokuba boyifikela ngeenxa
zonke ngemini yobubi.

<span id="an_51:3">51:3</span> Umtyedi wesaphetha makagobele kogobayo,
nakozinyusayo, enengubo yentsimbi, ningawayeki amadodana ayo; singelani
phantsi wonke umkhosi wayo;

<span id="an_51:4">51:4</span> bawe ababuleweyo ezweni lamaKaledi,
nabahlatywe amahlanza ezitratweni zayo.

<span id="an_51:5">51:5</span> Ngokuba uSirayeli, kwanoYuda,
akashiywanga wangumhlolokazi nguThixo wakhe, nguYehova wemikhosi; kuba
ilizwe labo lizele lityala koyiNgcwele kaSirayeli.

<span id="an_51:6">51:6</span> Sabani niphume eBhabheli, nisize elowo
umphefumlo wakhe; maningadaki ngenxa yobugwenxa bayo; ngokuba eli
lixesha lempindezelo kuYehova; uya kubuyekeza kuyo kwaimpatho yayo.

<span id="an_51:7">51:7</span> IBhabheli ibe iyindebe yegolide esandleni
sikaYehova, ilinxilisa lonke ihlabathi; zasela iintlanga ewayinini yayo.
Ngako oko ziyageza iintlanga.

<span id="an_51:8">51:8</span> Iwile iBhabheli ngesiquphe, yaphuka;
bhombolozani ngenxa yayo; intlungu yayo yithabatheleni amafutha
aqholiweyo, mhlawumbi ingapholiswa.

<span id="an_51:9">51:9</span> Bathi, Siba ngayinyanga iBhabheli,
ayiphili; yishiyeni, sihambe siye elowo ezweni lakowabo; ngokuba ityala
layo lifike emazulwini, liphakamele esibhakabhakeni.

<span id="an_51:10">51:10</span> UYehova ubuvelisile ubulungisa bethu;
yizani sibalise eZiyon isenzo sikaYehova uThixo wethu.

<span id="an_51:11">51:11</span> Khazimlisani iintolo, qubulani
amakhaka; uYehova uxhoxhe umoya wokumkani bamaKaledi. Ngokuba
umnkqangiyelo wakhe ukwiBhabheli, ukuba ayonakalise: ngokuba
yimpindezelo kaYehova, yimpindezelo yetempile yakhe.

<span id="an_51:12">51:12</span> Ziphakamiseleni ibhanile iindonga
zaseBhabheli. Qinisani ukulinda, misani abalindi, lungisani imilalela;
ngokuba njengoko uYehova wankqangiyelayo, ukwenzile awakuthethayo
ngabemi baseBhabheli.

<span id="an_51:13">51:13</span> Wena uhleliyo phezu kwamanzi amaninzi,
ubuncwane bakho buninzi; kufikile ukuphela kwakho, isilinganiselo
senzuzo yakho embi.

<span id="an_51:14">51:14</span> UYehova wemikhosi ufunge umphefumlo
wakhe, esithi, Noko ndikuzalisileyo ngabantu, banga ziinkumbi
ezinqunquthayo, kuya kususelwa ngawe ukwenziwa amayeyeye.

<span id="an_51:15">51:15</span> Ngulowenza ihlabathi ngamandla akhe,
ngulozinzisa elimiweyo ngobulumko bakhe, waneka izulu ngengqondo yakhe.

<span id="an_51:16">51:16</span> Kwakubon’ ukuba kukho isithonga
sokwenza kwakhe ingxolo yamanzi ezulwini, unyusa amafu esiphelweni
sehlabathi; imvula uyenzela imibane, arhole umoya koovimba bakhe.

<span id="an_51:17">51:17</span> Uba sisityhakala wonke umntu
engenakwazi, udaniswa wonke umnyibilikisi wegolide, ngenxa yomfanekiso
oqingqiweyo; ngokuba umfanekiso wakhe otyhidiweyo bubuxoki, awunamoya.

<span id="an_51:18">51:18</span> Zingamampunge ezo zinto, sisenzo
sokugxekwa; ngexesha lokuvelelwa kwazo ziya kutshabalala.

<span id="an_51:19">51:19</span> Akanjalo yena uSahlulelo sikaYakobi;
ngokuba nguMbumbi wezinto zonke yena, nowesizwe selifa lakhe yena;
nguYehova wemikhosi, igama lakhe.

<span id="an_51:20">51:20</span> Wena usisixengxe sam, usisikrweqe sam
sokulwa. Ndiya kuzihlekeza ngawe iintlanga, ndizonakalise ngawe
izikumkani;

<span id="an_51:21">51:21</span> ndihlekeze ngawe ihashe nomkhweli walo;
ndihlekeze inqwelo yokulwa nomkhweli wayo;

<span id="an_51:22">51:22</span> ndihlekeze ngawe indoda nomfazi,
ndihlekeze ngawe indoda enkulu nomfana, ndihlekeze ngawe amadodana
nomthinjana;

<span id="an_51:23">51:23</span> ndihlekeze ngawe umalusi nomhlambi
wakhe; ndihlekeze ngawe umlimi nesipani sakhe; ndihlekeze ngawe amabamba
neerhuluneli.

<span id="an_51:24">51:24</span> Ndobuyekekeza kwiBhabheli, nakubeni
bonke belamaKaledi, bonke ububi babo, ababenze kwiZiyon emehlweni enu;
utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_51:25">51:25</span> Yabona, ndikuchasile, ntaba
yokonakalisa, utsho uYehova, elonakalisileyo lonke ihlabathi; ndiya
kolula isandla sam phezu kwakho, ndikuqengqe uhle ezingxondorheni,
ndikwenze intaba etshisiweyo;

<span id="an_51:26">51:26</span> kungathatyathwa litye lambombo kuwe,
nalitye laziseko; ke uya kwenziwa kube senkangala ngonaphakade; utsho
uYehova.

<span id="an_51:27">51:27</span> Phakamisani ibhanile elizweni,
vuthelani isigodlo ezintlangeni; zingcwaliseni iintlanga kuyo,
zihlabeleni umkhosi, zize kuyo izikumkani zeArarati neMini neAshkenazi;
yalelani kuyo abathetheli; nyusani amahashe, eze njengeenkumbi
ezinqunquthayo, ezibetha ube namanwele.

<span id="an_51:28">51:28</span> Zingcwaliseni iintlanga kuyo, ookumkani
bamaMedi, namabamba awo, neerhuluneli zawo zonke, nelizwe lonke lolawulo
lwawo.

<span id="an_51:29">51:29</span> Ihlabathi liyanyikima,
liyazibhijabhija; ngokuba zenzeka kwiBhabheli iingcinga zikaYehova,
zokulenza ilizwe leBhabheli kube senkangala, lingamiwa.

<span id="an_51:30">51:30</span> Amagorha aseBhabheli ayekile ukulwa,
ahleli ezimboniselweni; ubugorha bawo buthe qoko, asuka aba ngabafazi.
Iminquba yayo ifakwe isikhuni, yaphukile imivalo yayo.

<span id="an_51:31">51:31</span> Isigidimi siyagidima, siqubisana
nesigidimi; umbiki uqubisana nombiki, abike kukumkani waseBhabheli ukuba
umzi wakhe uthinjwe kwaphela.

<span id="an_51:32">51:32</span> Amazibuko avingciwe, amadike atshe
ngumlilo, amadoda okulwa akhwankqisiwe.

<span id="an_51:33">51:33</span> Ngokuba utsho uYehova wemikhosi, uThixo
kaSirayeli, ukuthi, Intombi eyiBhabheli injengesanda ngexesha
lokugangathwa kwaso; kusaya kuba ngumzuzwana, lifike ixesha lokuvuna
kuyo.

<span id="an_51:34">51:34</span> Wasibhubhisa thina, wasincinitha
uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, wasibeka saba sisitya esize;
wasiginya njengengwenya, wahluthisa isisu sakhe ngokudla kwethu
okumnandi, wasigxotha.

<span id="an_51:35">51:35</span> Ukugonyamelwa kwam nenyama yam makube
phezu kweBhabheli, makatsho ummi waseZiyon; igazi lam malibe phezu
kwabemi belamaKaledi, mayitsho iYerusalem.

<span id="an_51:36">51:36</span> Ngako oko utsho uYehova ukuthi, Yabona,
ndiyalithetha ityala lakho, ndiphindezele impindezelo yakho, ndilutshise
ulwandle lwayo, ndilomise ithende layo;

<span id="an_51:37">51:37</span> iBhabheli iya kuba ngumwewe, isikhundla
seempungutye, ummangaliso nomsondlo, ingabi nammi.

<span id="an_51:38">51:38</span> Bonke bephela bangabharhula
njengeengonyama ezintsha, bangavungama njengamathole engonyamakazi.

<span id="an_51:39">51:39</span> Kanti ke ebushushwini babo ndiya
kubenzela umgidi wabo, ndibanxilise, ukuze badlamke, balale ubuthongo
obungunaphakade, bangavuki; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_51:40">51:40</span> Ndiya kubathobela ekuxhelweni
njengamatakane, njengeenkunzi zeegusha nezeebhokhwe.

<span id="an_51:41">51:41</span> Hayi, ukuthinjwa kweSheshaki, ukubanjwa
kweqhayiya lehlabathi lonke! Hayi, ukwenziwa ummangaliso kweBhabheli
phakathi kweentlanga!

<span id="an_51:42">51:42</span> Ulwandle lunyukile, lwayizela
iBhabheli; igutyungelwe kukuguguma kwamaza alo.

<span id="an_51:43">51:43</span> Imizi yayo yaba ngamanxuwa, yaba
lilizwe lomqwebedu nenkqantosi, lilizwe elingamiwe mntu, ekungadluli
nyana womntu kulo.

<span id="an_51:44">51:44</span> Ndiya kumvelela uBhele eBhabheli,
ndikurhole emlonyeni wakhe akuginyileyo; zingabi sasinga kuye iintlanga;
nodonga lweBhabheli luya kuwa.

<span id="an_51:45">51:45</span> Phumani phakathi kwayo, bantu bam;
sizani elowo umphefumlo wakhe, ngenxa yokuvutha komsindo kaYehova;

<span id="an_51:46">51:46</span> hleze ithambe intliziyo yenu, noyike
iindaba ezivakalayo ezweni. Ziya kuza nomnyaka iindaba ezo, emveni koko
ngomnye umnyaka kuze iindaba ezo, kuze ugonyamelo ezweni, umlawuli
ebambene nomlawuli.

<span id="an_51:47">51:47</span> Ngako oko, uyabona, kuza imihla endiya
kuyivelela imifanekiso eqingqiweyo yaseBhabheli, libharhe ilizwe layo
lonke, bawe phakathi kwayo ababuleweyo kuyo.

<span id="an_51:48">51:48</span> Liya kumemelela ngenxa yeBhabheli izulu
nomhlaba, nento yonke ekhona; ngokuba ababhuqi baphume entla, beza kuyo;
utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_51:49">51:49</span> Njengokuba iBhabheli yaphikela ukuwisa
ababuleweyo bakwaSirayeli, ngokunjalo baya kuwa ngenxa yeBhabheli
ababuleweyo behlabathi lonke.

<span id="an_51:50">51:50</span> Nina nisindileyo ekreleni, bambani,
musani ukuma. Mkhumbuleni uYehova nisekude, ithi qatha ezintliziyweni
zenu iYerusalem.

<span id="an_51:51">51:51</span> Sidanile, ngokuba sive isingcikivo;
ihlazo lagubungela ubuso bethu; ngokuba abasemzini bazingene iingcwele
zendlu kaYehova.

<span id="an_51:52">51:52</span> Ngako oko, yabonani, kuza imihla, utsho
uYehova, endiya kuyivelela imifanekiso eqingqiweyo elizweni layo,
bancwine abahlatyiweyo.

<span id="an_51:53">51:53</span> Nokuba iBhabheli ithe yenyuka yaya
ezulwini, nokuba ithe yayinqabisa indawo ephezulu, inqaba yayo, ababhuqi
bayo baya kuphuma kum; utsho uYehova.

<span id="an_51:54">51:54</span> Phulaphulani! Nako ukukhala kuphuma
eBhabheli, nomaphulo omkhulu uphuma ezweni lamaKaledi.

<span id="an_51:55">51:55</span> Ngokuba uYehova uyayibhuqa iBhabheli,
alitshabalalise kuyo izwi elikhulu; aguguma amaza ayo njengamanzi
amaninzi, kuvakala ingxolo yesandi sawo.

<span id="an_51:56">51:56</span> Ngokuba umbhuqi uya kuyifikela
iBhabheli, athinjwe amagorha ayo, ziqhawuke izaphetha zayo; ngokuba
nguThixo wembuyekezo uYehova, uya kuvuza evuzile.

<span id="an_51:57">51:57</span> Ndiyabanxilisa abathetheli bayo
nezilumko zayo, amabamba ayo neerhuluneli zayo, namagorha ayo; aya
kulala ubuthongo obungunaphakade, angavuki: utsho uKumkani, ogama lakhe
linguYehova wemikhosi.

<span id="an_51:58">51:58</span> Utsho uYehova wemikhosi ukuthi,
Iindonga ezibanzi zeBhabheli ziya kunqikwa kube kanye, amasango ayo
aphakamileyo atshiswe ngomlilo; izizwe zizixhamlele okulambathayo,
neentlanga zizixhamlele umlilo, zityhafe ke.

<span id="an_51:59">51:59</span> Ilizwi awathi uYeremiya umprofeti
wamwisela umthetho ngalo uSeraya, unyana kaNeriya, unyana kaMaseya,
ekuyeni kwakhe noZedekiya ukumkani wakwaYuda eBhabheli, ngomnyaka wesine
wobukumkani bakhe; uSeraya lo engumtshayeleli.

<span id="an_51:60">51:60</span> UYeremiya wabubhala encwadini bonke
ububi obuya kuyifikela iBhabheli, onke la mazwi abhaliweyo ngeBhabheli.

<span id="an_51:61">51:61</span> Wathi ke uYeremiya kuSeraya, Wakufika
eBhabheli, khangela onke lamazwi, uwalese.

<span id="an_51:62">51:62</span> Uze uthi, Yehova, wena uthethile ngale
ndawo ukuyinqumla, ingamiwa, kuthabathele kumntu kuse nakwinkomo; ke
yona iya kuba ngamanxuwa angunaphakade.

<span id="an_51:63">51:63</span> Kothi, wakugqiba ukuyilesa le ncwadi,
ubophe ilitye kuyo, uyinzulumbele esazulwini somEfrati;

<span id="an_51:64">51:64</span> uthi, Iya kwenjenje iBhabheli ukuthi
xumbu kwayo, ingaphumi, ngenxa yobubi endiya kuyizisela bona, batyhafe.
Aze ema apha amazwi kaYeremiya.

<span id="an_52:1">52:1</span> UZedekiya ubeminyaka imashumi mabini
anamnye ezelwe, ukuba ngukumkani kwakhe; waba neminyaka elishumi
elinamnye engukumkani eYerusalem; igama lonina belinguHamutali, intombi
kaYeremiya waseLibhena.

<span id="an_52:2">52:2</span> Wenza okubi emehlweni kaYehova, njengako
konke awakwenzayo uYehoyakim.

<span id="an_52:3">52:3</span> Ngokuba ngenxa yomsindo kaYehova kwenzeka
oko eYerusalem nakwaYuda, wada wabalahla ebusweni bakhe. UZedekiya
wamana egwilika kukumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_52:4">52:4</span> Kwathi ngomnyaka wesithoba wobukumkani
bakhe, ngenyanga yeshumi, ngosuku lweshumi enyangeni leyo, wayifikela
iYerusalem uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli, yena nempi yakhe
yonke, wayirhawula, wayakhela inqaba yokubonisela ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_52:5">52:5</span> Wangqingwa ke umzi, kwada kwaba ngumnyaka
weshumi elinamnye wokumkani uZedekiya.

<span id="an_52:6">52:6</span> Ngosuku lwesithoba lwenyanga yesine,
yaqina indlala phakathi komzi, ababa nasonka abantu belizwe.

<span id="an_52:7">52:7</span> Wagqojozwa umzi; asaba onke amadoda
okulwa, aphuma phakathi komzi ebusuku ngendlela yesango eliphakathi
kweendonga zombini, elisemyezweni wokumkani (aye ke amaKaledi
ewujikelezile umzi); abamba ngendlela yaseArabha.

<span id="an_52:8">52:8</span> Impi yamaKaledi yamsukela ukumkani,
yamfumana uZedekiya ezinkqantosini zaseYeriko; yonke impi yakhe
yamphalala, yemka kuye.

<span id="an_52:9">52:9</span> Ambamba ukumkani, anyuka naye, amsa
kukumkani waseBhabheli eRibhela ezweni leHamati; wawathetha apho
amatyala akhe.

<span id="an_52:10">52:10</span> Ukumkani waseBhabheli wabasikela
oonyana bakaZedekiya emehlweni akhe; nabathetheli bonke bakwaYuda
wabasikela eRibhela.

<span id="an_52:11">52:11</span> Wamtyhaphaza amehlo uZedekiya,
wamkhonkxa ngamakhamandela obhedu; ukumkani waseBhabheli wamsa
eBhabheli, wamfaka entolongweni kwada kwayimini yokufa kwakhe.

<span id="an_52:12">52:12</span> Ngenyanga yesihlanu, ngosuku lweshumi
enyangeni leyo (lo mnyaka ke ngoweshumi elineminyaka esithoba kakumkani
uNebhukadenetsare ukumkani waseBhabheli), wangena eYerusalem
uNebhuzaradan, umthetheli wabasiki, owema phambi kokumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_52:13">52:13</span> Wayitshisa indlu kaYehova, nendlu
yokumkani, nezindlu zonke zaseYerusalem; izindlu zonke zezikhulu
wazitshisa ngomlilo.

<span id="an_52:14">52:14</span> Iindonga zonke zaseYerusalem ngeenxa
zonke yazidiliza yonke impi yamaKaledi, ebinomthetheli wabasiki.

<span id="an_52:15">52:15</span> Kwizisweli zabantu, namasalela abantu
ababesele phakathi komzi, namaphamba awaphambelayo kukumkani
waseBhabheli, namasalela engxokolo, wawafudusa uNebhuzaradan, umthetheli
wabasiki.

<span id="an_52:16">52:16</span> Ke uNebhuzaradan, umthetheli wabasiki,
wasalisa kwizisweli zelizwe, ukuze zibe ngabasebenzi bemidiliya
nabalimi.

<span id="an_52:17">52:17</span> Iintsika zobhedu ezibe zisendlwini
kaYehova, neenqwelwana, nolwandle lobhedu obelusendlwini kaYehova, ezo
zinto aziqhekeza amaKaledi, aluthwalela eBhabheli lonke ubhedu lwazo.

<span id="an_52:18">52:18</span> Athabatha neembiza, nemihlakulwana,
nezitshetshe, nezitya zokutshiza, neenkamba, neempahla zonke zobhedu
ebekulungiselelwa ngazo.

<span id="an_52:19">52:19</span> Umthetheli wabasiki wathabatha
izidendeleko, neengcedevu, nezitya zokutshisa, neembiza, neziphatho
zezibane, neenkamba, namathunga, igolide kwezegolide, isilivere
kwezesilivere.

<span id="an_52:20">52:20</span> Neentsika zombini, ulwandle olunye,
neenkomo ezilishumi elinambini zobhedu ezibe ziphantsi kwalo,
neenqwelwana awazenzela indlu kaYehova uSolomon ukumkani, alwaba
nakulinganiswa ubhedu lwezo mpahla zonke.

<span id="an_52:21">52:21</span> Neentsika ezo, ukuphakama kwenye
intsika kube kuziikubhite ezilishumi elinesibhozo; umtya oziikubhite
ezilishumi elinambini ubuyithandela, nezinyuko zayo beziyiminwe emine;
ibiholoholo.

<span id="an_52:22">52:22</span> Ingqukuva yayo ibiyeyobhedu, ukuphakama
kwengqukuva bekuziikubhite ezintlanu; umnatha neerharnate
bezisengqukuveni ngeenxa zonke; yonke loo nto yabe ilubhedu. Intsika
yesibini yabe ikwanjalo, kunye neerharnate.

<span id="an_52:23">52:23</span> Iirharnate bezingamashumi asithoba
anantandathu, zibheke emoyeni; iirharnate zonke bezilikhulu phezu
komnatha ngeenxa zonke.

<span id="an_52:24">52:24</span> Umthetheli wabasiki wamthabatha uSeraya
umbingeleli oyintloko, noZefaniya umbingeleli weyesibini intlantlu,
nabagcini-mnyango bobathathu.

<span id="an_52:25">52:25</span> Kuwo umzi wathabatha umbusi wamnye,
owayengumveleli wamadoda okulwa, namadoda asixhenxe kuwo abebona ubuso
bokumkani, awafunyanwa phakathi komzi; nombhali womthetheli womkhosi,
obehlaba umkhosi kubantu belizwe, namadoda amashumi mathandathu kubantu
belizwe, awafunyanwayo phakathi komzi.

<span id="an_52:26">52:26</span> Wabathabatha abo uNebhuzaradan,
umthetheli wabasiki, wabasa eRibhela, kukumkani waseBhabheli.

<span id="an_52:27">52:27</span> Wabaxabela ukumkani waseBhabheli,
wababulala eRibhela ezweni laseHamati. Afuduswa ke amaYuda emhlabeni
wawo.

<span id="an_52:28">52:28</span> Ngabo aba abantu awabafudusayo
uNebhukadenetsare: ngomnyaka wesixhenxe, amaYuda angamawaka amathathu,
anamanci mabini anamathathu;

<span id="an_52:29">52:29</span> ngomnyaka weshumi elinesibhozo
kaNebhukadenetsare kwafuduswa eYerusalem imiphefumlo yaba makhulu
asibhozo, anamanci mathathu anamibini;

<span id="an_52:30">52:30</span> ngomnyaka wamashumi amabini anamithathu
kaNebhukadenetsare, uNebhuzaradan, umthetheli wabasiki, wafudusa amaYuda
ayimiphefumlo emakhulu asixhenxe, anamanci mane anamihlanu. Yonke
imiphefumlo yaba ngamawaka amane anamakhulu amathandathu.

<span id="an_52:31">52:31</span> Kwathi ngomnyaka wamashumi omathathu
anesixhenxe wokufuduswa kukaYehoyakim ukumkani wakwaYuda, ngenyanga
yeshumi elinesibini, ngosuku lwamashumi omabini anesihlanu enyangeni
leyo, uEvili-merodaki ukumkani waseBhabheli, ngomnyaka wokwenziwa kwakhe
ukumkani, wayiphakamisa intloko kaYehoyakim ukumkani wakwaYuda,
wamkhupha entolongweni.

<span id="an_52:32">52:32</span> Wathetha naye kakuhle, wayimisa itrone
yakhe, yaba ngaphezu kweetrone zabanye ookumkani ababenaye eBhabheli.

<span id="an_52:33">52:33</span> Wazikhulula iingubo zakhe zobubanjwa;
wamana ukudla isonka ebusweni bakhe yonke imihla yokuphila kwakhe.

<span id="an_52:34">52:34</span> Umxhesho wakhe, umxhesho wamaxesha
onke, wawunikwa, uvela kukumkani waseBhabheli, into yemini ngangemini
yayo, kwada kwayimini yokufa kwakhe, yonke imihla yokuphila kwakhe.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
